CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.C_SP_IFRS_STAGE_BENCANA (
	p_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE
)
AS
    v_STAGE_DETAIL     VARCHAR2(100);
    v_STR_SQL        VARCHAR2(4000);
    v_CURRDATE       DATE;
    v_TABLENAME      VARCHAR2(100);
BEGIN
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    -- INIT
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    IF p_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO v_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        v_CURRDATE := p_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    v_TABLENAME := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY';
  
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    -- RESET STAGE (DYNAMIC UPDATE)
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    v_STR_SQL :=
        'MERGE INTO ' || v_TABLENAME || ' A
			USING (
				SELECT I.MASTERID ,I.ACCOUNT_NUMBER, I.STAGE  FROM ' || v_TABLENAME || ' I 
				INNER JOIN (SELECT X.NOLOAN, MAX(NO_BUCKET) AS NO_BUCKET 
									FROM LIST_NASABAH_RESTRU_BENCANA X GROUP BY NOLOAN) J 
				ON I.ACCOUNT_NUMBER = J.NOLOAN 
				WHERE I.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(v_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' AND NVL(I.STAGE,0) < 2
			)B
			ON(A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(v_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || '''
				AND A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID)
			WHEN MATCHED THEN 
			UPDATE SET A.STAGE = 2,
					A.SICR_FLAG = 1';

    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_STR_SQL;
    COMMIT;

EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN C_SP_IFRS_STAGE_BENCANA: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.NITIP_ADAM
IS
BEGIN
	
	
INSERT INTO IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
(
	 DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,MASTERID
	,MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE
	,DATA_SOURCE
	,PRODUCT_TYPE 
	,PRODUCT_CODE 
	,BRANCH_CODE 
	,ACCOUNT_STATUS 
	,ACCOUNT_STATUS_ORI
	,ACCOUNT_NUMBER 
	,CUSTOMER_NUMBER 
	,CUSTOMER_NAME 
	,CURRENCY 
	,EXCHANGE_RATE 
	,OUTSTANDING 
	,PLAFOND 
	,MARGIN_RATE 
	,EIR 
	,FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT 
	,DAY_PAST_DUE 
	,DPD_CIF 
	,BI_COLLECTABILITY 
	,BI_COLLECT_CIF 
	,STAFF_LOAN_FLAG 
	,COLL_AMOUNT 
	,UNAMORT_FEE_AMT 
	,UNAMORT_COST_AMT 
	,MARGIN_TYPE 
	,DEFAULT_DATE 
	,LOAN_START_DATE 
	,LOAN_DUE_DATE  
	,DIVISION_CODE 
)
SELECT 
	 PMAM.DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,IMI.MASTERID
	,PMAM.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID
	,PMAM.DATA_SOURCE
	,PMAM.PRODUCT_TYPE 
	,PMAM.PRODUCT_CODE 
	,PMAM.BRANCH_CODE 
	,CASE WHEN NVL(PMAM.ACCOUNT_STATUS,'A') = 'E' THEN 'W' ELSE 'A' END ACCOUNT_STATUS  
	,PMAM.ACCOUNT_STATUS AS ACCOUNT_STATUS_ORI
	,PMAM.ACCOUNT_NUMBER 
	,PMAM.CUSTOMER_NUMBER 
	,PMAM.CUSTOMER_NAME 
	,PMAM.CURRENCY 
	,PMAM.EXCHANGE_RATE 
	,PMAM.OUTSTANDING 
	,PMAM.PLAFOND 
	,PMAM.INTEREST_RATE 
	,PMAM.EIR 
	,PMAM.FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT 
	,PMAM.DAY_PAST_DUE 
	,PMAM.DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF  
	,PMAM.BI_COLLECTABILITY 
	,PMAM.BI_COLLECTABILITY  
	,CASE WHEN NVL(PMAM.STAFF_LOAN_FLAG ,'N') = 'N' THEN 0 ELSE 1 END AS STAFF_LOAN_FLAG 
	,PMAM.COLLATERAL_VALUE_FOR_IMPAIR 
	,PMAM.UNAMOR_ORIGINATION_FEE_AMT 
	,PMAM.UNAMOR_TRANS_COST_AMT  
	,PMAM.AMORT_TYPE  
	,pmam.DEFAULT_DATE 
	,pmam.LOAN_START_DATE 
	,pmam.LOAN_END_DATE 
	,pmam.DIVISION_CODE 
FROM PSAK_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY pmam 
JOIN
IFRS_MASTER_ID IMI
ON
PMAM.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID = IMI.MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE; 



INSERT INTO IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY_EXT 
(
	 DOWNLOAD_DATE 
	,MASTERID 
)
SELECT 
	 DOWNLOAD_DATE 
	,MASTERID 
FROM PSAK_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY pmam 
JOIN
IFRS_MASTER_ID IMI
ON
PMAM.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID = IMI.MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE; 


INSERT INTO IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
(
	 DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,MASTERID
	,MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE
	,DATA_SOURCE
	,PRODUCT_TYPE 
	,PRODUCT_CODE 
	,BRANCH_CODE 
	,ACCOUNT_STATUS 
	,ACCOUNT_NUMBER 
	,CUSTOMER_NUMBER 
	,CUSTOMER_NAME 
	,CURRENCY 
	,EXCHANGE_RATE 
	,OUTSTANDING 
	,PLAFOND 
	,MARGIN_RATE 
	,EIR 
	,FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT 
	,DAY_PAST_DUE 
	,DPD_CIF 
	,BI_COLLECTABILITY 
	,BI_COLLECT_CIF 
	,STAFF_LOAN_FLAG 
	,COLL_AMOUNT 
	,UNAMORT_FEE_AMT 
	,UNAMORT_COST_AMT 
	,MARGIN_TYPE 
	,DEFAULT_DATE 
	,LOAN_START_DATE 
	,LOAN_DUE_DATE 
	,DIVISION_CODE 
	,RESTRUCTURE_FLAG 
	,OUTSTANDING_PAST_DUE 
	,MARGIN_PAST_DUE 
)
SELECT 
	 pmam.FICMISDATE AS DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,IMI.MASTERID
	,'HC_'|| pmam.NOMORREKENING AS MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE
	,'HC' AS DATA_SOURCE
	,'QARDH' AS PRODUCT_TYPE 
	,pmam.LOANTYPECODE AS PRODUCT_CODE 
	,pmam.KODECABANG AS BRANCH_CODE 
	,'A' AS ACCOUNT_STATUS 
	,pmam.NOMORREKENING  AS ACCOUNT_NUMBER 
	,pmam.NOMORNASABAH AS CUSTOMER_NUMBER 
	,pmam.NAMANASABAH  AS CUSTOMER_NAME 
	,pmam.JENISVALUTA AS CURRENCY 
	,1 AS EXCHANGE_RATE 
	,pmam.JUMLAHBULANLAPORAN  AS OUTSTANDING 
	,NULL AS PLAFOND 
	,NULL AS MARGIN_RATE 
	,NULL AS EIR 
	,NULL AS FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT 
	,pmam.TUNGGAKANHARI AS DAY_PAST_DUE 
	,NULL AS DPD_CIF 
	,pmam.KUALITAS AS BI_COLLECTABILITY 
	,pmam.KUALITAS AS BI_COLLECT_CIF 
	,NULL AS STAFF_LOAN_FLAG 
	,NULL AS COLL_AMOUNT 
	,NULL AS UNAMORT_FEE_AMT 
	,NULL AS UNAMORT_COST_AMT 
	,NULL AS MARGIN_TYPE 
	,NULL AS DEFAULT_DATE 
	,pmam.JANGKAWAKTUMULAI AS LOAN_START_DATE 
	,pmam.JANGKAWAKTUJATUHTEMPO AS LOAN_DUE_DATE 
	,pmam.DIVISIPISAH AS DIVISION_CODE 
	,CASE WHEN pmam.SIFATPIUTANG IN ('1', '5') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END RESTRUCTURE_FLAG
	,pmam.TUNGGAKANPOKOK AS OUTSTANDING_PAST_DUE
	,pmam.TUNGGAKANMARGIN AS MARGIN_PAST_DUE
FROM 
FORM12_SANDIRINCIANPIUTANGQARDH_RPT_TMP pmam 
JOIN
IFRS_MASTER_ID IMI
ON
'HC_'||TRIM(pmam.NOMORREKENING) = IMI.MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE;

INSERT INTO IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY_EXT 
(
	 DOWNLOAD_DATE 
	,MASTERID 
)
SELECT 
	 pmam.FICMISDATE AS DOWNLOAD_DATE 
	,IMI.MASTERID 
FROM FORM12_SANDIRINCIANPIUTANGQARDH_RPT_TMP pmam 
JOIN
IFRS_MASTER_ID IMI
ON
'HC_'||TRIM(PMAM.NOMORREKENING) = IMI.MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE; 


--SELECT * FROM KREDITPEMBIAYAAN_HC

	  FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A 
	  WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE  = V_START_dATE

/*
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * 
DECLARE
  v_start_date DATE := DATE '2020-01-31';  
  v_end_date   DATE := DATE '2025-12-31';  
 
BEGIN 

  WHILE v_start_date <= v_end_date LOOP
	  
	
UPDATE IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY  a
SET (a.sub_segment, a.segment, a.group_segment) =
    (SELECT x.sub_segment, x.segment, x.group_segment
     FROM TMP_IMA_SEGMENT x
     WHERE a.masterid = x.masterid
     AND a.sub_segment <> x.sub_segment)
WHERE a.download_date = v_start_date;

COMMIT ; 
    -- tambah 1 bulan
DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('Tanggal: ' || TO_CHAR(v_start_date, 'YYYY-MM-DD'));
    v_start_date := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(v_start_date, 1));
  END LOOP;
END;
 
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * 
 * 
DECLARE
  v_start_date DATE := DATE '2020-01-31';  
  v_end_date   DATE := DATE '2025-12-31';  
 
BEGIN 

  WHILE v_start_date <= v_end_date LOOP
	  
	INSERT INTO IMATES   
	 
		SELECT download_Date,  MASTERID, ACCOUNT_STATUS_ORI, DAY_PAST_DUE   FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A
		WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE  = LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(v_start_date, 1)) 
		AND ACCOUNT_STATUS_ORI <> 'E'
		AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY X 
		WHERE X.DOWNLOAD_DATE = V_START_dATE AND A.MASTERID = X.MASTERID AND X.ACCOUNT_STATUS_ORI IS NULL
		FETCH FIRST 1 ROWS ONLY) ;
 

COMMIT ; 
    -- tambah 1 bulan
DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('Tanggal: ' || TO_CHAR(v_start_date, 'YYYY-MM-DD'));
    v_start_date := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(v_start_date, 1));
  END LOOP;
END;

 * 
 * 
DECLARE
  v_start_date DATE := DATE '2020-02-29';  
  v_end_date   DATE := DATE '2025-12-31';  
 
BEGIN 

  WHILE v_start_date <= v_end_date LOOP
	  
	  
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IMA_DPD';

INSERT INTO GTMP_IMA_DPD
SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, DAY_PAST_DUE, DAY_PAST_DUE_ORI , DPD_ZERO_COUNTER, OUTSTANDING, ACCOUNT_STATUS_ORI 
FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A 
WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE IN (V_START_dATE, LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_START_dATE,-1)))
AND ACCOUNT_STATUS =  'A'
AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM IMATES X WHERE A.MASTERID = X.MASTERID  AND LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(X.DOWNLOAD_DATE,-1))  >= A.DOWNLOAD_DATE) 	  
	  
	MERGE INTO IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A
	USING ( 
		SELECT B.download_date, A.masterid, 
			GREATEST(nvl(B.DAY_PAST_DUE_ORI,0), nvl(A.DAY_PAST_DUE,0)) DPD,
			A.DPD_ZERO_COUNTER, A.OUTSTANDING - B.OUTSTANDING  AS DELTA_OS ,
			a.ACCOUNT_STATUS_ORI  AS prev_status, b.ACCOUNT_STATUS_ORI  AS curr_Status
		FROM GTMP_IMA_DPD a
			JOIN GTMP_IMA_DPD B ON A.MASTER = B.MASTERID 
		WHERE A.DOWNLOAD_DATE  = LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_START_dATE,-1)) 
			AND B.DOWNLOAD_DATE   = V_START_DATE
			
		) b 
		ON (A.download_date = B.download_date AND A.masterid = B.masterid) 
		
		WHEN MATCHED THEN 
		
		UPDATE 
		SET  A.DPD_ZERO_COUNTER = 
			CASE WHEN B.DPD_ZERO_COUNTER = 4 AND b.prev_status = b.curr_status THEN 4
			WHEN b.prev_Status <> b.curr_Status THEN 0 
			WHEN B.DELTA_OS > 0 AND NVL(A.DAY_PAST_DUE_ORI,0) = 0 AND b.prev_status = b.curr_status THEN B.DPD_ZERO_COUNTER + 1 
			WHEN B.DELTA_OS = 0 AND NVL(A.DAY_PAST_DUE_ORI,0) = 0 AND b.prev_status = b.curr_status THEN B.DPD_ZERO_COUNTER
			ELSE 0 END,
			A.DAY_PAST_DUE = 
			CASE WHEN B.DELTA_OS > 0 AND NVL(A.DAY_PAST_DUE_ORI,0) = 0 AND B.DPD_ZERO_COUNTER + 1 >= 4 AND b.prev_status = b.curr_status THEN nvl(A.DAY_PAST_DUE_ORI,0)	 
			ELSE B.DPD 
			END
	  
	   
COMMIT ; 
    -- tambah 1 bulan
DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('Tanggal: ' || TO_CHAR(v_start_date, 'YYYY-MM-DD'));
    v_start_date := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(v_start_date, 1));
  END LOOP;
END;

 DECLARE 
dtcurr DATE;
dtprev DATE;

BEGIN
	 dtcurr := '31-JAN-2020';
	 
	WHILE  dtcurr <=  '31-DEC-2025'
	LOOP 
		dtprev := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(dtcurr, -1));
	

MERGE INTO PSAK413.IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY a USING
(
	SELECT 
		imam.DOWNLOAD_DATE,
		imam.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID, 
		imam.DAY_PAST_DUE
	FROM PSAK413.PSAK_MASTER_ACCOUNT_DPD_ORI imam
	WHERE imam.DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr
) dat 
ON 
(
	a.MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE = dat.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID
	AND
	a.DOWNLOAD_DATE = dat.DOWNLOAD_DATE
)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE 
		SET 
			DAY_PAST_DUE_ORI = dat.DAY_PAST_DUE;

dbms_output.put_line(dtcurr||'|'||dtprev);
dtcurr := last_day(ADD_MONTHS(dtcurr, 1));

COMMIT;

END LOOP;

END;

UPDATE VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
SET 
	SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_PIUTANG'
				   WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_PIUTANG'	
				   WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_PIUTANG'
				   WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHS0001') THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_PIUTANG'
			  END, 
	
	SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_PIUTANG_MURABAHAH'
				   	   WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_PIUTANG_QARDH'	
				   	   WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_RAHN'
				   	   WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHS0001') THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_RAHN'
			  	  END,
			  	  
	GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'PENSIUN_PRAPENSIUN'
				   	   	 WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'PENSIUN_PRAPENSIUN'	
				   	   	 WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS'
				   	   	 WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHS0001')	THEN 'PENSIUN_PRAPENSIUN'
			  	  END
WHERE 
	PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'PENSIUN & PRA PENSIUN'
AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtCURR;

--BACK TO BACK & MURABAHAH EMAS--
UPDATE VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
SET 
	SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS_PIUTANG'
				   WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS_PIUTANG'	
				   WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' 			THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_PIUTANG'
			  END, 
	
	SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 	THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS_MURABAHAH'
				   	   WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   	THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS_QARDH'	
				   	   WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' 		THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_RAHN'
			  	  END,
			  	  
	GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS'
				   	   	 WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS'	
				   	   	 WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' 			THEN 'GADAI_EMAS'
			  	  END
WHERE 
	PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'BACK TO BACK & MURABAHAH EMAS'
AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtCURR;

--KUR--
UPDATE VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
SET 
	SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'KUR_PIUTANG' END, 
	SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 	THEN 'KUR_MURABAHAH' END,
	GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' THEN 'KUR' END
WHERE 
	PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'KUR'
AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtCURR;


--NON KUR--
UPDATE VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
SET 
	SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'NON_KUR_PIUTANG' END, 
	SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 	THEN 'NON_KUR_MURABAHAH' END,
	GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' THEN 'NON_KUR' END
WHERE 
	PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'NON KUR'
AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtCURR;

--IMPLAN--
UPDATE VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
SET 
	SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'MULTIGUNA_PIUTANG' END, 
	SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 	THEN 'MULTIGUNA_MURABAHAH' END,
	GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' THEN 'MULTIGUNA' END
WHERE 
	PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'IMPLAN'
AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtCURR;

dbms_output.put_line(dtcurr||'|'||dtprev);
dtcurr := last_day(ADD_MONTHS(dtcurr, 1));

COMMIT;

END LOOP;

END; 

 
  
*/

/*
--QUERY CHECK TABLE CONSUME--
SELECT TABSCHEMA, TABNAME, CREATE_TIME, ALTER_TIME
FROM SYSCAT.TABLES
WHERE TABSCHEMA = 'PSAK'
ORDER BY ALTER_TIME DESC
 
SELECT SUBSTR(TABSCHEMA,1,18) AS TABSCHEMA
, SUBSTR(TABNAME,1,30) AS TABNAME
,(DATA_OBJECT_P_SIZE + INDEX_OBJECT_P_SIZE + LONG_OBJECT_P_SIZE + LOB_OBJECT_P_SIZE + XML_OBJECT_P_SIZE) AS TOTAL_SIZE_IN_KB
,(DATA_OBJECT_P_SIZE + INDEX_OBJECT_P_SIZE + LONG_OBJECT_P_SIZE + LOB_OBJECT_P_SIZE + XML_OBJECT_P_SIZE) / 1024  AS TOTAL_SIZE_IN_MB
,(DATA_OBJECT_P_SIZE + INDEX_OBJECT_P_SIZE + LONG_OBJECT_P_SIZE + LOB_OBJECT_P_SIZE + XML_OBJECT_P_SIZE) / (1024*1024) AS TOTAL_SIZE_IN_GB
FROM SYSIBMADM.ADMINTABINFO
WHERE TABSCHEMA NOT LIKE 'SYS%'
ORDER BY TOTAL_SIZE_IN_GB DESC 
  
   
    
     
       
 --QUERY CHECK TABLE SPACE--
 select a.tablespace_name as "Tablespace Name",
       round(a.bytes_alloc / 1024 / 1024) "Allocated (MB)",
       round(nvl(b.bytes_free, 0) / 1024 / 1024) "Free (MB)",
       round((a.bytes_alloc - nvl(b.bytes_free, 0)) / 1024 / 1024) "Used (MB)",
       round((nvl(b.bytes_free, 0) / a.bytes_alloc) * 100) "% Free",
       100 - round((nvl(b.bytes_free, 0) / a.bytes_alloc) * 100) "% Used"
   --    round(maxbytes/1024 / 1024) "Max. Bytes (MB)"
from  ( select  f.tablespace_name,
               sum(f.bytes) bytes_alloc,
               sum(decode(f.autoextensible, 'YES',f.maxbytes,'NO', f.bytes)) maxbytes
        from dba_data_files f
        group by tablespace_name) a,
      ( select  f.tablespace_name,
               sum(f.bytes)  bytes_free
        from dba_free_space f
        group by tablespace_name) b
where a.tablespace_name = b.tablespace_name (+)
union all
select 
       h.tablespace_name as tablespace_name,
       round(sum(h.bytes_free + h.bytes_used) / 1048576) megs_alloc,
       round(sum((h.bytes_free + h.bytes_used) - nvl(p.bytes_used, 0)) / 1048576) megs_free,
       round(sum(nvl(p.bytes_used, 0))/ 1048576) megs_used,
       round((sum((h.bytes_free + h.bytes_used) - nvl(p.bytes_used, 0)) / sum(h.bytes_used + h.bytes_free)) * 100) Pct_Free,
       100 - round((sum((h.bytes_free + h.bytes_used) - nvl(p.bytes_used, 0)) / sum(h.bytes_used + h.bytes_free)) * 100) pct_used
     --  round(sum(f.maxbytes) / 1048576) max
from   sys.v_$TEMP_SPACE_HEADER h, sys.v_$Temp_extent_pool p, dba_temp_files f
where  p.file_id(+) = h.file_id
and    p.tablespace_name(+) = h.tablespace_name
and    f.file_id = h.file_id
and    f.tablespace_name = h.tablespace_name
group by h.tablespace_name
ORDER BY 2;

select * from CKPN_PMA
select * from CKPN_PAYM_SCHD_ALL
select * from CKPN_TRX
*/

   FROM PSAK_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY pmam
   WHERE MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID IN 
   (

		MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID	
   	   FROM PSAK_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY pmam

   )
   GROUP BY MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID

--PATCH LOAN_START_DATE, LOAN_DUE_DATE--
DECLARE dtcurr DATE;
dtprev DATE;

BEGIN
	 dtcurr := '31-DEC-2025';
	 
	WHILE  dtcurr >= '31-JAN-2020' -- '31-DEC-2025'
	LOOP 
		dtprev := ADD_MONTHS(dtcurr, -1);


MERGE INTO 	PSAK_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY a USING
(
	SELECT 
		pmam.rowid rowids, 
		pmam.DOWNLOAD_DATE,
		pmam.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID, 
		pmam.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, 
		pmal.LOAN_START_DATE,
		pmal.LOAN_DUE_DATE
	FROM PSAK_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY pmam, 
		PSAK_MASTER_ACCOUNT_LOAN_DATE pmal
	WHERE pmam.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID = pmal.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID 
    --AND trim(to_char(pmam.DOWNLOAD_DATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')) = trim(REPLACE(pmal.DOWNLOAD_DATE,'00.00.00,000000000',''))
	AND pmam.DOWNLOAD_DATE = pmal.DOWNLOAD_DATE 
	AND pmam.DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr
) dat 
ON 
(
	a.rowid = dat.rowids 
	AND 
	a.DOWNLOAD_DATE = dat.DOWNLOAD_DATE 
	AND 
	a.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID = dat.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID
)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE 
		SET 
			LOAN_START_DATE = dat.LOAN_START_DATE, 
			LOAN_END_DATE = dat.LOAN_DUE_DATE;

dbms_output.put_line(dtcurr||'|'||dtprev);
dtcurr := last_day(TO_DATE(dtcurr)-1-TO_NUMBER(TO_CHAR(TO_DATE(dtcurr),'DD')));

COMMIT;

END LOOP;

END;
--PATCH LOAN_START_DATE, LOAN_DUE_DATE--

--PATCH DIVISION CODE--
DECLARE dtcurr DATE;
dtprev DATE;

BEGIN
	 dtcurr := '31-DEC-2025';
	 
	WHILE  dtcurr >= '31-JAN-2020' -- '31-DEC-2025'
	LOOP 
		dtprev := ADD_MONTHS(dtcurr, -1);


MERGE INTO 	PSAK_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY a USING
(
	SELECT 
		pmam.rowid rowids, 
		pmam.DOWNLOAD_DATE,
		pmam.account_number, 
		pmam.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, 
		lpda.noloan,
		lpda.divisi_pisah
	FROM PSAK_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY pmam, 
		 LoanPerDivisi_All lpda
	WHERE pmam.account_number = lpda.noloan 
    --AND trim(to_char(pmam.DOWNLOAD_DATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')) = trim(REPLACE(pmal.DOWNLOAD_DATE,'00.00.00,000000000',''))
	AND pmam.DOWNLOAD_DATE = lpda.ficmisdate 
	AND pmam.DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr
) dat 
ON 
(
	a.rowid = dat.rowids 
	AND 
	a.DOWNLOAD_DATE = dat.DOWNLOAD_DATE 
	AND 
	a.account_number = dat.account_number
)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE 
		SET 
			DIVISION_CODE = dat.divisi_pisah;

dbms_output.put_line(dtcurr||'|'||dtprev);
dtcurr := last_day(TO_DATE(dtcurr)-1-TO_NUMBER(TO_CHAR(TO_DATE(dtcurr),'DD')));

COMMIT;

END LOOP;

END;

 WITH cte  AS (

GROUP BY MASTERID , PRODUCT_CODE 
),
cte2 AS (
SELECT min(DOWNLOAD_DATE) DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID  
FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY a 
WHERE DIVISION_CODE IS NOT NULL 
AND EXISTS (SELECT * FROM cte x WHERE a.masterid = x.MASTERID )
GROUP BY MASTERID 
)

SELECT  A.PRODUCT_CODE,count(*)
FROM cte a 
WHERE NOT  EXISTS (SELECT * FROM cte2 x WHERE a.masterid = x.masterid )  
GROUP BY a.PRODUCT_CODE

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_CEK_PROCESS_RIKO
AS
BEGIN
	
SELECT SID ,SERIAL#,OPNAME, SOFAR ,TOTALWORK ,UNITS ,
ROUND(SOFAR/TOTALWORK*100,2) AS PERCENT 
FROM "V$SESSION_LONGOPS" WHERE TOTALWORK != 0
AND SOFAR <> TOTALWORK 

	
/*

--2345322



MERGE INTO 	PSAK413.IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY a USING
(
	SELECT 
		pmam.DOWNLOAD_DATE,
		pmam.MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE, 
		pmam.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, 
		pmal.LOAN_START_DATE,
		pmal.LOAN_DUE_DATE
	FROM PSAK413.IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY pmam, 
		PSAK.X_PMA_ARCHIVE_2025_LOAN_DATE pmal
	WHERE pmam.MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE = pmal.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID 
    --AND trim(to_char(pmam.DOWNLOAD_DATE,'dd-mm-yyyy')) = trim(REPLACE(pmal.DOWNLOAD_DATE,'00.00.00,000000000',''))
	AND pmam.DOWNLOAD_DATE = pmal.DOWNLOAD_DATE 
	AND pmam.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 FEB 2026'
) dat 
ON 
(
	a.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 FEB 2026'
	AND 
	a.MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE = dat.MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE
)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE 
		SET 
			LOAN_START_DATE = dat.LOAN_START_DATE, 
			LOAN_DUE_DATE = dat.LOAN_DUE_DATE;


-- UPDATE DIVISION_CODE
MERGE INTO ifrs_master_account_monthly A
USING (
		SELECT COUNT(*) FROM IMPORT_LOANPERDIVISI_FEB26 ihf 
	)b
ON (a.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 feb 2026' AND b.NOLOAN = a.ACCOUNT_NUMBER)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET 
	a.DIVISION_CODE  = b.DIVISI_PISAH


-- UPDATE DPD LBUT
MERGE INTO ifrs_master_account_monthly A
USING (
		SELECT * FROM IMPORT_DPD_LBUT_FEB26 ihf 
	)b
ON (a.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 feb 2026' AND b.NOMORREKENING = a.ACCOUNT_NUMBER)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET 
	a.DAY_PAST_DUE  = b.TUNGGAKAN_HARI
	
			
-- UPDATE RESTRU FLAG
UPDATE IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A 
SET A.RESTRUCTURE_FLAG = 0
WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 FEB 2026'
	
UPDATE IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A 
SET A.RESTRUCTURE_FLAG = 1
WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 FEB 2026'
 AND (A.ACCOUNT_STATUS_ORI LIKE '%R%' OR A.ACCOUNT_STATUS_ORI LIKE '%P%')


-- UPDATE GLOBAL CUSTOMER NUMBER	
MERGE INTO ifrs_master_account_monthly A
USING (
		SELECT * FROM IMPORT_SUPERCIF_ONEOBLIGOR_FEB26 ihf 
	)b
ON (a.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 feb 2026' AND b.CIF_NO = a.CUSTOMER_NUMBER)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET 
	a.GLOBAL_CUSTOMER_NUMBER  = b.SUPERCIF_NO
	

-- INESRT IMA (DONE)
-- UPDATE LOAN_START_DATE/DUE_DATE (DONE)
-- UPDATE DIVISION_CODE YG DATA_SOURCE SELAIN HC DAN DVC (DONE)
-- UPDATE DPD LBUT (DONE)
-- RESTRU_FLAG YG ACCOUNT_STATUS_ORI (DONE)
-- UPDATE GCN (DONE)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

MERGE INTO IFRS_MASTER_ID X
	USING (
		SELECT * FROM IMPORT_HC_FEB26 A
		LEFT JOIN IFRS_MASTER_ID B ON B.ACCOUNT_NUMBER = TO_CHAR(A.NOMORREKENING)
		WHERE B.ACCOUNT_NUMBER IS NULL
		) Y
	ON (X.ACCOUNT_NUMBER = TO_CHAR(Y.NOMORREKENING))
WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN 
INSERT (MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE, ACCOUNT_NUMBER,IAS_CLASS,EFFDATE,CREATED_DATE)
VALUES ('HC_'||TO_CHAR(Y.NOMORREKENING),TO_CHAR(Y.NOMORREKENING),'A',TO_DATE(FICMISDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD'),SYSDATE);
	-- 5455


MERGE INTO IFRS_MASTER_ID X
	USING (
		SELECT * FROM IMPORT_DVC_FEB26 A
		LEFT JOIN IFRS_MASTER_ID B ON B.ACCOUNT_NUMBER = TO_CHAR(A.NOMORREKENING)
		WHERE B.ACCOUNT_NUMBER IS NULL
		) Y
	ON (X.ACCOUNT_NUMBER = TO_CHAR(Y.NOMORREKENING))
WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN 
INSERT (MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE, ACCOUNT_NUMBER,IAS_CLASS,EFFDATE,CREATED_DATE)
VALUES ('DVC_'||TO_CHAR(Y.NOMORREKENING),TO_CHAR(Y.NOMORREKENING),'A',TO_DATE(FICMISDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD'),SYSDATE);

(
	 DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,MASTERID
	,MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE
	,DATA_SOURCE
	,PRODUCT_TYPE 
	,PRODUCT_CODE 
	,BRANCH_CODE 
	,ACCOUNT_STATUS 
	,ACCOUNT_NUMBER 
	,CUSTOMER_NUMBER 
	,CUSTOMER_NAME 
	,CURRENCY 
	,EXCHANGE_RATE 
	,OUTSTANDING 
	,PLAFOND 
	,MARGIN_RATE 
	,EIR 
	,FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT 
	,DAY_PAST_DUE 
	,DPD_CIF 
	,BI_COLLECTABILITY 
	,BI_COLLECT_CIF 
	,STAFF_LOAN_FLAG 
	,COLL_AMOUNT 
	,UNAMORT_FEE_AMT 
	,UNAMORT_COST_AMT 
	,MARGIN_TYPE 
	,DEFAULT_DATE 
	,LOAN_START_DATE 
	,LOAN_DUE_DATE 
	,DIVISION_CODE 
	,RESTRUCTURE_FLAG 
	,OUTSTANDING_PAST_DUE 
	,MARGIN_PAST_DUE 
)
SELECT 
	 TO_DATE(pmam.FICMISDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') AS DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,IMI.MASTERID
	,'HC_'|| pmam.NOMORREKENING AS MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE
	,'HC' AS DATA_SOURCE
	,'QARDH' AS PRODUCT_TYPE 
	,pmam.LOANTYPECODE AS PRODUCT_CODE 
	,pmam.KODECABANG AS BRANCH_CODE 
	,'A' AS ACCOUNT_STATUS 
	,TO_CHAR(pmam.NOMORREKENING) AS ACCOUNT_NUMBER 
	,TO_CHAR(pmam.NOMORNASABAH) AS CUSTOMER_NUMBER 
	,pmam.NAMANASABAH  AS CUSTOMER_NAME 
	,pmam.JENISVALUTA AS CURRENCY 
	,1 AS EXCHANGE_RATE 
	,pmam.JUMLAHBULANLAPORAN AS OUTSTANDING 
	,NULL AS PLAFOND 
	,NULL AS MARGIN_RATE 
	,NULL AS EIR 
	,NULL AS FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT 
	,pmam.TUNGGAKANHARI AS DAY_PAST_DUE 
	,NULL AS DPD_CIF 
	,pmam.KUALITAS AS BI_COLLECTABILITY 
	,pmam.KUALITAS AS BI_COLLECT_CIF 
	,NULL AS STAFF_LOAN_FLAG 
	,NULL AS COLL_AMOUNT 
	,NULL AS UNAMORT_FEE_AMT 
	,NULL AS UNAMORT_COST_AMT 
	,NULL AS MARGIN_TYPE 
	,NULL AS DEFAULT_DATE 
	,TO_DATE(pmam.JANGKAWAKTUMULAI, 'YYYY-MM-DD') AS LOAN_START_DATE 
	,TO_DATE(pmam.JANGKAWAKTUJATUHTEMPO, 'YYYY-MM-DD') AS LOAN_DUE_DATE 
	,pmam.DIVISIPISAH AS DIVISION_CODE 
	,CASE WHEN pmam.SIFATPIUTANG IN ('1', '5') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END RESTRUCTURE_FLAG
	,pmam.TUNGGAKANPOKOK AS OUTSTANDING_PAST_DUE
	,pmam.TUNGGAKANMARGIN AS MARGIN_PAST_DUE
FROM 
IMPORT_HC_FEB26 pmam 
JOIN
IFRS_MASTER_ID IMI
ON
TRIM(pmam.NOMORREKENING) = IMI.ACCOUNT_NUMBER;

	,UNAMORT_FEE_AMT 
	,UNAMORT_COST_AMT 
	,MARGIN_TYPE

	,NULL AS COLL_AMOUNT

-- INSER PAYM_SCHEDULE
INSERT INTO PSAK413.IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_ALL(DOWNLOAD_DATE,MASTERID,PMTDATE,PRINCIPAL,MARGIN,COUNTER,SOURCE_PROCESS)
SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE ,
B.MASTERID ,
TO_DATE(A.PMTDATE,'YYYYMMDD')  AS N_PMTDATE,
TO_NUMBER(PRINCIPAL) AS N_PRINCIPAL,
TO_NUMBER(A.INTEREST) AS N_INTEREST,
rank() over (partition by A.ACC_MSTR_ID order by TO_DATE(A.PMTDATE, 'YYYYMMDD') ) - 1 counter,
'PSAK_PAYM_SCHD_DWH' AS SOURCE_PROCESS 
FROM psak.PSAK_PAYM_SCHD_DWH_STG_NEW A
LEFT JOIN PSAK413.IFRS_MASTER_ID B ON A.ACC_MSTR_ID = B.ACCOUNT_NUMBER 
WHERE A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 FEB 2026'

(
	 DOWNLOAD_DATE 
	,MASTERID 
)

	 DOWNLOAD_DATE 
	,MASTERID 
FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY  
WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = '31 JAN 2026'

--- STEP PATCHING SEGMENT ---
CALL PSAK413.SP_IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING();

CALL PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EIL_UPDATE_PORTFOLIO('S_00000_0000', '28 FEB 2026', 'M');

MERGE INTO IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY X
USING (
		SELECT B.DOWNLOAD_DATE , A.MASTERID, A.GROUP_SEGMENT ,B.GROUP_SEGMENT AS GS_RULES, A.SEGMENT , B.SEGMENT  AS S_RULES, A.SUB_SEGMENT, B.SUB_SEGMENT AS SS_RULES,
		A.SEGMENTATION_ID, A.DIVISION_CODE, B.DIVISION_CODE AS DIV_JAN, A.PRODUCT_TYPE, B.PRODUCT_TYPE AS PRD_TYPE_JAN, A.PRODUCT_CODE , B.PRODUCT_CODE AS PRD_CODE_JAN,
		A.ACCOUNT_STATUS 
		FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A
		INNER JOIN IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY B ON A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID 
		WHERE A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '31 DEC 2025' AND B.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 FEB 2026'
		AND (A.SEGMENT <> NVL(B.SEGMENT,' ') OR A.SUB_SEGMENT <> NVL(B.SUB_SEGMENT,' ') OR A.GROUP_SEGMENT <> NVL(B.GROUP_SEGMENT,' '))
		AND A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = 'A'
		)Y
ON (X.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 FEB 2026'
	AND X.MASTERID = Y.MASTERID)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET X.GROUP_SEGMENT = Y.GROUP_SEGMENT,
			X.SEGMENT = Y.SEGMENT,
			X.SUB_SEGMENT = Y.SUB_SEGMENT,
			X.SEGMENTATION_ID = Y.SEGMENTATION_ID
			
-- UPDATE SEGMENT MULTIJASA
MERGE INTO IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY X
USING (
	SELECT XX.DOWNLOAD_DATE,XX.NOMORREKENING, XX.GROUP_SEGMENT,XX.SEGMENT,XX.SUB_SEGMENT, C.PKID AS SEGMENTATION_ID FROM (
		SELECT TO_DATE(FICMISDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') AS DOWNLOAD_DATE, NOMORREKENING ,
		CASE WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'Pensiun & Pra Pensiun' THEN 'PENSIUN_PRAPENSIUN'
		WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'KUR' THEN 'KUR'
		WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'Griya' THEN 'GRIYA'
		WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'Mitraguna' THEN 'MULTIGUNA'
		WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'BISNIS BANKING/SMALL' THEN 'SME' END AS GROUP_SEGMENT, B.GROUP_SEGMENT AS GS_IMA,
		CASE WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'Pensiun & Pra Pensiun' THEN 'PENSIUN_PRAPENSIUN_PIUTANG'
		WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'KUR' THEN 'KUR_PIUTANG'
		WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'Griya' THEN 'GRIYA_PIUTANG'
		WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'Mitraguna' THEN 'MULTIGUNA_PIUTANG'
		WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'BISNIS BANKING/SMALL' THEN 'SME_PIUTANG' END AS SEGMENT, B.SEGMENT AS S_IMA,
		CASE WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'Pensiun & Pra Pensiun' THEN 'PENSIUN_PRAPENSIUN_IJARAH_PIUTANG'
		WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'KUR' THEN 'KUR_IJARAH_PIUTANG'
		WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'Griya' THEN 'GRIYA_IJARAH_PIUTANG'
		WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'Mitraguna' THEN 'MULTIGUNA_IJARAH_PIUTANG'
		WHEN TRIM(SEGMEN) = 'BISNIS BANKING/SMALL' THEN 'SME_IJARAH_PIUTANG' END AS SUB_SEGMENT, B.SUB_SEGMENT AS SS_IMA
		 FROM IMPORT_MULTIJASA_FEB26 A
		LEFT JOIN IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY B ON A.NOMORREKENING = B.ACCOUNT_NUMBER 
		AND B.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 FEB 2026' )XX LEFT JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING C ON XX.GROUP_SEGMENT = C.SEGMENT_NAME_LV1 
		AND XX.SEGMENT = C.SEGMENT_NAME_LV2 AND XX.SUB_SEGMENT = C.SEGMENT_NAME_LV3 
		GROUP BY XX.DOWNLOAD_DATE,XX.NOMORREKENING, XX.GROUP_SEGMENT,XX.SEGMENT,XX.SUB_SEGMENT, C.PKID
	)Y
ON (X.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 FEB 2026'
	AND X.ACCOUNT_NUMBER  = Y.NOMORREKENING)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET X.GROUP_SEGMENT = Y.GROUP_SEGMENT,
			X.SEGMENT = Y.SEGMENT,
			X.SUB_SEGMENT = Y.SUB_SEGMENT,
			X.SEGMENTATION_ID = Y.SEGMENTATION_ID
			
-- UPDATE TUNGGAKAN POKOK/TUNGGAKAN MARGIN

MERGE INTO IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A
USING (SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, TRIM(NOMORREKENING) AS ACCOUNT_NUMBER, TO_NUMBER(REPLACE(TUNGGAKAN,'.','')) AS TUNGGAKAN,TO_NUMBER(REPLACE(IMBALAN,'.','')) AS IMBALAN 
			FROM (
					SELECT TO_DATE(FICMISDATE,'DD/MM/YYYY') AS DOWNLOAD_DATE, NOMORREKENING
					,TRIM(REPLACE(" Tunggakan_Pokok ",' -   ',0)) AS TUNGGAKAN,TRIM(REPLACE(" Tunggakan_Imbalan ",' -   ',0)) AS IMBALAN --TO_NUMBER(REPLACE(REPLACE(" Tunggakan_Pokok ", '.', ','),' -   ',0)) ,TO_NUMBER(REPLACE(REPLACE(" Tunggakan_Imbalan ", '.', ','),' -   ',0)) 
					FROM IMPORT_IMBT_TUNGGAKAN_JAN26 
			)X 
		)B
ON (A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '31 JAN 2026'
	AND A.ACCOUNT_NUMBER = B.ACCOUNT_NUMBER)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET
			A.OUTSTANDING_PAST_DUE = B.TUNGGAKAN,
			A.MARGIN_PAST_DUE  = B.IMBALAN
			
-- UPDATE MARGIN ACCRUE
MERGE INTO IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY I
USING (	
		SELECT A.*,B.MASTERID  
		FROM PSAK413.IMPORT_ACRUE_MARGIN_MURABAHAH_202601 A
		LEFT JOIN IFRS_MASTER_ID B ON A.NOMORREKENING = B.ACCOUNT_NUMBER 
		) J
ON (I.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '31 JAN 2026'
	AND I.MASTERID = J.MASTERID)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET
			I.MARGIN_ACCRUED  = J.IMBALANYANGAKANDITERIMA	

-- UPDATE NASABAH INDIVIDU (IMPAIR_FLAG)
UPDATE IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
SET IMPAIRED_FLAG = 'C'
WHERE ACCOUNT_STATUS = 'A'
AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = '31 JAN 2026'

MERGE INTO IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY I
USING (	
		SELECT *  
		FROM PSAK413.IMPORT_LIST_INDIVIDUAL_JAN26
		) J
ON (I.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '31 JAN 2026'
	AND I.ACCOUNT_STATUS = 'A'
	AND I.ACCOUNT_NUMBER  = J."NOMOR LOAN")
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET
			I.IMPAIRED_FLAG = 'I'			

-- UPDATE TUNGGAKAN POKOK NON MURABAHAH
MERGE INTO IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A
USING (SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, TRIM(NOMORREKENING) AS ACCOUNT_NUMBER, TO_NUMBER(REPLACE(TUNGGAKAN,'.','')) AS TUNGGAKAN,TO_NUMBER(REPLACE(IMBALAN,'.','')) AS IMBALAN 
			FROM (
					SELECT TO_DATE(PERIODE,'DD/MM/YYYY') AS DOWNLOAD_DATE, NOMORREKENING
					,TRIM(REPLACE(" Tunggakan Pokok ",' -   ',0)) AS TUNGGAKAN,TRIM(REPLACE(" TunggakanBagiHasilJumlah ",' -   ',0)) AS IMBALAN  
					FROM IMPORT_TUNGGAKAN_NON_MURABAHAH_JAN26 
			)X 
		)B
ON (A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '31 JAN 2026'
	AND A.ACCOUNT_NUMBER = B.ACCOUNT_NUMBER)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET
			A.OUTSTANDING_PAST_DUE = B.TUNGGAKAN,
			A.MARGIN_PAST_DUE  = B.IMBALAN

-- UPDATE IS IMPAIRED			
UPDATE IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
SET IS_IMPAIRED  = 1
WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = '31 JAN 2026' 
AND ACCOUNT_STATUS = 'A'									
	
-- UPDATE IAS_CLASS BY DEFAULT
UPDATE IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
SET IAS_CLASS  = 'A'
WHERE ACCOUNT_STATUS = 'A'
AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = '31 JAN 2026'

-- UPDATE UNAMORT_OTHERS -- HARUS MENGGGUNAKAN USER HWDB
MERGE INTO PSAK413.IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A
USING (
			SELECT LOAN_NO, (KP+CABANG) AS UNAMORT FROM (
			SELECT LOAN_NO , TO_NUMBER(" KP ") AS KP, TO_NUMBER(REPLACE(" CABANG ",',','')) AS CABANG FROM PSAK.RINCIAN_EIR_NEW 
			WHERE PERIODE = '28/02/2026'
			)X
		)B
ON (A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 FEB 2026'
	AND A.ACCOUNT_NUMBER = B.LOAN_NO)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET
			A.UNAMORT_OTHERS = B.UNAMORT

-- UPDATE ACCOUNT_STATUS JADI C			
UPDATE IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY 
SET ACCOUNT_STATUS = 'C'
WHERE DAY_PAST_DUE IS NULL AND BI_COLLECTABILITY IS NULL AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = '28 FEB 2026'
			
								
*/
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_BUCKET_DETAIL
AS 
BEGIN
     
    
    MERGE INTO IFRS_BUCKET_DETAIL a
    USING (
    
    	 SELECT * 
	 FROM (
	 SELECT b."unique_code", a."bucket_id",  a."bucket_name",
		a."range_from_days", a."range_to_days",
		a."rating_value", a."bi_collectability_value",
		nvl(a."is_deleted",0) IS_DELETED,
		ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY b."unique_code", a."bucket_id" ORDER BY a."pkid" DESC ) RN 
	 FROM "GroupBucketDetail"@DBCONFIGLINK a 
	JOIN "GroupBucket"@DBCONFIGLINK b ON a."syscode_group_bucket" = b."syscode_group_bucket"
	WHERE a."bucket_id" IS NOT NULL ) x 
	WHERE x.rn = 1 
    ) b
    ON (a.bucket_group = b."unique_code" AND a.bucket_id = b."bucket_id" )  
    
     WHEN MATCHED THEN
        UPDATE SET   
            a.UPDATED_BY              = 'SP_IFRS_BUCKET_DETAIL',
            a.UPDATED_DATE            = sysdate,
            a.IS_DELETED              = B.IS_DELETED
    
    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
        INSERT (
            BUCKET_GROUP, bucket_id, BUCKET_NAME, RANGE_START, RANGE_END,
            RATING_VALUE, BI_COLLECTABILITY_VALUE,
            CREATED_BY, CREATED_DATE , IS_DELETED)
        VALUES (
            b."unique_code", b."bucket_id",
            b."bucket_name", b."range_from_days", b."range_to_days",
		b."rating_value", b."bi_collectability_value",
		'SP_IFRS_BUCKET_DETAIL',sysdate, B.IS_DELETED
         );
        
    commit;
     
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_BUCKET_HEADER
AS 
BEGIN
     
    
    MERGE INTO IFRS_BUCKET_HEADER a
    USING (
     
    SELECT * 
    from(
     SELECT "unique_code",
		"bucket_group_name",
		"bucket_type",
		"is_deleted",
		"syscode_group_bucket",
		ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY "syscode_group_bucket" ORDER BY "pkid" desc) rn 
	FROM "GroupBucket"@DBCONFIGLINK) WHERE rn = 1 
    ) b 
    ON (a.syscode_group_bucket = b."syscode_group_bucket" )  
     
    WHEN MATCHED THEN
        UPDATE SET   
            a.UPDATED_BY              = 'SP_IFRS_BUCKET_HEADER',
            a.UPDATED_DATE            = sysdate,
            a.IS_DELETED              = nvl(b."is_deleted",0)
 
    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
        INSERT (
            BUCKET_GROUP, BUCKET_DESCRIPTION, OPTION_GROUPING, IS_DELETED,
            CREATED_BY, CREATED_DATE,
            SYSCODE_GROUP_BUCKET)
        VALUES (
            b."unique_code", b."bucket_group_name",
            b."bucket_type", NVL(b."is_deleted",0),
            'SP_IFRS_BUCKET_HEADER', sysdate ,
            b."syscode_group_bucket"
        );
        
    commit;
 
     
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413."SP_IFRS_DEFAULT_CRITERIA" 
AS 
 
BEGIN
     
    
    MERGE INTO IFRS_DEFAULT_CRITERIA a
    USING (
    
     SELECT * 
     FROM (
     selecT "pkid", "syscode_default_criteria", "default_criteria_name",  
        "sql_conditions", "source_table_conditions", "is_deleted",
        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY "syscode_default_criteria" ORDER BY "pkid" DESC ) rn 
     from "DefaultCriteria"@DBCONFIGLINK) A 
     WHERE RN = 1 
    ) b
    ON (a.SYSCODE_DEFAULT_CRITERIA = b."syscode_default_criteria"
        )  
     
    WHEN MATCHED THEN
        UPDATE SET  
            a.sql_conditions          = b."sql_conditions",
            a.UPDATED_BY              = 'SP_IFRS_DEFAULT_CRITERIA',
            a.UPDATED_DATE            = sysdate,
            a.IS_DELETED              = b."is_deleted"
 
    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
        INSERT (
            SYSCODE_DEFAULT_CRITERIA, DEFAULT_CRITERIA_NAME,
            SQL_CONDITIONS, SOURCE_TABLE_CONDITIONS,
            IS_DELETED, 
            CREATED_BY, CREATED_DATE 
            )
        VALUES (
            b."syscode_default_criteria", b."default_criteria_name",
            b."sql_conditions", b."source_table_conditions",
            nvl(b."is_deleted", 0),
            'SP_IFRS_DEFAULT_CRITERIA', sysdate
        );
        
        commit;
     
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413."SP_IFRS_DEFAULT_RULE" (
	p_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    p_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    p_MODEL_TYPE    IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '',
    p_MODEL_ID      IN NUMBER   DEFAULT 0,
    p_PRC           IN CHAR     DEFAULT 'M'
)
AS
    v_CURRDATE      DATE;
    v_TABLENAME     VARCHAR2(50);
    v_STR_SQL       CLOB;
    v_SCRIPT1       CLOB;
	v_SQL_CONDITIONS CLOB;
    v_RULE_ID       NUMBER;
BEGIN
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- INIT
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF p_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO v_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        v_CURRDATE := p_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    v_TABLENAME :=
        CASE
            WHEN p_PRC = 'M' THEN 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT'
            WHEN p_PRC = 'S' THEN 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY'
            ELSE 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_' || p_RUNID
        END;

   	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE TMPRULE';

    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- LOAD DEFAULT RULES
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF p_MODEL_TYPE IS NULL OR p_MODEL_TYPE = '' THEN

        INSERT INTO TMPRULE
        SELECT DISTINCT DEFAULT_RULE_ID
        FROM IFRS_PD_RULES_CONFIG
        WHERE IS_ACTIVE = 1
          AND IS_DELETED = 0
          AND PD_METHOD <> 'VAS'
          AND (PKID = p_MODEL_ID OR p_MODEL_ID = 0);

        INSERT INTO TMPRULE
        SELECT DISTINCT DEFAULT_RULE_ID
        FROM IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
        WHERE IS_DELETED = 0
          AND LGD_METHOD <> 'VAS'
          AND (PKID = p_MODEL_ID OR p_MODEL_ID = 0);

    ELSIF p_MODEL_TYPE = 'PD' THEN

        INSERT INTO TMPRULE
        SELECT DISTINCT DEFAULT_RULE_ID
        FROM IFRS_PD_RULES_CONFIG
        WHERE IS_ACTIVE = 1
          AND IS_DELETED = 0
          AND PD_METHOD <> 'VAS'
          AND (PKID = p_MODEL_ID OR p_MODEL_ID = 0);
	
     ELSIF p_MODEL_TYPE = 'LGD' THEN

        INSERT INTO TMPRULE
        SELECT DISTINCT DEFAULT_RULE_ID
        FROM IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
        WHERE IS_DELETED = 0
          AND LGD_METHOD <> 'VAS'
          AND (PKID = p_MODEL_ID OR p_MODEL_ID = 0);
    END IF;

    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- DELETE EXISTING DEFAULT DATA
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    DELETE FROM IFRS_DEFAULT
    WHERE RULE_ID IN (SELECT DEFAULT_RULE_ID FROM TMPRULE)
      AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = LAST_DAY(v_CURRDATE);

    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- LOOP RULE
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    FOR r_rule IN (
        SELECT
		    A.PKID,
		    A.SQL_CONDITIONS
		FROM IFRS_DEFAULT_CRITERIA A
		JOIN TMPRULE B
		  ON A.PKID = B.DEFAULT_RULE_ID
		ORDER BY A.PKID     
    )
    LOOP
        v_RULE_ID := r_rule.PKID;
    	v_SQL_CONDITIONS := r_rule.SQL_CONDITIONS;
       
        v_SCRIPT1 :=' ' || v_SQL_CONDITIONS || ' ';
        ------------------------------------------------------------------
        -- BUILD FINAL INSERT SQL
        ------------------------------------------------------------------
        v_STR_SQL :=
            'INSERT INTO IFRS_DEFAULT (
                DOWNLOAD_DATE,
                RULE_ID,
                MASTERID,
                FACILITY_NUMBER,
                CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
                OS_AT_DEFAULT,
                EQV_AT_DEFAULT,
                PLAFOND_AT_DEFAULT,
                EQV_PLAFOND_AT_DEFAULT,
                EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
                CCY_AT_DEFAULT,
                CREATED_DATE
            )
            SELECT
                LAST_DAY(ifrs_master_account.DOWNLOAD_DATE),
                ' || v_RULE_ID || ',
                ifrs_master_account.MASTERID,
                ifrs_master_account.FACILITY_NUMBER,
                ifrs_master_account.CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
                NVL(B.OUTSTANDING, ifrs_master_account.OUTSTANDING),
                NVL(B.OUTSTANDING, ifrs_master_account.OUTSTANDING) * ifrs_master_account.EXCHANGE_RATE,
                ifrs_master_account.PLAFOND,
                ifrs_master_account.PLAFOND * ifrs_master_account.EXCHANGE_RATE,
                NVL(ifrs_master_account.EIR, ifrs_master_account.MARGIN_RATE),
                ifrs_master_account.CURRENCY,
                SYSDATE
            FROM ' || v_TABLENAME || ' ifrs_master_account
            LEFT JOIN IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_WO B
                   ON ifrs_master_account.MASTERID = B.MASTERID
                  AND ifrs_master_account.DOWNLOAD_DATE >= B.DOWNLOAD_DATE
            WHERE ifrs_master_account.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' ||
            TO_CHAR(v_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || '''
              AND ' || v_SCRIPT1 ||'';

        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_STR_SQL;
    END LOOP;

    COMMIT;
    
    MERGE INTO IFRS_DEFAULT A
	USING (
	    SELECT
	        A.RULE_ID,
	        A.DOWNLOAD_DATE,
	        A.MASTERID,
	        B.OUTSTANDING AS OS_12M,
	        B.OUTSTANDING * B.EXCHANGE_RATE EQV_OS_12M,
	        ROW_NUMBER() OVER (
	            PARTITION BY A.RULE_ID, A.MASTERID
	            ORDER BY B.DOWNLOAD_DATE
	        ) RN
	    FROM IFRS_DEFAULT A
	    JOIN IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY B
	      ON A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID
	    JOIN TMPRULE C
	      ON A.RULE_ID = C.DEFAULT_RULE_ID
	    WHERE B.DOWNLOAD_DATE BETWEEN ADD_MONTHS(A.DOWNLOAD_DATE, -12)
	                              AND A.DOWNLOAD_DATE
	      AND A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = v_CURRDATE
	      AND B.OUTSTANDING > 0
	) B
	ON (
	    A.RULE_ID = B.RULE_ID
	    AND A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID
	    AND A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE
	)
	WHEN MATCHED THEN
	UPDATE SET
	    A.OS_12M_BEFORE_DEFAULT      = B.OS_12M,
	    A.EQV_OS_12M_BEFORE_DEFAULT  = B.EQV_OS_12M
	WHERE B.RN = 1;

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EAD_RESULT (
    P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS 
    V_CURRDATE       DATE;
    V_DATADATE       VARCHAR2(20);
    V_TABLE_NAME     VARCHAR2(50);
    V_COUNT          NUMBER;
	V_MODEL_ID       NUMBER;

-- DYNAMIC NAMES / QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY      CLOB;

    -- TABLE NAMES
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT 		VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_IFRS_EIL_IMA					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT				VARCHAR2(100);

    -- LOG / RESULT
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_EAD_RESULT';
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_QUERYS        VARCHAR2(8000);
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
    
    V_STR_SQL        CLOB;
    V_STR_SQL_RULE   CLOB;
    V_RULE_ID        VARCHAR2(250);
    V_ID             NUMBER := 0;
    V_MAX_ID         NUMBER := 0;
    V_SEQUENCE       VARCHAR2(50);
    
BEGIN
	-- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := 0;

    -- CHOOSE TABLE NAMES BASED ON MODE
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT		:= 'IFRS_EAD_RESULT_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 		:= 'GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD';
    ELSE
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 		:= 'GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD';
    	V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT		:= 'IFRS_EAD_RESULT';
    END IF;

    BEGIN
        SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, P_RUNID, 0, SYSTIMESTAMP);
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('WARNING: SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG FAILED: ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
    COMMIT;

    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        
        -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS (OWNED BY CURRENT SCHEMA)
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM USER_TABLES
        WHERE TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT || ' AS SELECT * FROM IFRS_EAD_RESULT WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        
    ELSE
    	    
	   	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE ' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT || ' ' ;
   
    END IF;
   
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD' ; 
    COMMIT;
   /*
    V_STR_QUERY := '
	INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, PMTDATE, SEQ, PRINCIPAL, SUM_PRINCIPAL)
		WITH CTE_INIT AS ( ' ||
		'	SELECT MAX(DOWNLOAD_DATE) AS DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID ' ||
		'	FROM IFRS_INITIAL_PAYM_SCHD ' ||
		'	WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')  
			GROUP BY MASTERID ' ||
		'), CTE AS ( ' ||
		'SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE , A.MASTERID ,LAST_DAY(A.PMTDATE) AS PMTDATE ,MAX(MONTHS_BETWEEN(LAST_DAY(A.PMTDATE),A.DOWNLOAD_DATE)) AS SEQ , '||
		'SUM(A.PRINCIPAL) AS PRINCIPAL , '||
		'	SUM(SUM(A.PRINCIPAL)) OVER (ORDER BY LAST_DAY(A.PMTDATE)) AS SUM_PRINCIPAL ' ||
		'	FROM IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_ALL A ' ||
		'	WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE  <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
				AND PMTDATE > TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
				AND EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM CTE_INIT X WHERE X.DOWNLOAD_DATE = A.DOWNLOAD_DATE AND X.MASTERID = A.MASTERID)
		GROUP BY LAST_DAY(A.PMTDATE),A.DOWNLOAD_DATE , A.MASTERID )
		SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, PMTDATE, SEQ, PRINCIPAL, SUM_PRINCIPAL
		FROM CTE ';
	*/	
	
	V_STR_QUERY := ' INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, PMTDATE, SEQ, PRINCIPAL, SUM_PRINCIPAL)
		WITH CTE_INIT AS ( 
			SELECT MAX(DOWNLOAD_DATE) AS DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID 
			FROM IFRS_INITIAL_PAYM_SCHD 
			WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE <=  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
			GROUP BY MASTERID 
		), CTE AS ( 
		SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE , A.MASTERID ,LAST_DAY(A.PMTDATE) AS PMTDATE ,
		MAX(MONTHS_BETWEEN(LAST_DAY(A.PMTDATE),A.DOWNLOAD_DATE)) AS SEQ ,  
		SUM(A.PRINCIPAL) AS PRINCIPAL 
		FROM IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_ALL A 
		WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE  <=  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
				AND PMTDATE >  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
				AND EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM CTE_INIT X WHERE X.DOWNLOAD_DATE = A.DOWNLOAD_DATE AND X.MASTERID = A.MASTERID)
		GROUP BY LAST_DAY(A.PMTDATE),A.DOWNLOAD_DATE , A.MASTERID )
		SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, PMTDATE, SEQ, PRINCIPAL, sum(PRINCIPAL) OVER (PARTITION BY MASTERID ORDER BY seq )
		FROM CTE ' ; 
	
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
	COMMIT;

	V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO ' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT || '(DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, GROUP_SEGMENT, SEGMENT, SUB_SEGMENT, RATING_CODE, DAY_PAST_DUE, BI_COLLECTABILITY,
					 ACCOUNT_NUMBER, ACCOUNT_STATUS, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, CUSTOMER_NAME, EXCHANGE_RATE, IMPAIRED_FLAG, OUTSTANDING, BUCKET_ID, REVOLVING_FLAG, 
					 PRODUCT_CODE, PRODUCT_TYPE, PLAFOND, LOAN_START_DATE, DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, EIR, LOAN_DUE_DATE, MARGIN_PAST_DUE, SEGMENTATION_ID,
					 LT_RULE_ID, CUSTOMER_GRADE, PRODUCT_ENTITY, DATA_SOURCE, PRODUCT_GROUP, IS_IMPAIRED, IFRS9_CLASS, PD_SEGMENT, LGD_SEGMENT, EAD_SEGMENT, BUCKET_GROUP,
					 LIFETIME, STAGE, UNAMORT_COST_AMT, UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, MARGIN_ACCRUED, FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, EAD_BALANCE, EAD_MARGIN, EIL_MODEL_ID, EAD_RULE_ID, LGD_RULE_ID,
					 LGD_ME_MODEL_ID, PD_RULE_ID, PD_ME_MODEL_ID, CURRENCY, EIL_AMOUNT, FLAG_VAS, UNUSED_AMOUNT, EAD_TYPE, SEQ, EAD_PRINCIPAL, CREATEDBY, CREATEDDATE)
					WITH CTE2 (
					    DOWNLOAD_DATE,INCLUDE_BULLET_PAYMENT, MASTERID, LIFETIME, SEQ,EAD_BALANCE, EAD_PRINCIPAL, EAD_MARGIN, SUM_PRINCIPAL
					) AS (
					    SELECT 
					        A.DOWNLOAD_DATE,CASE WHEN A.LOAN_DUE_DATE < A.DOWNLOAD_DATE THEN 0 ELSE 1 END AS INCLUDE_BULLET_PAYMENT, A.MASTERID, A.LIFETIME, 0 AS SEQ, A.EAD_BALANCE,
					        A.EAD_BALANCE + A.EAD_BALANCE_ADDITIONAL AS EAD_PRINCIPAL, A.EAD_MARGIN, CAST (0 AS NUMBER(32,6)) SUM_PRINCIPAL
					    FROM IFRS_EIL_IMA A 
					    UNION ALL
					    SELECT
					        X.DOWNLOAD_DATE, X.INCLUDE_BULLET_PAYMENT, X.MASTERID, X.LIFETIME, X.SEQ + 1 AS SEQ,X.EAD_BALANCE,
					        CASE 
					            WHEN X.SEQ + 1 = X.LIFETIME AND B.MASTERID IS NULL AND INCLUDE_BULLET_PAYMENT = 1 THEN 0
					            ELSE X.EAD_BALANCE - NVL(B.SUM_PRINCIPAL, X.SUM_PRINCIPAL)
					        END AS EAD_PRINCIPAL,
					        X.EAD_MARGIN,NVL(B.SUM_PRINCIPAL,X.SUM_PRINCIPAL)
					    FROM CTE2 X
					    LEFT JOIN GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD B
					        ON X.MASTERID = B.MASTERID       
					       AND X.SEQ + 1 = B.SEQ
					    WHERE X.SEQ + 1 <= X.LIFETIME
					)
					SELECT B.DOWNLOAD_DATE, B.MASTERID, B.GROUP_SEGMENT, B.SEGMENT, B.SUB_SEGMENT, B.RATING_CODE, B.DAY_PAST_DUE, B.BI_COLLECTABILITY, B.ACCOUNT_NUMBER,
					 B.ACCOUNT_STATUS, B.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, B.CUSTOMER_NAME, B.EXCHANGE_RATE, B.IMPAIRED_FLAG, B.OUTSTANDING, B.BUCKET_ID, B.REVOLVING_FLAG, B.PRODUCT_CODE,
					 B.PRODUCT_TYPE, B.PLAFOND, B.LOAN_START_DATE, B.DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, B.RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, B.EIR, B.LOAN_DUE_DATE, B.MARGIN_PAST_DUE, B.SEGMENTATION_ID,
					 B.LT_RULE_ID, B.CUSTOMER_GRADE, B.PRODUCT_ENTITY, B.DATA_SOURCE, B.PRODUCT_GROUP, B.IS_IMPAIRED, B.IFRS9_CLASS, B.PD_SEGMENT, B.LGD_SEGMENT,
					 B.EAD_SEGMENT, B.BUCKET_GROUP, B.LIFETIME, B.STAGE, B.UNAMORT_COST_AMT, B.UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, B.MARGIN_ACCRUED, B.FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, B.EAD_BALANCE,
					 A.EAD_MARGIN, B.EIL_MODEL_ID, B.EAD_RULE_ID, B.LGD_RULE_ID, B.LGD_ME_MODEL_ID, B.PD_RULE_ID, B.PD_ME_MODEL_ID, B.CURRENCY, B.EIL_AMOUNT,
					 B.FLAG_VAS, B.UNUSED_AMOUNT, B.EAD_TYPE, A.SEQ, CASE WHEN A.EAD_PRINCIPAL < 0 THEN 0 ELSE A.EAD_PRINCIPAL END AS EAD_PRINCIPAL, ''SP_IFRS_EAD_RESULT'' AS CREATEDBY, SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE
					FROM CTE2 A 
					INNER JOIN IFRS_EIL_IMA B 
						ON A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE 
						AND A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID 
						AND A.SEQ <= CASE WHEN B.STAGE = 1 THEN 11 ELSE A.SEQ END ';
					
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
		COMMIT;
        -----------------------------
	    -- Log & insert final data
	    -----------------------------
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT ||
                ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')' ;

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;

EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN SP_IFRS_PD_RULE_DATA: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EAD_RESULT_2 (
    P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS 
    V_CURRDATE       DATE;
    V_DATADATE       VARCHAR2(20);
    V_TABLE_NAME     VARCHAR2(50);
    V_COUNT          NUMBER;
	V_MODEL_ID       NUMBER;

-- DYNAMIC NAMES / QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY      CLOB;

    -- TABLE NAMES
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT 		VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_IFRS_EIL_IMA					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT				VARCHAR2(100);

    -- LOG / RESULT
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_EAD_RESULT';
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_QUERYS        VARCHAR2(8000);
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
    
    V_STR_SQL        CLOB;
    V_STR_SQL_RULE   CLOB;
    V_RULE_ID        VARCHAR2(250);
    V_ID             NUMBER := 0;
    V_MAX_ID         NUMBER := 0;
    V_SEQUENCE       VARCHAR2(50);
    
BEGIN
	-- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := 0;

    -- CHOOSE TABLE NAMES BASED ON MODE
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT		:= 'IFRS_EAD_RESULT_NEW_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 		:= 'GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD';
    ELSE
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 		:= 'GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD';
    	V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT		:= 'IFRS_EAD_RESULT_NEW';
    END IF;

    BEGIN
        SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, P_RUNID, 0, SYSTIMESTAMP);
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('WARNING: SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG FAILED: ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
    COMMIT;

    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        
        -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS (OWNED BY CURRENT SCHEMA)
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM USER_TABLES
        WHERE TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT || ' AS SELECT * FROM IFRS_EAD_RESULT_NEW WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        
    ELSE
    	    
	   	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE ' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT || ' ' ;
   
    END IF;
   
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD' ; 
    COMMIT;
	
	V_STR_QUERY := ' INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, PMTDATE, SEQ, PRINCIPAL, SUM_PRINCIPAL)
		WITH CTE_INIT AS ( 
			SELECT MAX(DOWNLOAD_DATE) AS DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID 
			FROM IFRS_INITIAL_PAYM_SCHD 
			WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE <=  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
			GROUP BY MASTERID 
		), CTE AS ( 
		SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE , A.MASTERID ,LAST_DAY(A.PMTDATE) AS PMTDATE ,
		MAX(MONTHS_BETWEEN(LAST_DAY(A.PMTDATE),A.DOWNLOAD_DATE)) AS SEQ ,  
		SUM(A.PRINCIPAL) AS PRINCIPAL 
		FROM IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_ALL A 
		WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE  <=  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
				AND PMTDATE >  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
				AND EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM CTE_INIT X WHERE X.DOWNLOAD_DATE = A.DOWNLOAD_DATE AND X.MASTERID = A.MASTERID)
		GROUP BY LAST_DAY(A.PMTDATE),A.DOWNLOAD_DATE , A.MASTERID )
		SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, PMTDATE, SEQ, PRINCIPAL, sum(PRINCIPAL) OVER (PARTITION BY MASTERID ORDER BY seq )
		FROM CTE ' ; 
	
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
	COMMIT;



	V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO ' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT || '(DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, GROUP_SEGMENT, SEGMENT, SUB_SEGMENT, ACCOUNT_NUMBER, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, EXCHANGE_RATE,
					 OUTSTANDING, BUCKET_ID, REVOLVING_FLAG, PLAFOND, EIR, MARGIN_PAST_DUE, SEGMENTATION_ID, LT_RULE_ID, DATA_SOURCE, BUCKET_GROUP, LIFETIME, STAGE, UNAMORT_COST_AMT,
					 UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, MARGIN_ACCRUED, FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, EAD_BALANCE, EAD_MARGIN, EIL_MODEL_ID, EAD_RULE_ID, LGD_RULE_ID, LGD_ME_MODEL_ID, 
					 PD_RULE_ID, PD_ME_MODEL_ID, CURRENCY, EIL_AMOUNT, UNUSED_AMOUNT, SEQ, EAD_PRINCIPAL, CREATEDBY, CREATEDDATE)
					WITH CTE2 (
					    DOWNLOAD_DATE,INCLUDE_BULLET_PAYMENT, MASTERID, LIFETIME, SEQ,EAD_BALANCE, EAD_PRINCIPAL, EAD_MARGIN, SUM_PRINCIPAL
					) AS (
					    SELECT 
					        A.DOWNLOAD_DATE,CASE WHEN A.LOAN_DUE_DATE < A.DOWNLOAD_DATE THEN 0 ELSE 1 END AS INCLUDE_BULLET_PAYMENT, A.MASTERID, A.LIFETIME, 0 AS SEQ, A.EAD_BALANCE,
					        A.EAD_BALANCE + A.EAD_BALANCE_ADDITIONAL AS EAD_PRINCIPAL, A.EAD_MARGIN, CAST (0 AS NUMBER(32,6)) SUM_PRINCIPAL
					    FROM IFRS_EIL_IMA A 
					    UNION ALL
					    SELECT
					        X.DOWNLOAD_DATE, X.INCLUDE_BULLET_PAYMENT, X.MASTERID, X.LIFETIME, X.SEQ + 1 AS SEQ,X.EAD_BALANCE,
					        CASE 
					            WHEN X.SEQ + 1 = X.LIFETIME AND B.MASTERID IS NULL AND INCLUDE_BULLET_PAYMENT = 1 THEN 0
					            ELSE X.EAD_BALANCE - NVL(B.SUM_PRINCIPAL, X.SUM_PRINCIPAL)
					        END AS EAD_PRINCIPAL,
					        X.EAD_MARGIN,NVL(B.SUM_PRINCIPAL,X.SUM_PRINCIPAL)
					    FROM CTE2 X
					    LEFT JOIN GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD B
					        ON X.MASTERID = B.MASTERID       
					       AND X.SEQ + 1 = B.SEQ
					    WHERE X.SEQ + 1 <= X.LIFETIME
					)
					SELECT B.DOWNLOAD_DATE, B.MASTERID, B.GROUP_SEGMENT, B.SEGMENT, B.SUB_SEGMENT, B.ACCOUNT_NUMBER, B.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, B.EXCHANGE_RATE,
					 B.OUTSTANDING, B.BUCKET_ID, B.REVOLVING_FLAG, B.PLAFOND, B.EIR, B.MARGIN_PAST_DUE, B.SEGMENTATION_ID,
					 B.LT_RULE_ID, B.DATA_SOURCE, B.BUCKET_GROUP, B.LIFETIME, B.STAGE, B.UNAMORT_COST_AMT, B.UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, B.MARGIN_ACCRUED, B.FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, B.EAD_BALANCE,
					 A.EAD_MARGIN, B.EIL_MODEL_ID, B.EAD_RULE_ID, B.LGD_RULE_ID, B.LGD_ME_MODEL_ID, B.PD_RULE_ID, B.PD_ME_MODEL_ID, B.CURRENCY, B.EIL_AMOUNT,
					 B.UNUSED_AMOUNT, A.SEQ, CASE WHEN A.EAD_PRINCIPAL < 0 THEN 0 ELSE A.EAD_PRINCIPAL END AS EAD_PRINCIPAL, ''SP_IFRS_EAD_RESULT'' AS CREATEDBY, SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE
					FROM CTE2 A 
					INNER JOIN IFRS_EIL_IMA B 
						ON A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE 
						AND A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID 
						AND A.SEQ <= CASE WHEN B.STAGE = 1 THEN 11 ELSE A.SEQ END ';
					
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
		COMMIT;
        -----------------------------
	    -- Log & insert final data
	    -----------------------------
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT ||
                ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')' ;

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;

EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN SP_IFRS_EAD_RESULT_2: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EAD_RULES_CONFIG
AS 
 
BEGIN
     
    MERGE INTO IFRS_EAD_RULES_CONFIG a
    USING (
    
    	 SELECT * 
		 FROM (
		 
				SELECT a."ead_name",A."syscode_ead_config" ,
					B.PKID AS SEGMENTATION_ID, A."balance_source",  
					NVL(C.PKID,0) AS LIFETIME_RULE_ID,
					a."is_ead_parameter_lifetime", A."include_accrued_interest", A."include_unamortized_fee_cost", a."include_interest_margin_past_due",
					NVL(A."is_deleted",0) AS IS_DELETE,
					ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY a."syscode_ead_config" ORDER BY a."pkid" desc) RN
					 FROM "EadConfiguration"@DBCONFIGLINK a 
					JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING B ON a."segment_code" = b.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION
					LEFT JOIN IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG C ON a."lifetime_code" = C.SYSCODE_LIFETIME
						) x 
		WHERE x.rn = 1 
    ) b
    ON (a.SYSCODE_EAD = b."syscode_ead_config" )  
    WHEN MATCHED THEN
        UPDATE SET   
            a.UPDATEDBY              = 'SP_IFRS_EAD_RULES_CONFIG',
            a.UPDATEDDATE            = sysdate,
            a.IS_DELETE              = B.IS_DELETE,
            a.EAD_BALANCE			 = B."balance_source",
            A.UNAMORTIZED_FEE_COST_FLAG = B."include_unamortized_fee_cost",
            A.MARGIN_ACCRUED_FLAG	 = B."include_accrued_interest",
            A.MARGIN_PAST_DUE_FLAG	 = B."include_interest_margin_past_due"
    
    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
        INSERT (
            EAD_RULE_NAME,
		    SYSCODE_EAD,
		    SEGMENTATION_ID,
		    EAD_BALANCE,
		    LIFETIME_RULE_ID,
		    LIFETIME_FLAG,
		    UNAMORTIZED_FEE_COST_FLAG,
		    MARGIN_ACCRUED_FLAG,
		    MARGIN_PAST_DUE_FLAG,
		    IS_DELETE,
		    CREATEDBY,
		    CREATEDDATE
		    )
        VALUES (
            b."ead_name",b."syscode_ead_config" ,
		b.SEGMENTATION_ID,b."balance_source", 
		b.LIFETIME_RULE_ID, b."is_ead_parameter_lifetime",B."include_unamortized_fee_cost",B."include_accrued_interest",B."include_interest_margin_past_due", B.IS_DELETE,
		'SP_IFRS_EAD_RULES_CONFIG',sysdate
        );
        
        commit;
     
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EIL_GENERATE_IMA (
    P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS 
	
	c               INTEGER;
	rows_processed  INTEGER;
	 
    V_CURRDATE       DATE;
    V_DATADATE       VARCHAR2(20);
    V_TABLE_NAME     VARCHAR2(50);
	V_PREVDATE       DATE;
    V_COUNT          NUMBER;
	V_MODEL_ID       NUMBER;

-- DYNAMIC NAMES / QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY      VARCHAR2(8000);

    -- TABLE NAMES
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT 		VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_PMA				  			VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TMP_PD  						VARCHAR2(100);
    V_IFRS_EIL_IMA					VARCHAR2(100);
    v_eil_model_id				 	NUMBER;
    v_maxrn			 				NUMBER;
    V_IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING 	VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG					VARCHAR2(100);

    -- LOG / RESULT
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_EIL_GENERATE_IMA';
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_QUERYS        VARCHAR2(8000);
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
    
    V_STR_SQL        CLOB;
    V_STR_SQL_RULE   CLOB;
    V_RULE_ID        VARCHAR2(250);
    V_ID             NUMBER := 0;
    V_MAX_ID         NUMBER := 0;
    V_SEQUENCE       VARCHAR2(50);
    
BEGIN
	-- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, -1));
    V_MODEL_ID := 0;

    -- CHOOSE TABLE NAMES BASED ON MODE
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_PMA  				:= 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY_' || P_RUNID;
        V_TMP_PD  			:= 'TMP_PD_' || P_RUNID;
        V_IFRS_EIL_IMA		:= 'IFRS_EIL_IMA_' || P_RUNID;
    ELSE
        V_PMA  				:= 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY';
        V_TMP_PD  			:= 'TMP_PD';
        V_IFRS_EIL_IMA		:= 'IFRS_EIL_IMA';
    END IF;

    BEGIN
        SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, P_RUNID, 0, SYSTIMESTAMP);
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN 
            DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('WARNING: SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG FAILED: ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
    COMMIT;

    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        
        -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS (OWNED BY CURRENT SCHEMA)
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM USER_TABLES
        WHERE TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_IFRS_EIL_IMA);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_IMA;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_IMA || ' AS SELECT * FROM IFRS_EIL_IMA WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        
        COMMIT;
    ELSE
    	    
    	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE ' || V_IFRS_EIL_IMA || '';
	    COMMIT;
    
    END IF;

  -- Pilih nama tabel sesuai PRC
  v_table_name := V_PMA;

  -- Ambil EIL_MODEL_ID yang aktif atau persis p_model_id
  SELECT pkid
    INTO v_eil_model_id
    FROM IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER
   WHERE pkid = v_model_id
      OR (v_model_id = 0 AND IS_EOM = 1);

  EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE TMP_QRY';

  -- Build query dinamis per baris model, mirip T-SQL Anda (masuk ke TMP_QRY)
  INSERT INTO TMP_QRY (RN, QRY)
  SELECT
    ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY A.EIL_MODEL_ID) AS RN,
    
    'SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE, A.MASTERID, A.GROUP_SEGMENT, A.SEGMENT, A.SUB_SEGMENT, '
      || TO_CHAR(A.SEGMENTATION_ID) || ', A.ACCOUNT_NUMBER, NVL(A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, ''''), '
      || NVL(A.LT_RULE_ID,0) || ', A.DPD_CIF, A.DAY_PAST_DUE, A.RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, '
      || 'A.DATA_SOURCE, A.PRODUCT_CODE, A.PRODUCT_TYPE, A.PRODUCT_GROUP, A.IS_IMPAIRED, A.IFRS9_CLASS, '''
      || NVL(A.SUB_SEGMENT_PD, '') || ''', ''' || NVL(A.SUB_SEGMENT_LGD, '') || ''', ''' || NVL(A.SUB_SEGMENT_EAD, '') || ''', '
      || ' ''' || A.BUCKET_GROUP || ''', CASE WHEN D.BUCKET_ID > NVL(G.NO_BUCKET,0) THEN D.BUCKET_ID 
			ELSE 
			NVL(G.NO_BUCKET,0) END BUCKET_ID, A.STAGE, A.REVOLVING_FLAG, NVL(A.EIR, A.MARGIN_RATE) AS EIR, '
      || 'A.OUTSTANDING, NVL(A.UNAMORT_COST_AMT,0), NVL(A.UNAMORT_FEE_AMT,0), NVL(A.FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT,0), '
      || 'NVL(A.PLAFOND,0) PLAFOND, ' || TO_CHAR(A.EIL_MODEL_ID) || ', ' || TO_CHAR(A.EAD_RULE_ID) || ', '''
      || TO_CHAR(A.EAD_TYPE) || ''', ' || NVL(A.LGD_RULE_ID,0) || ', '
      || NVL(A.LGD_ME_MODEL_ID,0) || ', ' || TO_CHAR(A.PD_RULE_ID) || ', ' || TO_CHAR(A.PD_ME_MODEL_ID)
      || ', A.CURRENCY, A.CREATEDBY, A.IMPAIRED_FLAG, A.CUSTOMER_NAME, A.ACCOUNT_STATUS, '
      || 'NVL(A.EIL_AMOUNT,0) AS EIL_AMOUNT,  '
      || ' A.RATING_CODE, NVL(A.EXCHANGE_RATE,0) AS EXCHANGE_RATE, A.LOAN_START_DATE, A.LOAN_DUE_DATE,  '
      || TO_CHAR(A.FLAG_VAS) || ', '
      || ' A.BI_COLLECTABILITY ,CASE WHEN LAST_DAY(NVL(A.LOAN_DUE_DATE,''31 JAN 1990'')) <= LAST_DAY(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(v_currdate, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')) THEN '
      || NVL(A.LIFETIME,0) || ' ELSE MONTHS_BETWEEN( LAST_DAY(NVL(A.LOAN_DUE_DATE,''31 JAN 1990'')), LAST_DAY(A.DOWNLOAD_DATE)) END AS LIFETIME, NVL(A.' 
      || TO_CHAR(A.EAD_BALANCE) || ',0) , ' || TO_CHAR(A.EAD_BALANCE_INTEREST) || ' AS EAD_BALANCE_INTEREST,'
      || TO_CHAR(A.EAD_BALANCE_ADDITIONAL) || ', 0 AS EAD_BALANCE_INTEREST_ADDITIONAL, A.MARGIN_ACCRUED '
      || 'FROM ' || v_table_name || ' A '
      || 'JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING B ON A.SEGMENTATION_ID = B.PKID '
      || 'LEFT JOIN IFRS_BUCKET_HEADER C ON ''' || A.BUCKET_GROUP || ''' = C.BUCKET_GROUP '
      || 'LEFT JOIN IFRS_BUCKET_DETAIL D ON C.BUCKET_GROUP = D.BUCKET_GROUP '
      || 'AND ( CASE '
      || '              WHEN C.OPTION_GROUPING = ''DPD_ACCT'' THEN A.DAY_PAST_DUE '
      || '              WHEN C.OPTION_GROUPING = ''DPD_CIF''  THEN A.DPD_CIF '
      || '              WHEN C.OPTION_GROUPING = ''BIC''      THEN A.BI_COLLECTABILITY '
      || '            END '
      || '           BETWEEN D.RANGE_START AND D.RANGE_END )'
      || 'LEFT JOIN VW_IFRS_MAX_BUCKET F ON C.BUCKET_GROUP = F.BUCKET_GROUP '
      || 'LEFT JOIN (SELECT X.DOWNLOAD_DATE,X.NOLOAN,X.MASTERID, MAX(NO_BUCKET) AS NO_BUCKET 
									FROM LIST_NASABAH_RESTRU_BENCANA X GROUP BY X.DOWNLOAD_DATE,X.NOLOAN,X.MASTERID) G ON A.MASTERID = G.MASTERID '
      || 'WHERE B.PKID = ' || TO_CHAR(A.SEGMENTATION_ID)
      || ' AND A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(v_currdate, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') '
      || 'AND B.SEGMENT_TYPE = ''PORTFOLIO'' AND A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A'' '
      || 'AND A.IAS_CLASS = ''A'' AND NVL(A.IFRS9_CLASS, '' '') <> ''FVTPL'' '
      || 'AND (C.BUCKET_GROUP IS NOT NULL) ' --AND A.IS_IMPAIRED = 1 
      || 'AND NVL(A.IMPAIRED_FLAG,''C'') = ''C'''
    AS QRY
  FROM IFRS_EIL_MODEL A
  WHERE A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = v_currdate
    AND A.EIL_MODEL_ID = v_eil_model_id;

  COMMIT; 

	  V_STR_SQL := '(' ||
	    'DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, GROUP_SEGMENT, SEGMENT, SUB_SEGMENT, SEGMENTATION_ID, ' ||
			'ACCOUNT_NUMBER, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, LT_RULE_ID, DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, DAY_PAST_DUE, RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, DATA_SOURCE, PRODUCT_CODE, PRODUCT_TYPE, ' ||
			'PRODUCT_GROUP, IS_IMPAIRED, IFRS9_CLASS, PD_SEGMENT, LGD_SEGMENT, EAD_SEGMENT, BUCKET_GROUP, BUCKET_ID, ' ||
			'STAGE, REVOLVING_FLAG, EIR, OUTSTANDING, UNAMORT_COST_AMT, UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, PLAFOND, ' ||
			'EIL_MODEL_ID, EAD_RULE_ID, EAD_TYPE, LGD_RULE_ID, LGD_ME_MODEL_ID, ' ||
			'PD_RULE_ID, PD_ME_MODEL_ID, CURRENCY, CREATEDBY, IMPAIRED_FLAG, CUSTOMER_NAME, ACCOUNT_STATUS, ' ||
			' EIL_AMOUNT, RATING_CODE, EXCHANGE_RATE, LOAN_START_DATE, LOAN_DUE_DATE, ' ||
			'FLAG_VAS, BI_COLLECTABILITY, LIFETIME, EAD_BALANCE, EAD_MARGIN,EAD_BALANCE_ADDITIONAL,EAD_BALANCE_INTEREST_ADDITIONAL,MARGIN_ACCRUED )';
	
	  FOR r IN (SELECT rn, qry FROM TMP_QRY ORDER BY rn) LOOP
		  
		V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO ' || V_IFRS_EIL_IMA || ' ' || V_STR_SQL || ' ' || r.qry;

		DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	
	    DELETE FROM TMP_QRY WHERE rn = r.rn;
	  END LOOP;
		
	  COMMIT;

    -----------------------------
    -- Log & insert final data
    -----------------------------
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_IMA;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_IMA ||
                ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')';

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;

EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN SP_IFRS_EIL_GENERATE_IMA: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EIL_MODEL (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0', 
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'X'
)
IS
    v_currdate    	DATE;
    v_EIL_model_id 	NUMBER := 0;
    v_script      	CLOB;
    v_tmp1        	VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_COUNT         NUMBER;
   
   -- LOG / RESULT
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_EIL_MODEL';
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_QUERYS        VARCHAR2(8000);
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
BEGIN
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- Set tanggal
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF p_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO v_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        v_currdate := p_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- Ambil EIL Model ID
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    SELECT pkid
    INTO   v_EIL_model_id
    FROM   IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER
    WHERE  is_eom = 1 AND IS_DELETE = 0 
    FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY;
   
    
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- Nama tabel target
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
   IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN 

        v_tmp1 := 'IFRS_EIL_MODEL_' || p_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE 

        v_tmp1 := 'IFRS_EIL_MODEL'; 
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(v_currdate, 'SP_IFRS_EIL_MODEL', p_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- Build dynamic SQL
    ------------------------------------------------------------------

	IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(v_tmp1); 
        
		IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN 
		 v_script := '';
         v_script := v_script || 'DROP TABLE ' || v_tmp1 || ' ';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (v_script);
		END IF;

        v_script := '';
        v_script := v_script || 'CREATE TABLE ' || v_tmp1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM IFRS_EIL_MODEL WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (v_script);
        
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
	
	--v_script := 'TRUNCATE TABLE PSAK413.' || v_tmp1 || '';

    v_script := 'DELETE FROM ' || v_tmp1 || ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(v_currdate,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND EIL_MODEL_ID =  ' ||v_EIL_model_id  ;
     
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_script;
	COMMIT;

    v_script := 'INSERT INTO PSAK413.' || v_tmp1 || '
	(DOWNLOAD_DATE,
		EIL_MODEL_ID,
		EAD_RULE_ID,
		SUB_SEGMENT_EAD,
		SEGMENTATION_ID,
		LGD_RULE_ID,
		LGD_ME_MODEL_ID,
		SUB_SEGMENT_LGD,
		LGD_DATE,
		LGD_OVERRIDE_FLAG,
		PD_RULE_ID,
		PD_ME_MODEL_ID,
		SUB_SEGMENT_PD,
		PD_DATE,
		BUCKET_GROUP,
		EAD_BALANCE,
		EAD_BALANCE_INTEREST,
		LT_RULE_ID,
		LT_EFF_DATE,
		LT_OVERRIDE_FLAG,
		FLAG_VAS,
		MODEL_TYPE, 
		EAD_BALANCE_ADDITIONAL,
		EAD_BALANCE_INTEREST_ADDITIONAL,
		CREATEDBY, CREATEDDATE)
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(v_currdate,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') AS DOWNLOAD_DATE,
		A.PKID AS EIL_MODEL_ID,
		C.PKID AS EAD_RULE_ID,
		I.SEGMENT_NAME_LV3 AS SUB_SEGMENT_EAD,
		b.SEGMENTATION_ID AS SEGMENTATION_ID,
		D.LGD_RULE_ID AS LGD_RULE_ID,
		D.LGD_MODEL_ID AS LGD_ME_MODEL_ID,
		J.SEGMENT_NAME_LV3 AS SUB_SEGMENT_LGD,
		CASE WHEN D.EFF_DATE_OPTION = ''Current Month'' THEN TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(v_currdate,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
			WHEN D.EFF_DATE_OPTION = ''Previous Month'' THEN TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(v_currdate,-1)),'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
			WHEN D.EFF_DATE_OPTION = ''Last Year'' THEN TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(v_currdate,-12)),'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
			WHEN D.EFF_DATE_OPTION = ''Selected Date'' THEN D.EFF_DATE END AS LGD_DATE,
		D.IS_OVERRIDE AS LGD_OVERRIDE_FLAG,
		E.PD_RULE_ID AS PD_RULE_ID,
		E.PD_MODEL_ID AS PD_ME_MODEL_ID,
		K.SEGMENT_NAME_LV3 AS SUB_SEGMENT_PD,
		CASE WHEN E.EFF_DATE_OPTION = ''Current Month'' THEN TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(v_currdate,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
			WHEN E.EFF_DATE_OPTION = ''Previous Month'' THEN TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(v_currdate,-1)),'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
			WHEN E.EFF_DATE_OPTION = ''Last Year'' THEN TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(v_currdate,-12)),'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
			WHEN E.EFF_DATE_OPTION = ''Selected Date'' THEN E.EFF_DATE END AS PD_DATE ,
		H.BUCKET_GROUP AS BUCKET_GROUP,
		C.EAD_BALANCE AS EAD_BALANCE,
		CASE WHEN L.SEGMENT_NAME_LV2 LIKE ''%INVESTASI%'' THEN ''CASE WHEN BI_COLLECTABILITY IN (1,2) THEN MARGIN_PAST_DUE ELSE 0 END '' ELSE ''0'' END AS EAD_BALANCE_INTEREST,
		C.LIFETIME_RULE_ID AS LT_RULE_ID,
		B.LIFETIME_DATE AS LT_EFF_DATE,
		B.IS_OVERRIDE_LIFETIME AS LT_OVERRIDE_FLAG,
		CASE WHEN H.PD_METHOD = ''VAS'' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS FLAG_VAS,
		CASE WHEN D.LGD_RULE_ID = 0 AND E.PD_RULE_ID = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS MODEL_TYPE,
		''0'' || CASE WHEN C.UNAMORTIZED_FEE_COST_FLAG = 1 THEN '' + NVL(UNAMORT_COST_AMT,0) + NVL(UNAMORT_FEE_AMT,0) + NVL(UNAMORT_OTHERS,0) '' ELSE '''' END || 
		CASE WHEN C.MARGIN_ACCRUED_FLAG = 1 THEN '' + CASE WHEN BI_COLLECTABILITY IN(1,2) THEN NVL(MARGIN_ACCRUED,0) ELSE 0 END '' ELSE '''' END AS EAD_BALANCE_ADDITIONAL,
		''0'' AS EAD_BALANCE_INTEREST_ADDITIONAL,
		''SP_IFRS_EIL_MODEL'' AS CREATEDBY,
		SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE
	 FROM IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER A
	  JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_EAD B ON A.PKID = B.EIL_MODEL_ID
	   JOIN IFRS_EAD_RULES_CONFIG C ON B.EAD_RULE_ID = C.PKID
	  JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_LGD D ON A.PKID = D.EIL_MODEL_ID
	   AND B.SEGMENTATION_ID = D.SEGMENTATION_ID
	  JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_PD E ON A.PKID = E.EIL_MODEL_ID
	   AND B.SEGMENTATION_ID = E.SEGMENTATION_ID
	  JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_PF F ON A.PKID = F.EIL_MODEL_ID
	   AND B.SEGMENTATION_ID = F.SEGMENTATION_ID
	    JOIN IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG G ON D.LGD_RULE_ID = G.PKID
	    JOIN IFRS_PD_RULES_CONFIG H ON E.PD_RULE_ID  = H.PKID
	    JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING I ON C.SEGMENTATION_ID = I.PKID  
	    JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING J ON G.SEGMENTATION_ID = J.PKID
	    JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING K ON H.SEGMENTATION_ID = K.PKID 
		JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING L ON F.SEGMENTATION_ID = L.PKID 
	  WHERE A.PKID = ' || v_EIL_model_id || '' ;
	 
	--DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(v_script);
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_script;
	COMMIT;

	v_script := 'UPDATE PSAK413.' || v_tmp1 || ' A 
		SET LGD = (SELECT LGD FROM IFRS_LGD_RESULT X WHERE A.LGD_DATE = X.EFF_DATE AND A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.LGD_RULE_ID)
		, LIFETIME = (SELECt LIFETIME fROM IFRS_LIFETIME_HEADER Y WHERE A.LT_EFF_DATE = Y.EFF_DATE AND A.LT_RULE_ID = Y.LIFETIME_RULE_ID ) 
		WHERE A.EIL_MODEL_ID = ' || v_EIL_model_id || '
		AND A.DOWNLOAD_DATE =  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(v_currdate,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') '; 
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_script;
	COMMIT;
	

	-----------------------------
    -- Log & insert final data
    -----------------------------
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || v_tmp1;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(v_currdate, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || v_tmp1 ||
                ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(v_currdate,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')' || '';

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(v_currdate, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), p_RUNID);
    COMMIT;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413."SP_IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_EAD" 
AS 
    
BEGIN

	--====>> EilEadModel <<=======
     MERGE INTO IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_EAD a
	    USING (
	    
		    selecT A."pkid",
		       B.PKID AS EIL_MODEL_ID ,C.PKID AS SEGMENTATION_ID,
		       D.PKID AS EAD_RULE_ID,A."lifetime_date" ,A."is_override_lifetime", A."is_deleted", A."lifetime_effective_date"
		   from "EilEadModel"@DBCONFIGLINK A
			 INNER JOIN "Segmentation"@DBCONFIGLINK seg ON A."code_segmentation" = seg."syscode_segmentation"
			 INNER JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING C on CASE WHEN seg."level" = 1 THEN C.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV1 
			    											 WHEN seg."level" = 2 THEN C.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV2 
			    											 WHEN seg."level" = 3 THEN C.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV3 END = A."code_segmentation"
			 INNER JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER B on A."syscode_eil_configuration" = B.SYSCODE_EIL
			 INNER JOIN IFRS_EAD_RULES_CONFIG D on A."code_ead_configuration" = D.SYSCODE_EAD
			    
	    ) b
	    ON ( a.EIL_MODEL_ID = b.EIL_MODEL_ID AND A.SEGMENTATION_ID = B.SEGMENTATION_ID )  
	    WHEN MATCHED THEN
	        UPDATE SET  
	        	a.IS_OVERRIDE_LIFETIME	 = b."is_override_lifetime",
	            a.UPDATEDBY              = 'SP_IFRS_EIL_CONFIG_MAPPING_1',
	            a.UPDATEDDATE            = sysdate,
	            a.IS_DELETE              = b."is_deleted" 
	 
	    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
	        INSERT (
	            EIL_MODEL_ID, SEGMENTATION_ID,
	            EAD_RULE_ID,LIFETIME_DATE,LIFETIME_EFF_DATE_OPTION,IS_OVERRIDE_LIFETIME, IS_DELETE,  
	            UPDATEDBY, UPDATEDDATE
	        )
	        VALUES (
	            b.EIL_MODEL_ID, b.SEGMENTATION_ID,
	            b.EAD_RULE_ID,b."lifetime_date" ,B."lifetime_effective_date",nvl(b."is_override_lifetime",0),nvl(b."is_deleted",0), 'SP_IFRS_EIL_CONFIG_MAPPING_1', sysdate 
	        );
	        
	        commit;
       
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413."SP_IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_LGD" 
AS 
    
BEGIN
    
	     --====>> EilLgdModel <<=======
     MERGE INTO IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_LGD a
	    USING (
	    
		    selecT A."pkid",
		       B.PKID AS EIL_MODEL_ID ,C.PKID AS SEGMENTATION_ID,
		       D.PKID AS LGD_RULE_ID,A."lgd_date", A."effective_date",A."is_override_lgd", A."is_deleted"
		    from "EilLgdModel"@DBCONFIGLINK A
		    INNER JOIN "Segmentation"@DBCONFIGLINK seg ON A."code_segmentation" = seg."syscode_segmentation"
			INNER JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING C on CASE WHEN seg."level" = 1 THEN C.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV1 
			    											 WHEN seg."level" = 2 THEN C.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV2 
			    											 WHEN seg."level" = 3 THEN C.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV3 END = A."code_segmentation"
			INNER JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER B on A."syscode_eil_configuration" = B.SYSCODE_EIL
		    INNER JOIN IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG D on A."code_lgd_configuration" = D.SYSCODE_LGD
	    ) b
	    ON ( a.EIL_MODEL_ID = b.EIL_MODEL_ID AND A.SEGMENTATION_ID = B.SEGMENTATION_ID )  
	     
	    WHEN MATCHED THEN
	        UPDATE SET  
	        	a.IS_OVERRIDE			 = b."is_override_lgd",
	            a.UPDATEDBY              = 'SP_IFRS_EIL_CONFIG_MAPPING_2',
	            a.UPDATEDDATE            = sysdate,
	            a.IS_DELETE              = b."is_deleted"
	 
	    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
	        INSERT (
	            EIL_MODEL_ID, SEGMENTATION_ID,
	            LGD_RULE_ID,EFF_DATE ,EFF_DATE_OPTION,IS_OVERRIDE, IS_DELETE,  
	            UPDATEDBY, UPDATEDDATE
	        )
	        VALUES (
	            b.EIL_MODEL_ID, b.SEGMENTATION_ID,
	            b.LGD_RULE_ID,b."lgd_date", b."effective_date",b."is_override_lgd",nvl(b."is_deleted",0), 'SP_IFRS_EIL_CONFIG_MAPPING_2', sysdate 
	        );
	        
	        commit;
	     
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413."SP_IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_PD" 
AS 
    
BEGIN
    
	         --====>> EilPdModel <<=======
     MERGE INTO IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_PD a
	    USING (
			selecT A."pkid",
				       B.PKID AS EIL_MODEL_ID ,C.PKID AS SEGMENTATION_ID,
