				       D.PKID AS PD_RULE_ID,NVL(A."workflow_header_draft_pkid",0) AS PD_MODEL_ID, A."effective_date",A."pd_date",A."is_override_pd", A."is_deleted"
				    from "EilPdModel"@DBCONFIGLINK A
				    INNER JOIN "Segmentation"@DBCONFIGLINK seg ON A."code_segmentation" = seg."syscode_segmentation"
					INNER JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING C on CASE WHEN seg."level" = 1 THEN C.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV1 
					    											 WHEN seg."level" = 2 THEN C.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV2 
					    											 WHEN seg."level" = 3 THEN C.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV3 END = A."code_segmentation"
					INNER JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER B on A."syscode_eil_configuration" = B.SYSCODE_EIL
				    INNER JOIN IFRS_PD_RULES_CONFIG D on A."code_pd_configuration" = D.SYSCODE_PD
	    ) b
	    ON ( a.EIL_MODEL_ID = b.EIL_MODEL_ID AND A.SEGMENTATION_ID = B.SEGMENTATION_ID)  
	     
	    WHEN MATCHED THEN
	        UPDATE SET  
	        	a.IS_OVERRIDE			 = b."is_override_pd",
	            a.UPDATEDBY              = 'SP_IFRS_EIL_CONFIG_MAPPING_3',
	            a.UPDATEDDATE            = sysdate,
	            a.IS_DELETE              = b."is_deleted",
	            a.PD_MODEL_ID			 = b.PD_MODEL_ID
	 
	    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
	        INSERT (
	            EIL_MODEL_ID, SEGMENTATION_ID,
	            PD_RULE_ID,PD_MODEL_ID,EFF_DATE_OPTION,EFF_DATE ,IS_OVERRIDE,IS_DELETE,  
	            UPDATEDBY, UPDATEDDATE
	        )
	        VALUES (
	            b.EIL_MODEL_ID, b.SEGMENTATION_ID,
	            b.PD_RULE_ID,b.PD_MODEL_ID,b."effective_date",b."pd_date",b."is_override_pd",nvl(b."is_deleted",0), 'SP_IFRS_EIL_CONFIG_MAPPING_3', sysdate 
	        );
	        
	        commit;
	     
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413."SP_IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_PF" 
AS 
    
BEGIN
    
	          --====>> EilPortfolio <<=======
     MERGE INTO IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_PF a
	    USING (
	    
		    selecT A."pkid",
			       B.PKID AS EIL_MODEL_ID ,C.PKID AS SEGMENTATION_ID,
			       D.PKID AS LT_RULE_ID, A."is_deleted"
			    from "EilPortfolio"@DBCONFIGLINK A
			    INNER JOIN "Segmentation"@DBCONFIGLINK seg ON A."code_segmentation" = seg."syscode_segmentation"
			    INNER JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING C on CASE WHEN seg."level" = 1 THEN C.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV1 
			    											 WHEN seg."level" = 2 THEN C.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV2 
			    											 WHEN seg."level" = 3 THEN C.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV3 END = A."code_segmentation"
			    INNER JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER B on A."syscode_eil_configuration" = B.SYSCODE_EIL
			    LEFT  JOIN IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG D on C.PKID  = D.SEGMENTATION_ID
			    
		    ) b
		    ON ( a.EIL_MODEL_ID = b.EIL_MODEL_ID AND A.SEGMENTATION_ID = B.SEGMENTATION_ID) 
		    WHEN MATCHED THEN
		        UPDATE SET  
		            a.UPDATEDBY              = 'SP_IFRS_EIL_CONFIG_MAPPING_4',
		            a.UPDATEDDATE            = sysdate,
		            a.IS_DELETE              = b."is_deleted"
		    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
		        INSERT (
		            EIL_MODEL_ID, SEGMENTATION_ID,
		            LT_RULE_ID, IS_DELETE,
		            UPDATEDBY, UPDATEDDATE
		        )
		        VALUES (
		            b.EIL_MODEL_ID, b.SEGMENTATION_ID,
		            b.LT_RULE_ID,b."is_deleted", 'SP_IFRS_EIL_CONFIG_MAPPING_4', sysdate 
	        );
	        
	        commit;
	     
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413."SP_IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER" 
AS 
    
BEGIN
    
	--EilConfiguration	-- HEADER
    MERGE INTO IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER a
    USING (
    
    SELECT * FROM (
	    selecT "pkid",
	        "syscode_eil_configuration", "eil_configuration_name",
	        "effective_start_date","description", "is_active",
	        "is_eom", "is_deleted",ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY "syscode_eil_configuration" ORDER BY "pkid" DESC ) rn 
	    from "EilConfiguration"@DBCONFIGLINK ) x 
    where x.rn = 1
    ) b
    ON ( a.SYSCODE_EIL = b."syscode_eil_configuration" )  
     
    WHEN MATCHED THEN
        UPDATE SET  
            a.DATA_DATE    			  = b."effective_start_date",
            a.ACTIVE_STATUS			  = b."is_active",
            a.RUN_STATUS			  = b."is_eom",
            a.UPDATEDBY              = 'SP_IFRS_EIL_CONFIG_MAPPING',
            a.UPDATEDDATE            = sysdate,
            a.IS_DELETE              = b."is_deleted",
            A.IS_EOM = B."is_eom"
 
    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
        INSERT (
            SYSCODE_EIL, EIL_MODEL_NAME,
            DATA_DATE, ACTIVE_STATUS, is_eom,
            IS_DELETE, CREATEDBY,  
            UPDATEDBY, UPDATEDDATE
        )
        VALUES (
            b."syscode_eil_configuration", b."eil_configuration_name",
            b."effective_start_date",b."is_active",nvl(b."is_eom",0) ,nvl(b."is_deleted",0), 'SP_IFRS_EIL_CONFIG_MAPPING', sysdate , sysdate
        );
        
        commit;
       
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EIL_MODEL_SCENARIO (
	p_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    p_download_date IN DATE,
    p_model_id      IN NUMBER DEFAULT 0,
    p_prc           IN CHAR   DEFAULT 'M'
)
IS
    v_currdate    	DATE;
    v_ecl_model_id 	NUMBER := 0;
    v_script      	CLOB;
    v_tmp1        	VARCHAR2(100);
BEGIN
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- Set tanggal
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF p_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO v_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        v_currdate := p_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- Ambil ECL Model ID
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    SELECT pkid
    INTO   v_ecl_model_id
    FROM   IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER
    WHERE  (pkid = p_model_id OR p_model_id = 0) AND (active_status = 1)
    FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY;
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- Nama tabel target
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    v_tmp1 := 'IFRS_EIL_MODEL_SCENARIO';
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- Build dynamic SQL
    ------------------------------------------------------------------
    v_script := 'TRUNCATE TABLE ' || v_tmp1;

    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_script;

    v_script := 'INSERT INTO ' || v_tmp1 || '
        (DOWNLOAD_DATE, EIL_MODEL_ID, SEGMENTATION_ID, SCENARIO_NO,
         PROB, PRC, CREATEDBY, CREATEDDATE, CREATEDHOST)
    SELECT DISTINCT
        DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(v_currdate, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' AS DOWNLOAD_DATE,
        A.PKID AS ECL_MODEL_ID,
        B.SEGMENTATION_ID,
        G.SCENARIO_NO,
        NVL(G.PROB, 0),
        ''' || p_prc || ''' AS PRC,
        ''SP_IFRS_ECL_MODEL_SCENARIO'' AS CREATEDBY,
        SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE,
        '''' AS CREATEDHOST
    FROM IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER A
    JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_EAD B
        ON A.PKID = B.ECL_MODEL_ID
    JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL_DETAIL_PF F
        ON A.PKID = F.ECL_MODEL_ID
       AND B.SEGMENTATION_ID = F.SEGMENTATION_ID
    CROSS JOIN (
        SELECT 0 AS SCENARIO_NO, CAST(1 AS NUMBER) AS PROB FROM DUAL
        UNION ALL
        SELECT 1, CAST(F.SCENARIO_1_PROB_OUTCOME / 100 AS NUMBER) FROM DUAL
        UNION ALL
        SELECT 2, CAST(F.SCENARIO_2_PROB_OUTCOME / 100 AS NUMBER) FROM DUAL
        UNION ALL
        SELECT 3, CAST(F.SCENARIO_3_PROB_OUTCOME / 100 AS NUMBER) FROM DUAL
        UNION ALL
        SELECT 4, CAST(F.SCENARIO_4_PROB_OUTCOME / 100 AS NUMBER) FROM DUAL
        UNION ALL
        SELECT 5, CAST(F.SCENARIO_5_PROB_OUTCOME / 100 AS NUMBER) FROM DUAL
    ) G
    WHERE ((' || p_model_id || ' = 0 AND A.ACTIVE_STATUS = 1)
           OR A.PKID = ' || p_model_id || ')
    ';

    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_script;
	COMMIT;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL (
    P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS 
    V_CURRDATE       DATE;
    V_DATADATE       VARCHAR2(20);
    V_TABLE_NAME     VARCHAR2(50);
    V_COUNT          NUMBER;
	V_MODEL_ID       NUMBER;
	v_EIL_model_id	 NUMBER;

-- DYNAMIC NAMES / QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY      CLOB;

    -- TABLE NAMES
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT 		VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_IFRS_EIL_IMA					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL				VARCHAR2(100);

    -- LOG / RESULT
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL';
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_QUERYS        VARCHAR2(8000);
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
    
    V_STR_SQL        CLOB;
    V_STR_SQL_RULE   CLOB;
    V_RULE_ID        VARCHAR2(250);
    V_ID             NUMBER := 0;
    V_MAX_ID         NUMBER := 0;
    V_SEQUENCE       VARCHAR2(50);
    
BEGIN
	-- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := 0;
   
   	SELECT pkid
    INTO   v_EIL_model_id
    FROM   IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER
    WHERE  SYSCODE_EIL = P_SYSCODE OR (P_SYSCODE = '0' AND is_eom = 1)
    	AND IS_DELETE = 0 
    FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY;

    -- CHOOSE TABLE NAMES BASED ON MODE
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL		:= 'IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 				:= 'GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL';
    ELSE
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 				:= 'GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL';
    	V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL		:= 'IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL';
    END IF;

    BEGIN
        SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, P_RUNID, 0, SYSTIMESTAMP);
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('WARNING: SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG FAILED: ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
    COMMIT;

    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        
        -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS (OWNED BY CURRENT SCHEMA)
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM USER_TABLES
        WHERE TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL || ' AS SELECT * FROM IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        
    ELSE
    	    
	   	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'DELETE FROM ' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL || ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ' ;
   
    END IF;
   
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL' ; 
    COMMIT;
   
    V_STR_QUERY := '
	INSERT INTO GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL (EFF_DATE,SEGMENTATION_ID,PD_RULE_ID,MODEL_ID,FL_SEQ,FL_YEAR,FL_MONTH,BUCKET_ID,PD,PD_DATE,LGD,LGD_DATE)
	SELECT A.EFF_DATE, B.SEGMENTATION_ID ,A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID , A.FL_SEQ , A.FL_YEAR, A.FL_MONTH, A.BUCKET_ID , A.PD,B.PD_DATE, B.LGD, B.LGD_DATE  
	FROM IFRS_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE  A 
		JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL B ON A.EFF_DATE = B.PD_DATE AND A.PD_RULE_ID = B.PD_RULE_ID AND A.MODEL_ID = B.PD_ME_MODEL_ID 
		WHERE A.PD > 0 AND B.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ';
	
	--DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
		COMMIT;
	
	V_STR_QUERY := '
		INSERT INTO IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL ( DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, GROUP_SEGMENT, SEGMENT, SUB_SEGMENT, RATING_CODE, DAY_PAST_DUE, BI_COLLECTABILITY,
			 ACCOUNT_NUMBER, ACCOUNT_STATUS, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, CUSTOMER_NAME, EXCHANGE_RATE, IMPAIRED_FLAG, OUTSTANDING, BUCKET_ID, REVOLVING_FLAG, PRODUCT_CODE,
			 PRODUCT_TYPE, PLAFOND, LOAN_START_DATE, DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, EIR, LOAN_DUE_DATE, MARGIN_PAST_DUE, SEGMENTATION_ID, LT_RULE_ID, CUSTOMER_GRADE,
			 PRODUCT_ENTITY, DATA_SOURCE, PRODUCT_GROUP, IS_IMPAIRED, IFRS9_CLASS, PD_SEGMENT, LGD_SEGMENT, EAD_SEGMENT, BUCKET_GROUP, LIFETIME, STAGE, UNAMORT_COST_AMT,
			 UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, MARGIN_ACCRUED, FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, EAD_BALANCE, EAD_MARGIN, EIL_MODEL_ID, EAD_RULE_ID, LGD_RULE_ID, LGD_ME_MODEL_ID,
			 PD_RULE_ID, PD_ME_MODEL_ID, CURRENCY, EIL_AMOUNT, EIL_PRINCIPAL, EIL_MARGIN, FLAG_VAS, UNUSED_AMOUNT, EAD_TYPE, SEQ, EAD_PRINCIPAL,FL_YEAR,FL_MONTH,PD,LGD, CREATEDBY, CREATEDDATE)
		SELECT X.DOWNLOAD_DATE, X.MASTERID, X.GROUP_SEGMENT, X.SEGMENT, X.SUB_SEGMENT, X.RATING_CODE, X.DAY_PAST_DUE, X.BI_COLLECTABILITY,
			 X.ACCOUNT_NUMBER, X.ACCOUNT_STATUS, X.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, X.CUSTOMER_NAME, X.EXCHANGE_RATE, X.IMPAIRED_FLAG, X.OUTSTANDING, X.BUCKET_ID, X.REVOLVING_FLAG, X.PRODUCT_CODE,
			 X.PRODUCT_TYPE, X.PLAFOND, X.LOAN_START_DATE, X.DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, X.RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, X.EIR, X.LOAN_DUE_DATE, X.MARGIN_PAST_DUE, X.SEGMENTATION_ID, X.LT_RULE_ID, X.CUSTOMER_GRADE,
			 X.PRODUCT_ENTITY, X.DATA_SOURCE, X.PRODUCT_GROUP, X.IS_IMPAIRED, X.IFRS9_CLASS, X.PD_SEGMENT, X.LGD_SEGMENT, X.EAD_SEGMENT, X.BUCKET_GROUP, X.LIFETIME, X.STAGE, X.UNAMORT_COST_AMT,
			 X.UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, X.MARGIN_ACCRUED, X.FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, X.EAD_BALANCE, X.EAD_MARGIN, X.EIL_MODEL_ID, X.EAD_RULE_ID, X.LGD_RULE_ID, X.LGD_ME_MODEL_ID,
			 X.PD_RULE_ID, X.PD_ME_MODEL_ID, X.CURRENCY,
			 ((X.EAD_PRINCIPAL + X.EAD_MARGIN) * Y.PD * Y.LGD ) AS EIL_AMOUNT, 
			 ((X.EAD_PRINCIPAL ) * Y.PD * Y.LGD ) AS EIL_PRINCIPAL, 
			 ((X.EAD_MARGIN) * Y.PD * Y.LGD ) AS EIL_MARGIN, 
			 X.FLAG_VAS, X.UNUSED_AMOUNT, X.EAD_TYPE, X.SEQ, X.EAD_PRINCIPAL,Y.FL_YEAR,Y.FL_MONTH,Y.PD,Y.LGD, ''SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL'', SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE
		FROM IFRS_EAD_RESULT X
			INNER JOIN GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL Y
			ON  X.SEGMENTATION_ID = Y.SEGMENTATION_ID
			AND X.BUCKET_ID = Y.BUCKET_ID
			AND X.SEQ = Y.FL_SEQ 
		WHERE X.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ';
	
		--DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);			
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
		COMMIT;
        -----------------------------
	    -- Log & insert final data
	    -----------------------------
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL ||
                ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')' ;

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;

EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL3 (
    P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS 
    V_CURRDATE       DATE;
    V_DATADATE       VARCHAR2(20);
    V_TABLE_NAME     VARCHAR2(50);
    V_COUNT          NUMBER;
	V_MODEL_ID       NUMBER;
	v_EIL_model_id	 NUMBER;

-- DYNAMIC NAMES / QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY      CLOB;

    -- TABLE NAMES
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT 		VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_IFRS_EIL_IMA					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL				VARCHAR2(100);

    -- LOG / RESULT
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL';
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_QUERYS        VARCHAR2(8000);
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
    
    V_STR_SQL        CLOB;
    V_STR_SQL_RULE   CLOB;
    V_RULE_ID        VARCHAR2(250);
    V_ID             NUMBER := 0;
    V_MAX_ID         NUMBER := 0;
    V_SEQUENCE       VARCHAR2(50);
    
BEGIN
	-- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := 0;
   
   	SELECT pkid
    INTO   v_EIL_model_id
    FROM   IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER
    WHERE  SYSCODE_EIL = P_SYSCODE OR (P_SYSCODE = '0' AND is_eom = 1)
    	AND IS_DELETE = 0 
    FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY;

    -- CHOOSE TABLE NAMES BASED ON MODE
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL		:= 'IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 				:= 'GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL';
    ELSE
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 				:= 'GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL';
    	V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL		:= 'IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL';
    END IF;

    BEGIN
        SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, P_RUNID, 0, SYSTIMESTAMP);
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('WARNING: SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG FAILED: ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
    COMMIT;

    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        
        -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS (OWNED BY CURRENT SCHEMA)
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM USER_TABLES
        WHERE TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL || ' AS SELECT * FROM IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        
    ELSE
    	    
	   	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'DELETE FROM ' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL || ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ' ;
   
    END IF;
   
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL' ; 
    COMMIT;
   
    V_STR_QUERY := '
	INSERT INTO GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL (EFF_DATE,SEGMENTATION_ID,PD_RULE_ID,MODEL_ID,FL_SEQ,FL_YEAR,FL_MONTH,BUCKET_ID,PD,PD_DATE,LGD,LGD_DATE)
	SELECT A.EFF_DATE, B.SEGMENTATION_ID ,A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID , A.FL_SEQ , A.FL_YEAR, A.FL_MONTH, A.BUCKET_ID , A.PD,B.PD_DATE, B.LGD, B.LGD_DATE  
	FROM IFRS_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE  A 
		JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL B ON A.EFF_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE AND A.PD_RULE_ID = B.PD_RULE_ID AND (A.MODEL_ID =  B.PD_ME_MODEL_ID OR ( A.MODEL_ID = 0 AND B.PD_RULE_ID = B.PD_ME_MODEL_ID ))
		WHERE A.PD > 0 AND A.EFF_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ';
	
	--DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
		COMMIT;
	
	V_STR_QUERY := '
		INSERT INTO IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL ( DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, GROUP_SEGMENT, SEGMENT, SUB_SEGMENT, RATING_CODE, DAY_PAST_DUE, BI_COLLECTABILITY,
			 ACCOUNT_NUMBER, ACCOUNT_STATUS, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, CUSTOMER_NAME, EXCHANGE_RATE, IMPAIRED_FLAG, OUTSTANDING, BUCKET_ID, REVOLVING_FLAG, PRODUCT_CODE,
			 PRODUCT_TYPE, PLAFOND, LOAN_START_DATE, DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, EIR, LOAN_DUE_DATE, MARGIN_PAST_DUE, SEGMENTATION_ID, LT_RULE_ID, CUSTOMER_GRADE,
			 PRODUCT_ENTITY, DATA_SOURCE, PRODUCT_GROUP, IS_IMPAIRED, IFRS9_CLASS, PD_SEGMENT, LGD_SEGMENT, EAD_SEGMENT, BUCKET_GROUP, LIFETIME, STAGE, UNAMORT_COST_AMT,
			 UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, MARGIN_ACCRUED, FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, EAD_BALANCE, EAD_MARGIN, EIL_MODEL_ID, EAD_RULE_ID, LGD_RULE_ID, LGD_ME_MODEL_ID,
			 PD_RULE_ID, PD_ME_MODEL_ID, CURRENCY, EIL_AMOUNT, EIL_PRINCIPAL, EIL_MARGIN, FLAG_VAS, UNUSED_AMOUNT, EAD_TYPE, SEQ, EAD_PRINCIPAL,FL_YEAR,FL_MONTH,PD,LGD, CREATEDBY, CREATEDDATE)
		SELECT X.DOWNLOAD_DATE, X.MASTERID, X.GROUP_SEGMENT, X.SEGMENT, X.SUB_SEGMENT, X.RATING_CODE, X.DAY_PAST_DUE, X.BI_COLLECTABILITY,
			 X.ACCOUNT_NUMBER, X.ACCOUNT_STATUS, X.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, X.CUSTOMER_NAME, X.EXCHANGE_RATE, X.IMPAIRED_FLAG, X.OUTSTANDING, X.BUCKET_ID, X.REVOLVING_FLAG, X.PRODUCT_CODE,
			 X.PRODUCT_TYPE, X.PLAFOND, X.LOAN_START_DATE, X.DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, X.RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, X.EIR, X.LOAN_DUE_DATE, X.MARGIN_PAST_DUE, X.SEGMENTATION_ID, X.LT_RULE_ID, X.CUSTOMER_GRADE,
			 X.PRODUCT_ENTITY, X.DATA_SOURCE, X.PRODUCT_GROUP, X.IS_IMPAIRED, X.IFRS9_CLASS, X.PD_SEGMENT, X.LGD_SEGMENT, X.EAD_SEGMENT, X.BUCKET_GROUP, X.LIFETIME, X.STAGE, X.UNAMORT_COST_AMT,
			 X.UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, X.MARGIN_ACCRUED, X.FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, X.EAD_BALANCE, X.EAD_MARGIN, X.EIL_MODEL_ID, X.EAD_RULE_ID, X.LGD_RULE_ID, X.LGD_ME_MODEL_ID,
			 X.PD_RULE_ID, X.PD_ME_MODEL_ID, X.CURRENCY,
			 ((X.EAD_PRINCIPAL + X.EAD_MARGIN) * Y.PD * Y.LGD ) AS EIL_AMOUNT, 
			 ((X.EAD_PRINCIPAL ) * Y.PD * Y.LGD ) AS EIL_PRINCIPAL, 
			 ((X.EAD_MARGIN) * Y.PD * Y.LGD ) AS EIL_MARGIN, 
			 X.FLAG_VAS, X.UNUSED_AMOUNT, X.EAD_TYPE, X.SEQ, X.EAD_PRINCIPAL,Y.FL_YEAR,Y.FL_MONTH,Y.PD,Y.LGD, ''SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL'', SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE 
		FROM IFRS_EAD_RESULT X
			INNER JOIN GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL Y
			ON  X.SEGMENTATION_ID = Y.SEGMENTATION_ID
			AND X.BUCKET_ID = Y.BUCKET_ID
			AND X.SEQ = Y.FL_SEQ 
		WHERE X.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ';
	
		--DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);			
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
		COMMIT;
        -----------------------------
	    -- Log & insert final data
	    -----------------------------
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL ||
                ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')' ;

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;

EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAILX (
    P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS 
    V_CURRDATE       DATE;
    V_DATADATE       VARCHAR2(20);
    V_TABLE_NAME     VARCHAR2(50);
    V_COUNT          NUMBER;
	V_MODEL_ID       NUMBER;
	v_EIL_model_id	 NUMBER;

-- DYNAMIC NAMES / QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY      CLOB;

    -- TABLE NAMES
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT 		VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_IFRS_EIL_IMA					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL				VARCHAR2(100);

    -- LOG / RESULT
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL';
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_QUERYS        VARCHAR2(8000);
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
    
    V_STR_SQL        CLOB;
    V_STR_SQL_RULE   CLOB;
    V_RULE_ID        VARCHAR2(250);
    V_ID             NUMBER := 0;
    V_MAX_ID         NUMBER := 0;
    V_SEQUENCE       VARCHAR2(50);
    
BEGIN
	-- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := 0;
   
   	SELECT pkid
    INTO   v_EIL_model_id
    FROM   IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER
    WHERE  SYSCODE_EIL = P_SYSCODE OR (P_SYSCODE = '0' AND is_eom = 1)
    	AND IS_DELETE = 0 
    FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY;

    -- CHOOSE TABLE NAMES BASED ON MODE
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL		:= 'IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAILX_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 				:= 'GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL';
    ELSE
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 				:= 'GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL';
    	V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL		:= 'IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAILX';
    END IF;

    BEGIN
        SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, P_RUNID, 0, SYSTIMESTAMP);
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('WARNING: SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG FAILED: ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
    COMMIT;

    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        
        -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS (OWNED BY CURRENT SCHEMA)
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM USER_TABLES
        WHERE TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL || ' AS SELECT * FROM IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        
    ELSE
    	    
	   	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'DELETE FROM ' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL || ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ' ;
   
    END IF;
   
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL' ; 
    COMMIT;
   
    V_STR_QUERY := '
	INSERT INTO GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL (EFF_DATE,SEGMENTATION_ID,PD_RULE_ID,MODEL_ID,FL_SEQ,FL_YEAR,FL_MONTH,BUCKET_ID,PD,PD_DATE,LGD,LGD_DATE)
	SELECT A.EFF_DATE, B.SEGMENTATION_ID ,A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID , A.FL_SEQ , A.FL_YEAR, A.FL_MONTH, A.BUCKET_ID , A.PD,B.PD_DATE, B.LGD, B.LGD_DATE  
	FROM IFRS_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE  A 
		JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL B ON A.EFF_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE AND A.PD_RULE_ID = B.PD_RULE_ID AND A.MODEL_ID = B.PD_ME_MODEL_ID 
		WHERE A.PD > 0
		AND B.SEGMENTATION_ID = 13 
		 AND A.EFF_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ';
	
	--DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
		COMMIT;
	
	V_STR_QUERY := '
		INSERT INTO IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAILX ( DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, GROUP_SEGMENT, SEGMENT, SUB_SEGMENT, RATING_CODE, DAY_PAST_DUE, BI_COLLECTABILITY,
			 ACCOUNT_NUMBER, ACCOUNT_STATUS, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, CUSTOMER_NAME, EXCHANGE_RATE, IMPAIRED_FLAG, OUTSTANDING, BUCKET_ID, REVOLVING_FLAG, PRODUCT_CODE,
			 PRODUCT_TYPE, PLAFOND, LOAN_START_DATE, DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, EIR, LOAN_DUE_DATE, MARGIN_PAST_DUE, SEGMENTATION_ID, LT_RULE_ID, CUSTOMER_GRADE,
			 PRODUCT_ENTITY, DATA_SOURCE, PRODUCT_GROUP, IS_IMPAIRED, IFRS9_CLASS, PD_SEGMENT, LGD_SEGMENT, EAD_SEGMENT, BUCKET_GROUP, LIFETIME, STAGE, UNAMORT_COST_AMT,
			 UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, MARGIN_ACCRUED, FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, EAD_BALANCE, EAD_MARGIN, EIL_MODEL_ID, EAD_RULE_ID, LGD_RULE_ID, LGD_ME_MODEL_ID,
			 PD_RULE_ID, PD_ME_MODEL_ID, CURRENCY, EIL_AMOUNT, EIL_PRINCIPAL, EIL_MARGIN, FLAG_VAS, UNUSED_AMOUNT, EAD_TYPE, SEQ, EAD_PRINCIPAL,FL_YEAR,FL_MONTH,PD,LGD, CREATEDBY, CREATEDDATE)
		SELECT X.DOWNLOAD_DATE, X.MASTERID, X.GROUP_SEGMENT, X.SEGMENT, X.SUB_SEGMENT, X.RATING_CODE, X.DAY_PAST_DUE, X.BI_COLLECTABILITY,
			 X.ACCOUNT_NUMBER, X.ACCOUNT_STATUS, X.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, X.CUSTOMER_NAME, X.EXCHANGE_RATE, X.IMPAIRED_FLAG, X.OUTSTANDING, X.BUCKET_ID, X.REVOLVING_FLAG, X.PRODUCT_CODE,
			 X.PRODUCT_TYPE, X.PLAFOND, X.LOAN_START_DATE, X.DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, X.RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, X.EIR, X.LOAN_DUE_DATE, X.MARGIN_PAST_DUE, X.SEGMENTATION_ID, X.LT_RULE_ID, X.CUSTOMER_GRADE,
			 X.PRODUCT_ENTITY, X.DATA_SOURCE, X.PRODUCT_GROUP, X.IS_IMPAIRED, X.IFRS9_CLASS, X.PD_SEGMENT, X.LGD_SEGMENT, X.EAD_SEGMENT, X.BUCKET_GROUP, X.LIFETIME, X.STAGE, X.UNAMORT_COST_AMT,
			 X.UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, X.MARGIN_ACCRUED, X.FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, X.EAD_BALANCE, X.EAD_MARGIN, X.EIL_MODEL_ID, X.EAD_RULE_ID, X.LGD_RULE_ID, X.LGD_ME_MODEL_ID,
			 X.PD_RULE_ID, X.PD_ME_MODEL_ID, X.CURRENCY,
			 ((X.EAD_PRINCIPAL + X.EAD_MARGIN) * Y.PD * Y.LGD ) AS EIL_AMOUNT, 
			 ((X.EAD_PRINCIPAL ) * Y.PD * Y.LGD ) AS EIL_PRINCIPAL, 
			 ((X.EAD_MARGIN) * Y.PD * Y.LGD ) AS EIL_MARGIN, 
			 X.FLAG_VAS, X.UNUSED_AMOUNT, X.EAD_TYPE, X.SEQ, X.EAD_PRINCIPAL,Y.FL_YEAR,Y.FL_MONTH,Y.PD,Y.LGD, ''SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL'', SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE
		FROM IFRS_EAD_RESULT X
			INNER JOIN GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL Y
			ON  X.SEGMENTATION_ID = Y.SEGMENTATION_ID
			AND X.BUCKET_ID = Y.BUCKET_ID
			AND X.SEQ = Y.FL_SEQ 
		WHERE X.SEGMENTATION_ID = 13 AND X.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ';
	
		--DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);			
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
		COMMIT;
        -----------------------------
	    -- Log & insert final data
	    -----------------------------
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL ||
                ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')' ;

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;

EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL_2 (
    P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS 
    V_CURRDATE       DATE;
    V_DATADATE       VARCHAR2(20);
    V_TABLE_NAME     VARCHAR2(50);
    V_COUNT          NUMBER;
	V_MODEL_ID       NUMBER;
	v_EIL_model_id	 NUMBER;

-- DYNAMIC NAMES / QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY      CLOB;

    -- TABLE NAMES
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT 		VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_IFRS_EIL_IMA					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL		VARCHAR2(100);

    -- LOG / RESULT
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL';
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_QUERYS        VARCHAR2(8000);
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
    
    V_STR_SQL        CLOB;
    V_STR_SQL_RULE   CLOB;
    V_RULE_ID        VARCHAR2(250);
    V_ID             NUMBER := 0;
    V_MAX_ID         NUMBER := 0;
    V_SEQUENCE       VARCHAR2(50);
    
BEGIN
	-- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := 0;
   
   	SELECT pkid
    INTO   v_EIL_model_id
    FROM   IFRS_EIL_MODEL_HEADER
    WHERE  SYSCODE_EIL = P_SYSCODE OR (P_SYSCODE = '0' AND is_eom = 1)
    	AND IS_DELETE = 0 
    FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY;

    -- CHOOSE TABLE NAMES BASED ON MODE
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL		:= 'IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 				:= 'GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL';
    ELSE
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 				:= 'GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL';
    	V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL		:= 'IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL';
    END IF;

    BEGIN
        SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, P_RUNID, 0, SYSTIMESTAMP);
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('WARNING: SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG FAILED: ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
    COMMIT;

    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        
        -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS (OWNED BY CURRENT SCHEMA)
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM USER_TABLES
        WHERE TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL || ' AS SELECT * FROM IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        
    ELSE
    	    
	   	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'DELETE FROM ' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL || ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ' ;
   
    END IF;
   
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL' ; 
    COMMIT;
   
    V_STR_QUERY := '
	INSERT INTO GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL (EFF_DATE,SEGMENTATION_ID,PD_RULE_ID,MODEL_ID,FL_SEQ,FL_YEAR,FL_MONTH,BUCKET_ID,PD,PD_DATE,LGD,LGD_DATE)
	SELECT A.EFF_DATE, B.SEGMENTATION_ID ,A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID , A.FL_SEQ , A.FL_YEAR, A.FL_MONTH, A.BUCKET_ID , A.PD,B.PD_DATE, B.LGD, B.LGD_DATE  
	FROM IFRS_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE  A 
		JOIN IFRS_EIL_MODEL B ON A.EFF_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE AND A.PD_RULE_ID = B.PD_RULE_ID AND A.MODEL_ID = B.PD_ME_MODEL_ID 
		WHERE A.PD > 0 AND A.EFF_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ';
	
	--DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
		COMMIT;
	
	V_STR_QUERY := '
		INSERT INTO IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL ( DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, GROUP_SEGMENT, SEGMENT, SUB_SEGMENT, RATING_CODE, DAY_PAST_DUE, BI_COLLECTABILITY,
			 ACCOUNT_NUMBER, ACCOUNT_STATUS, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, CUSTOMER_NAME, EXCHANGE_RATE, IMPAIRED_FLAG, OUTSTANDING, BUCKET_ID, REVOLVING_FLAG, PRODUCT_CODE,
			 PRODUCT_TYPE, PLAFOND, LOAN_START_DATE, DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, EIR, LOAN_DUE_DATE, MARGIN_PAST_DUE, SEGMENTATION_ID, LT_RULE_ID, CUSTOMER_GRADE,
			 PRODUCT_ENTITY, DATA_SOURCE, PRODUCT_GROUP, IS_IMPAIRED, IFRS9_CLASS, PD_SEGMENT, LGD_SEGMENT, EAD_SEGMENT, BUCKET_GROUP, LIFETIME, STAGE, UNAMORT_COST_AMT,
			 UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, MARGIN_ACCRUED, FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, EAD_BALANCE, EAD_MARGIN, EIL_MODEL_ID, EAD_RULE_ID, LGD_RULE_ID, LGD_ME_MODEL_ID,
			 PD_RULE_ID, PD_ME_MODEL_ID, CURRENCY, EIL_AMOUNT, EIL_PRINCIPAL, EIL_MARGIN, FLAG_VAS, UNUSED_AMOUNT, EAD_TYPE, SEQ, EAD_PRINCIPAL,FL_YEAR,FL_MONTH,PD,LGD, CREATEDBY, CREATEDDATE)
		SELECT X.DOWNLOAD_DATE, X.MASTERID, X.GROUP_SEGMENT, X.SEGMENT, X.SUB_SEGMENT, X.RATING_CODE, X.DAY_PAST_DUE, X.BI_COLLECTABILITY,
			 X.ACCOUNT_NUMBER, X.ACCOUNT_STATUS, X.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, X.CUSTOMER_NAME, X.EXCHANGE_RATE, X.IMPAIRED_FLAG, X.OUTSTANDING, X.BUCKET_ID, X.REVOLVING_FLAG, X.PRODUCT_CODE,
			 X.PRODUCT_TYPE, X.PLAFOND, X.LOAN_START_DATE, X.DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, X.RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, X.EIR, X.LOAN_DUE_DATE, X.MARGIN_PAST_DUE, X.SEGMENTATION_ID, X.LT_RULE_ID, X.CUSTOMER_GRADE,
			 X.PRODUCT_ENTITY, X.DATA_SOURCE, X.PRODUCT_GROUP, X.IS_IMPAIRED, X.IFRS9_CLASS, X.PD_SEGMENT, X.LGD_SEGMENT, X.EAD_SEGMENT, X.BUCKET_GROUP, X.LIFETIME, X.STAGE, X.UNAMORT_COST_AMT,
			 X.UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, X.MARGIN_ACCRUED, X.FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, X.EAD_BALANCE, X.EAD_MARGIN, X.EIL_MODEL_ID, X.EAD_RULE_ID, X.LGD_RULE_ID, X.LGD_ME_MODEL_ID,
			 X.PD_RULE_ID, X.PD_ME_MODEL_ID, X.CURRENCY,
			 ((X.EAD_PRINCIPAL + X.EAD_MARGIN) * Y.PD * Y.LGD ) AS EIL_AMOUNT, 
			 ((X.EAD_PRINCIPAL ) * Y.PD * Y.LGD ) AS EIL_PRINCIPAL, 
			 ((X.EAD_MARGIN) * Y.PD * Y.LGD ) AS EIL_MARGIN, 
			 X.FLAG_VAS, X.UNUSED_AMOUNT, X.EAD_TYPE, X.SEQ, X.EAD_PRINCIPAL,Y.FL_YEAR,Y.FL_MONTH,Y.PD,Y.LGD, ''SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL'', SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE
		FROM IFRS_EAD_RESULT X
			INNER JOIN GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL Y
			ON  X.SEGMENTATION_ID = Y.SEGMENTATION_ID
			AND X.BUCKET_ID = Y.BUCKET_ID
			AND X.SEQ = Y.FL_SEQ 
		WHERE X.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ';
	
		--DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);			
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
		COMMIT;
        -----------------------------
	    -- Log & insert final data
	    -----------------------------
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL ||
                ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')' ;

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;

EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER (
    P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS 
    V_CURRDATE       DATE;
    V_DATADATE       VARCHAR2(20);
    V_TABLE_NAME     VARCHAR2(50);
    V_COUNT          NUMBER;
	V_MODEL_ID       NUMBER;

-- DYNAMIC NAMES / QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY      CLOB;

    -- TABLE NAMES
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT 		VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER		VARCHAR2(100);

    -- LOG / RESULT
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER';
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_QUERYS        VARCHAR2(8000);
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
    
    V_STR_SQL        CLOB;
    V_STR_SQL_RULE   CLOB;
    V_RULE_ID        VARCHAR2(250);
    V_ID             NUMBER := 0;
    V_MAX_ID         NUMBER := 0;
    V_SEQUENCE       VARCHAR2(50);
    
BEGIN
	-- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := 0;

    -- CHOOSE TABLE NAMES BASED ON MODE
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER		:= 'IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 				:= 'GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL';
    ELSE
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 				:= 'GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL';
    	V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER		:= 'IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER';
    END IF;

    BEGIN
        SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, P_RUNID, 0, SYSTIMESTAMP);
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('WARNING: SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG FAILED: ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
    COMMIT;

    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        
        -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS (OWNED BY CURRENT SCHEMA)
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM USER_TABLES
        WHERE TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER || ' AS SELECT * FROM IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        
    ELSE
    	    
	   	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'DELETE FROM ' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER || ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ' ;
   
    END IF;
   
	V_STR_QUERY := '
		INSERT INTO IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER ( 
			DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, GROUP_SEGMENT, SEGMENT, SUB_SEGMENT, 
			DAY_PAST_DUE, BI_COLLECTABILITY, ACCOUNT_NUMBER, ACCOUNT_STATUS,
			CUSTOMER_NUMBER, CUSTOMER_NAME, EXCHANGE_RATE, IMPAIRED_FLAG, OUTSTANDING, BUCKET_ID, REVOLVING_FLAG, PRODUCT_CODE,
			PRODUCT_TYPE,  LOAN_START_DATE, DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, EIR, LOAN_DUE_DATE, MARGIN_PAST_DUE,
			SEGMENTATION_ID, LT_RULE_ID,   DATA_SOURCE, PRODUCT_GROUP, IS_IMPAIRED,   PD_SEGMENT, LGD_SEGMENT,
			EAD_SEGMENT, BUCKET_GROUP, LIFETIME, STAGE, UNAMORT_COST_AMT, UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, MARGIN_ACCRUED, FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, EIL_MODEL_ID,
			EAD_RULE_ID, LGD_RULE_ID, LGD_ME_MODEL_ID, PD_RULE_ID, PD_ME_MODEL_ID, CURRENCY, EIL_AMOUNT,   PD,LGD, EIL_PRINCIPAL,EIL_MARGIN,EAD_AMOUNT,
			CREATEDBY, CREATEDDATE)
		SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, MAX(GROUP_SEGMENT), MAX(SEGMENT), MAX(SUB_SEGMENT), MAX(DAY_PAST_DUE), MAX(BI_COLLECTABILITY), MAX(ACCOUNT_NUMBER), MAX(ACCOUNT_STATUS),
			MAX(CUSTOMER_NUMBER), MAX(CUSTOMER_NAME), MAX(EXCHANGE_RATE), MAX(IMPAIRED_FLAG), MAX(OUTSTANDING), MAX(BUCKET_ID), MAX(REVOLVING_FLAG), MAX(PRODUCT_CODE), MAX(PRODUCT_TYPE),  
			MAX(LOAN_START_DATE), MAX(DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF), MAX(RESTRUCTURE_FLAG), MAX(EIR), MAX(LOAN_DUE_DATE), MAX(MARGIN_PAST_DUE), MAX(SEGMENTATION_ID), MAX(LT_RULE_ID),  
			MAX(DATA_SOURCE), MAX(PRODUCT_GROUP), MAX(IS_IMPAIRED), MAX(PD_SEGMENT), MAX(LGD_SEGMENT), MAX(EAD_SEGMENT), MAX(BUCKET_GROUP), MAX(LIFETIME), MAX(STAGE), MAX(UNAMORT_COST_AMT),
			MAX(UNAMORT_FEE_AMT), MAX(MARGIN_ACCRUED), MAX(FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT), MAX(EIL_MODEL_ID), MAX(EAD_RULE_ID), MAX(LGD_RULE_ID), MAX(LGD_ME_MODEL_ID), MAX(PD_RULE_ID), MAX(PD_ME_MODEL_ID), MAX(CURRENCY),
			SUM(EIL_AMOUNT), AVG(PD),AVG(LGD), SUM(EIL_PRINCIPAL), SUM(EIL_MARGIN) , MAX(CASE WHEN SEQ = 0 THEN EAD_PRINCIPAL + EAD_MARGIN  ELSE 0 END ) EAD,
			''IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER'' AS CREATEDBY,SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE
			FROM IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAIL 
			WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || '''
			GROUP BY DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID' ;
			 
	
		--DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);			
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
		COMMIT;
        -----------------------------
	    -- Log & insert final data
	    -----------------------------
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER ||
                ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')' ;

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;

EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADERX (
    P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS 
    V_CURRDATE       DATE;
    V_DATADATE       VARCHAR2(20);
    V_TABLE_NAME     VARCHAR2(50);
    V_COUNT          NUMBER;
	V_MODEL_ID       NUMBER;

-- DYNAMIC NAMES / QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY      CLOB;

    -- TABLE NAMES
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT 		VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER		VARCHAR2(100);

    -- LOG / RESULT
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER';
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_QUERYS        VARCHAR2(8000);
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
    
    V_STR_SQL        CLOB;
    V_STR_SQL_RULE   CLOB;
    V_RULE_ID        VARCHAR2(250);
    V_ID             NUMBER := 0;
    V_MAX_ID         NUMBER := 0;
    V_SEQUENCE       VARCHAR2(50);
    
BEGIN
	-- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := 0;

    -- CHOOSE TABLE NAMES BASED ON MODE
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER		:= 'IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADERX_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 				:= 'GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL';
    ELSE
    	V_TABLEPDCONFIG 				:= 'GTMP_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE_EIL';
    	V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER		:= 'IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADERX';
    END IF;

    BEGIN
        SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, P_RUNID, 0, SYSTIMESTAMP);
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('WARNING: SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG FAILED: ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
    COMMIT;

    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        
        -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS (OWNED BY CURRENT SCHEMA)
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM USER_TABLES
        WHERE TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER || ' AS SELECT * FROM IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        
    ELSE
    	    
	   	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'DELETE FROM ' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER || ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ' ;
   
    END IF;
   
	V_STR_QUERY := '
		INSERT INTO IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADERX ( 
			DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, GROUP_SEGMENT, SEGMENT, SUB_SEGMENT, 
			DAY_PAST_DUE, BI_COLLECTABILITY, ACCOUNT_NUMBER, ACCOUNT_STATUS,
			CUSTOMER_NUMBER, CUSTOMER_NAME, EXCHANGE_RATE, IMPAIRED_FLAG, OUTSTANDING, BUCKET_ID, REVOLVING_FLAG, PRODUCT_CODE,
			PRODUCT_TYPE,  LOAN_START_DATE, DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, EIR, LOAN_DUE_DATE, MARGIN_PAST_DUE,
			SEGMENTATION_ID, LT_RULE_ID,   DATA_SOURCE, PRODUCT_GROUP, IS_IMPAIRED,   PD_SEGMENT, LGD_SEGMENT,
			EAD_SEGMENT, BUCKET_GROUP, LIFETIME, STAGE, UNAMORT_COST_AMT, UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, MARGIN_ACCRUED, FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, EIL_MODEL_ID,
			EAD_RULE_ID, LGD_RULE_ID, LGD_ME_MODEL_ID, PD_RULE_ID, PD_ME_MODEL_ID, CURRENCY, EIL_AMOUNT,   PD,LGD, EIL_PRINCIPAL,EIL_MARGIN,EAD_AMOUNT,
			CREATEDBY, CREATEDDATE)
		SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, MAX(GROUP_SEGMENT), MAX(SEGMENT), MAX(SUB_SEGMENT), MAX(DAY_PAST_DUE), MAX(BI_COLLECTABILITY), MAX(ACCOUNT_NUMBER), MAX(ACCOUNT_STATUS),
			MAX(CUSTOMER_NUMBER), MAX(CUSTOMER_NAME), MAX(EXCHANGE_RATE), MAX(IMPAIRED_FLAG), MAX(OUTSTANDING), MAX(BUCKET_ID), MAX(REVOLVING_FLAG), MAX(PRODUCT_CODE), MAX(PRODUCT_TYPE),  
			MAX(LOAN_START_DATE), MAX(DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF), MAX(RESTRUCTURE_FLAG), MAX(EIR), MAX(LOAN_DUE_DATE), MAX(MARGIN_PAST_DUE), MAX(SEGMENTATION_ID), MAX(LT_RULE_ID),  
			MAX(DATA_SOURCE), MAX(PRODUCT_GROUP), MAX(IS_IMPAIRED), MAX(PD_SEGMENT), MAX(LGD_SEGMENT), MAX(EAD_SEGMENT), MAX(BUCKET_GROUP), MAX(LIFETIME), MAX(STAGE), MAX(UNAMORT_COST_AMT),
			MAX(UNAMORT_FEE_AMT), MAX(MARGIN_ACCRUED), MAX(FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT), MAX(EIL_MODEL_ID), MAX(EAD_RULE_ID), MAX(LGD_RULE_ID), MAX(LGD_ME_MODEL_ID), MAX(PD_RULE_ID), MAX(PD_ME_MODEL_ID), MAX(CURRENCY),
			SUM(EIL_AMOUNT), AVG(PD),AVG(LGD), SUM(EIL_PRINCIPAL), SUM(EIL_MARGIN) , MAX(CASE WHEN SEQ = 0 THEN EAD_PRINCIPAL + EAD_MARGIN  ELSE 0 END ) EAD,
			''IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER'' AS CREATEDBY,SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE
			FROM IFRS_EIL_RESULT_DETAILX 
			WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || '''
			GROUP BY DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID' ;
			 
	
		--DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);			
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
		COMMIT;
        -----------------------------
	    -- Log & insert final data
	    -----------------------------
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER ||
                ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')' ;

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;

EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN V_IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EIL_UPDATE_PORTFOLIO (
    p_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
	p_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    p_PRC           IN CHAR DEFAULT 'M'
)
AS
    v_RULE_ID        VARCHAR2(250);
    v_TABLE_NAME     VARCHAR2(100);
    v_STR_SQL        CLOB;
    v_GROUP_SEGMENT  VARCHAR2(250);
    v_SEGMENT        VARCHAR2(250);
    v_SUB_SEGMENT    VARCHAR2(250);
    v_CONDITION      VARCHAR2(4000);
    v_CURRDATE       DATE;
    v_EXCEPT_ID      VARCHAR2(50);
    v_ERROR_FLAG     NUMBER(1) := 0;
    v_TABLENAME      VARCHAR2(100);
BEGIN
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    -- INIT
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    IF p_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO v_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        v_CURRDATE := p_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;


    v_TABLENAME :=
        CASE
            WHEN p_PRC = 'M' THEN 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY'
            ELSE 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY_' || p_RUNID ||''
        END;

    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    -- RESET SEGMENT DATA (DYNAMIC UPDATE)
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    v_STR_SQL :=
        'UPDATE ' || v_TABLENAME || ' A ' ||
        'SET A.SUB_SEGMENT = NULL, ' ||
        '    A.SEGMENT = NULL, ' ||
        '    A.GROUP_SEGMENT = NULL, ' ||
        '    A.SEGMENTATION_ID = NULL ' ||
        'WHERE A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' ||
        TO_CHAR(v_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || '''';

    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_STR_SQL;
   
   
   v_STR_SQL :=
    ' DELETE PSAK413.IFRS_EXCEPTION_ACCOUNT WHERE EXCEPTION_ID = 1 AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' ||
            TO_CHAR(v_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ';
       
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_STR_SQL;

    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    -- CURSOR LOOP
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    FOR rec IN (
        SELECT PKID AS RULE_ID,
               v_TABLENAME AS TABLE_NAME,
               SEGMENT_NAME_LV1 AS GROUP_SEGMENT,
               SEGMENT_NAME_LV2 AS SEGMENT,
               SEGMENT_NAME_LV3 AS SUB_SEGMENT,
               MERGE_SQL_CONDITIONS AS CONDITION
        FROM IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING
        WHERE SEGMENT_TYPE = 'PORTFOLIO'
    )
    LOOP
        v_RULE_ID       := rec.RULE_ID;
        v_TABLE_NAME    := rec.TABLE_NAME;
        v_GROUP_SEGMENT := rec.GROUP_SEGMENT;
        v_SEGMENT       := rec.SEGMENT;
        v_SUB_SEGMENT   := rec.SUB_SEGMENT;
        v_CONDITION     := rec.CONDITION;
       
      
      v_STR_SQL :=
    ' INSERT INTO PSAK413.IFRS_EXCEPTION_ACCOUNT 
	(DOWNLOAD_DATE, DATA_SOURCE, EXCEPTION_ID, MASTERID, ACCOUNT_NUMBER, CUSTOMER_NAME,
    PRODUCT_GROUP, TABLE_NAME, FIELD_NAME, VALUE, CREATEDBY, CREATEDDATE, CREATEDHOST,
    FLAG)
	SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE , DATA_SOURCE ,  1 , MASTERID ,
	ACCOUNT_NUMBER , CUSTOMER_NAME, PRODUCT_GROUP , ''' || V_TABLE_NAME || ''', ''SEGMENTATION_ID'',
	''MULTIPLE_SEGMENT-'' || SEGMENTATION_ID || ''-' || V_RULE_ID || ''' , ''SP_IFRS_EIL_UPDATE_PORTFOLIO'', SYSDATE , ''HOST'', ''0'' 
	 FROM ' || V_TABLE_NAME || ' ifrs_master_account 
	 WHERE (' || v_CONDITION || ') ' ||
            'AND ifrs_master_account.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' ||
            TO_CHAR(v_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || '''
	AND SEGMENTATION_ID IS NOT NULL ';

 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(v_STR_SQL, 1, 30000));

        v_STR_SQL :=
            'UPDATE ' || v_TABLE_NAME || ' ifrs_master_account ' ||
            'SET ifrs_master_account.SUB_SEGMENT = ''' || v_SUB_SEGMENT || ''', ' ||
            '    ifrs_master_account.SEGMENT = ''' || v_SEGMENT || ''', ' ||
            '    ifrs_master_account.GROUP_SEGMENT = ''' || v_GROUP_SEGMENT || ''', ' ||
            '    ifrs_master_account.SEGMENTATION_ID = ''' || v_RULE_ID || ''' ' ||
            'WHERE (' || v_CONDITION || ') ' ||
            'AND ifrs_master_account.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' ||
            TO_CHAR(v_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || '''';

        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_STR_SQL;
    END LOOP;

    COMMIT;

EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN SP_IFRS_EIL_UPDATE_PORTFOLIO: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG
(
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE    IN DATE DEFAULT NULL,
    P_TABLE_DEST       IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL,
    P_COLUMN_DEST      IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL,
    P_STORENAME        IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL,
    P_OPERATION        IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL,
    P_AFFECTED_RECORD  IN NUMBER DEFAULT NULL,
    P_RUNID            IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000'
)
AS
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO IFRS_LOGS_PROCESS
        (DOWNLOAD_DATE,
         TABLE_DEST,
         COLUMN_DEST,
         SP_NAME,
         OPERATION,
         RUN_ID,
         PROCESS_ID,
         AFFECTED_RECORD,
         PROCESS_DATE)
    VALUES
        (P_DOWNLOAD_DATE,
         P_TABLE_DEST,
         P_COLUMN_DEST,
         P_STORENAME,
         P_OPERATION,
         P_RUNID,
         TO_NUMBER(SYS_CONTEXT('USERENV', 'SESSIONID')),  
         P_AFFECTED_RECORD,
         SYSTIMESTAMP);  

END SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_IMPI_JOURNAL_DATA (
    P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    P_PRC           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AUTHID CURRENT_USER
AS
    -- DATES / COUNTERS
    V_CURRDATE      DATE;
    V_PREVDATE      DATE;
    V_COUNT         NUMBER;

    -- DYNAMIC SQL
    V_STR_QUERY     CLOB;

    -- TABLE NAMES
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLENAME  VARCHAR2(100);

    -- MISC
    V_RETURNROWS    NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_RUNID VARCHAR2(50);
	V_PRC   VARCHAR2(1);

    -- RESULT QUERY
    V_QUERYS        CLOB;
BEGIN
    -- SET PROCEDURE NAME
    V_SP_NAME := 'SP_IFRS_IMPI_JOURNAL_DATA';

    -- SET IF NULL
	V_RUNID := NVL(P_RUNID, 'S_00000_0000');
	V_PRC   := NVL(P_PRC, 'S');

    -- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
          INTO V_CURRDATE
          FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE; 
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    IF V_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_TABLENAME  := 'IFRS_IMP_JOURNAL_DATA_' || V_RUNID;
    ELSE
        V_TABLENAME  := 'IFRS_IMP_JOURNAL_DATA';
    END IF;

   PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, V_RUNID, 0, SYSDATE);
   COMMIT;

    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    -- PRE-SIMULATION TABLE: CREATE/DROP TEMP TABLES IF V_PRC = 'S'
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    IF V_PRC = 'S' THEN
        -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM ALL_TABLES
        WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER
          AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLENAME);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLENAME;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLENAME ||
                       ' AS SELECT *  FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_IMP_JOURNAL_DATA';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;

    END IF;
    COMMIT;


    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLENAME;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), V_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLENAME;

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), V_RUNID);
    COMMIT;

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_IMP_FILL_IMA_PREV_CURR (
    P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    P_PRC           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AUTHID CURRENT_USER
AS
    -- DATES / COUNTERS
    V_CURRDATE      DATE;
    V_PREVDATE      DATE;
    V_COUNT         NUMBER;

    -- DYNAMIC SQL
    V_STR_QUERY     CLOB;

    -- TABLE NAMES
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLENAME  VARCHAR2(100);

    -- MISC
    V_RETURNROWS    NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_RUNID VARCHAR2(50);
	V_PRC   VARCHAR2(1);

    -- RESULT QUERY
    V_QUERYS        CLOB;
BEGIN
    -- SET PROCEDURE NAME
    V_SP_NAME := 'SP_IFRS_IMP_FILL_IMA_PREV_CURR';

    -- SET IF NULL
	V_RUNID := NVL(P_RUNID, 'S_00000_0000');
	V_PRC   := NVL(P_PRC, 'S');

    
    -- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
          INTO V_CURRDATE
          FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE; 
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    IF V_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_TABLENAME  := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_' || V_RUNID;
    ELSE
        V_TABLENAME  := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT';
    END IF;

   PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, V_RUNID, 0, SYSDATE);
   COMMIT;

    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    -- PRE-SIMULATION TABLE: CREATE/DROP TEMP TABLES IF V_PRC = 'S'
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    IF V_PRC = 'S' THEN
        -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM ALL_TABLES
        WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER
          AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLENAME);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLENAME;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLENAME ||
                       ' AS SELECT *  FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;

    END IF;
    COMMIT;


    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLENAME;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), V_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLENAME;

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), V_RUNID);
    COMMIT;

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_IMP_INITIAL_CONFIG (
        P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
        P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
        P_PRC           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
    )
    AUTHID CURRENT_USER
    AS
        -- DATES / COUNTERS
        V_CURRDATE      DATE;
        V_PREVDATE      DATE;
        V_COUNT         NUMBER;

        -- DYNAMIC SQL
        V_STR_QUERY     CLOB;

        -- TABLE NAMES
        V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
        V_TABLENAME  VARCHAR2(100);

        -- MISC
        V_RETURNROWS    NUMBER;
        V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
        V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
        V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
        V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100);
        V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
        V_RUNID VARCHAR2(50);
        V_PRC   VARCHAR2(1);

        -- RESULT QUERY
        V_QUERYS        CLOB;
    BEGIN
        -- SET PROCEDURE NAME
        V_SP_NAME := 'SP_IFRS_IMP_INITIAL_CONFIG';
    
        -- SET IF NULL
        V_RUNID := NVL(P_RUNID, 'S_00000_0000');
        V_PRC   := NVL(P_PRC, 'S');

        -- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
        IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
            SELECT CURRDATE
            INTO V_CURRDATE
            FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE; 
        ELSE
            V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
        END IF;

        IF V_PRC = 'S' THEN
            V_TABLENAME  := 'IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG_' || V_RUNID;
        ELSE
            V_TABLENAME  := 'IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG';
        END IF;

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, V_RUNID, 0, SYSDATE);
    COMMIT;

        ----------------------------------------------------------------
        -- PRE-SIMULATION TABLE: CREATE/DROP TEMP TABLES IF V_PRC = 'S'
        ----------------------------------------------------------------
        IF V_PRC = 'S' THEN
            -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS
            SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
            FROM ALL_TABLES
            WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER
            AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLENAME);

            IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
                V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLENAME;
                EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
            END IF;

            V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLENAME ||
                        ' AS SELECT *  FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG';
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;

        END IF;
        COMMIT;


        V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLENAME;
        V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
        V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
        PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), V_RUNID);
        COMMIT;  
    
        V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLENAME;

        PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), V_RUNID);
        COMMIT;

    END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_INITIAL_PAYM_SCHD (
P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE )
AS
V_CURRDATE       DATE;
BEGIN
	-- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;
   
   	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE IFRS_INITIAL_PAYM_SCHD ' ; 
   	
	INSERT INTO IFRS_INITIAL_PAYM_SCHD(DOWNLOAD_DATE,MASTERID,CREATED_DATE)
	SELECT MAX(DOWNLOAD_DATE),MASTERID ,SYSDATE FROM IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_ALL 
	WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE <= V_CURRDATE
	GROUP BY MASTERID;

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_INITIAL_UPDATE_IMP
(
    P_RUNID         VARCHAR2,
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS
    -- DATE
    V_CURRDATE   DATE;
    V_PREVDATE   DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID   VARCHAR2(22);
    V_COUNT      NUMBER;

    -- QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY  CLOB;

    -- TABLE LIST
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG  VARCHAR2(100);

    -- CONDITION / LOG
    V_RETURNROWS  NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST  VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME      VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION   VARCHAR2(100);

    V_QUERYS      CLOB;

BEGIN

	-- set procedure name
    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_INITIAL_UPDATE_IMP';
    
   ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- SET CURRDATE
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE_AMORT ipda ;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;
	
    V_PREVDATE := V_CURRDATE - 1;
    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
   
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- SET TABLE NAMES
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_TABLEINSERT1  := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_' || P_RUNID;
    ELSE
        V_TABLEINSERT1  := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT';
    END IF;
   

    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- UPDATE GLOBAL_CUSTOMER_NUMBER
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    V_STR_QUERY := 
    '
			MERGE INTO '|| V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' a USING
			(
				SELECT 
					 TO_DATE(SUBSTR(DOWNLOAD_DATE,1,10),''YYYY-MM-DD'') AS DDATE
					,CUSTOMER_NUMBER
					,GLOBAL_CUSTIMER_NUMBER
				FROM BSI_SUPER_CIF_FINAL
				WHERE TO_DATE(SUBSTR(DOWNLOAD_DATE,1,10),''YYYY-MM-DD'') = '|| TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || '
			) cif 
			ON 
			(
				a.DOWNLOAD_DATE = cif.DDATE 
				AND 
				a.CUSTOMER_NUMBER = cif.CUSTOMER_NUMBER
			)
			WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE 
			SET 
				GLOBAL_CUSTOMER_NUMBER = dat.GLOBAL_CUSTOMER_NUMBER        
   ';

	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
    --DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;   

   
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- UPDATE DIVISION_CODE
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------   
    V_STR_QUERY := 
    '
			MERGE INTO '|| V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' a USING
			(
				SELECT 
					 TO_DATE(SUBSTR(FICMISDATE,1,10),''YYYY-MM-DD'') AS DDATE
					,NOLOAN
					,DIVISI_PISAH
				FROM LOANPERDIVISI_ALL
				WHERE TO_DATE(SUBSTR(FICMISDATE,1,10),''YYYY-MM-DD'') = '|| TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || '
			) cif 
			ON 
			(
				a.DOWNLOAD_DATE = cif.DDATE 
				AND 
				a.ACCOUNT_NUMBER = cif.NOLOAN
				AND
				a.DATA_SOURCE IN (''iBSM'',''JFAST'')
			)
			WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE 
			SET 
				DIVISION_CODE = dat.DIVISI_PISAH        
   ';

	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
    --DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;      
   
   
   
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_INSERT_STG_PMA
(
    P_RUNID         VARCHAR2,
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS
    -- DATE
    V_CURRDATE   DATE;
    V_PREVDATE   DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID   VARCHAR2(22);
    V_COUNT      NUMBER;

    -- QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY  CLOB;

    -- TABLE LIST
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG  VARCHAR2(100);

    -- CONDITION / LOG
    V_RETURNROWS  NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST  VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME      VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION   VARCHAR2(100);

    V_QUERYS      CLOB;

BEGIN

	-- set procedure name
    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_INSERT_STG_PMA';
    
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- SET CURRDATE
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE_AMORT ipda ;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;
	
   
    V_PREVDATE := V_CURRDATE - 1;
    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
   
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- SET TABLE NAMES
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_TABLEINSERT1  := 'IFRS_STG_MASTER_ACCOUNT_' || P_RUNID;
    ELSE
        V_TABLEINSERT1  := 'IFRS_STG_MASTER_ACCOUNT';
    END IF;
   
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- LOG RUN_ID → Oracle tidak bisa CALL, cukup prosedur langsung
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    /*
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG
    (
        V_CURRDATE,
        V_SPNAME,
        P_RUNID,
        SYS_CONTEXT('USERENV','SID'),
        SYSDATE
    );
    COMMIT;
    */
   
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- DELETE EXISTING DATA--
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    V_STR_QUERY := '
            DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '
            WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
			AND SOURCE_PROCESS = ''CKPN_PMA_iBSM''
        ';

	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
    --DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;   
      
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- INSERT DATA FROM CKPN_BSI--
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
 	V_STR_QUERY := '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '
	(
	 DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,DATA_SOURCE
	,BRANCH_CODE
	,MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID
	,ACCOUNT_NUMBER
	,CUSTOMER_NUMBER
	,CUSTOMER_NAME
	,FACILITY_NUMBER
	,PRODUCT_CODE
	,PRODUCT_TYPE
	,COMMITTED_FLAG
	,SEGMENT
	,COLLATERAL_VALUE_FOR_IMPAIR
	,KODE_JENIS_PENGGUNAAN
	,SEKTOR_INDUSTRI
	,KODE_SEKTOR_EKONOMI
	,CURRENCY
	,EXCHANGE_RATE
	,PLAFOND
	,MARGIN_RATE
	,OUTSTANDING
	,OUTSTANDING_MARGIN
	,ACCOUNT_STATUS
	,LOAN_START_DATE
	,LOAN_DUE_DATE
	,TENOR
	,MARGIN_CALCULATION_CODE
	,DAY_PAST_DUE
	,ORIGINAL_BI_COLLECTABILITY
	,BI_COLLECTABILITY
	,RESTRUCTURED_FLAG
	,RESTRUCTURE_DATE
	,DEFAULT_DATE
	,SOURCE_PROCESS
	,AYDA
	,DESC_JENIS_PENGGUNAAN
	,DIVISION_CODE
	,ACCRUED_MARGIN
	,MARGIN_PASTDUE
	,OUTSTANDING_PASTDUE
	,RATING_CODE
	,RATING_AGENCY
	)
	SELECT
	 A.DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,A.DATA_SOURCE
	,A.BRANCH_CODE
	,A.DATA_SOURCE||A.ACCOUNT_NUMBER AS MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID
	,A.ACCOUNT_NUMBER
	,A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER
	,A.CUSTOMER_NAME
	,A.FACILITY_NUMBER
	,A.PRODUCT_CODE
	,A.PRODUCT_TYPE
	,A.COMMITTED_FLAG
	,A.SEGMENT
	,A.COLLATERAL_VALUE_FOR_IMPAIR
	,A.KODE_JENIS_PENGGUNAAN
	,A.SEKTOR_INDUSTRI
	,A.KODE_SEKTOR_EKONOMI
	,A.CURRENCY
	,A.EXCHANGE_RATE
	,A.PLAFOND
	,A.INTEREST_RATE
	,A.OUTSTANDING_POKOK
	,A.OUTSTANDING_MARGIN
	,A.ACCOUNT_STATUS
	,A.LOAN_START_DATE
	,A.LOAN_DUE_DATE
	,A.TENOR
	,A.INTEREST_CALCULATION_CODE
	,A.DAY_PAST_DUE
	,A.ORIGINAL_COLLECTABILITY
	,A.BI_COLLECTABILITY
	,A.RESTRUCTURED_LOAN_FLAG
	,A.RESTRUCTURE_DATE
	,A.DEFAULT_DATE
	,''CKPN_PMA_iBSM'' AS SOURCE_PROCESS
	,A.AYDA
	,A.DESC_JENIS_PENGGUNAAN
	,NULL AS DIVISION_CODE
	,A.ACCRUED_MARGIN
	,A.TUNGGAKAN_MARGIN
	,A.TUNGGAKAN_POKOK
	,A.RATING_CODE
	,A.RATING_AGENCY
	FROM CKPN_PMA_IBSM A
	WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	';	

 EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
 --DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
 COMMIT; 


END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_INSERT_STG_PMA_DVC_HC
(
    P_RUNID         VARCHAR2,
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS
    -- DATE
    V_CURRDATE   DATE;
    V_PREVDATE   DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID   VARCHAR2(22);
    V_COUNT      NUMBER;

    -- QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY  CLOB;

    -- TABLE LIST
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG  VARCHAR2(100);

    -- CONDITION / LOG
    V_RETURNROWS  NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST  VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME      VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION   VARCHAR2(100);

    V_QUERYS      CLOB;

BEGIN

	-- set procedure name
    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_INSERT_STG_PMA_DVC_HC';
    
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- SET CURRDATE
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE_AMORT ipda ;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;
	
   
    V_PREVDATE := V_CURRDATE - 1;
    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
   
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- SET TABLE NAMES
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_TABLEINSERT1  := 'IFRS_STG_MASTER_ACCOUNT_' || P_RUNID;
    ELSE
        V_TABLEINSERT1  := 'IFRS_STG_MASTER_ACCOUNT';
    END IF;
   
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- LOG RUN_ID → Oracle tidak bisa CALL, cukup prosedur langsung
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    /*
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG
    (
        V_CURRDATE,
        V_SPNAME,
        P_RUNID,
        SYS_CONTEXT('USERENV','SID'),
        SYSDATE
    );
    COMMIT;
    */
   
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- DELETE EXISTING DATA--
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    V_STR_QUERY := '
            DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '
            WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
			AND SOURCE_PROCESS = ''CKPN_PMA_DVC_HC''
        ';

	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
    --DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;   
      
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- INSERT DATA FROM CKPN_BSI--
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
 	V_STR_QUERY := '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '
	(
	 DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,DATA_SOURCE
	,BRANCH_CODE
	,MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID
	,ACCOUNT_NUMBER
	,CUSTOMER_NUMBER
	,CUSTOMER_NAME
	,FACILITY_NUMBER
	,PRODUCT_CODE
	,PRODUCT_TYPE
	,COMMITTED_FLAG
	,SEGMENT
	,COLLATERAL_VALUE_FOR_IMPAIR
	,KODE_JENIS_PENGGUNAAN
	,SEKTOR_INDUSTRI
	,KODE_SEKTOR_EKONOMI
	,CURRENCY
	,EXCHANGE_RATE
	,PLAFOND
	,MARGIN_RATE
	,OUTSTANDING
	,OUTSTANDING_MARGIN
	,ACCOUNT_STATUS
	,LOAN_START_DATE
	,LOAN_DUE_DATE
	,TENOR
	,MARGIN_CALCULATION_CODE
	,DAY_PAST_DUE
	,ORIGINAL_BI_COLLECTABILITY
	,BI_COLLECTABILITY
	,RESTRUCTURED_FLAG
	,RESTRUCTURE_DATE
	,DEFAULT_DATE
	,SOURCE_PROCESS
	,AYDA
	,DESC_JENIS_PENGGUNAAN
	,DIVISION_CODE
	,ACCRUED_MARGIN
	,MARGIN_PASTDUE
	,OUTSTANDING_PASTDUE
	,RATING_CODE
	,RATING_AGENCY
	)
	SELECT
	 FICMISDATE AS DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,DATA_SOURCE
	,KODECABANG AS BRANCH_CODE
	,DATA_SOURCE||''-''||NOMORREKENING AS MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID
	,NOMORREKENING AS ACCOUNT_NUMBER
	,NOMORNASABAH AS CUSTOMER_NUMBER
	,NAMANASABAH AS CUSTOMER_NAME
	,NULL AS FACILITY_NUMBER
	,LOANTYPECODE AS PRODUCT_CODE
	,NULL AS PRODUCT_TYPE
	,NULL AS COMMITTED_FLAG
	,NULL AS SEGMENT
	,NULL AS COLLATERAL_VALUE_FOR_IMPAIR
	,NULL AS KODE_JENIS_PENGGUNAAN
	,NULL AS SEKTOR_INDUSTRI
	,NULL AS KODE_SEKTOR_EKONOMI
	,JENISVALUTA AS CURRENCY
	,1 AS EXCHANGE_RATE
	,PLAFONAWAL AS PLAFOND
	,PERSENTASEIMBALANBULANLAPORAN AS MARGIN_RATE
	,JUMLAHBULANLAPORAN AS OUTSTANDING
	,NULL AS OUTSTANDING_MARGIN
	,''A'' AS ACCOUNT_STATUS
	,JANGKAWAKTUMULAI AS LOAN_START_DATE
	,JANGKAWAKTUJATUHTEMPO AS LOAN_DUE_DATE
	,NULL AS TENOR
	,NULL AS MARGIN_CALCULATION_CODE
	,TUNGGAKANHARI AS DAY_PAST_DUE
	,KUALITAS AS ORIGINAL_BI_COLLECTABILITY
	,KUALITAS AS BI_COLLECTABILITY
	,CASE WHEN SIFATPIUTANG in (1,5) then ''Y'' ELSE ''N'' END AS RESTRUCTURED_FLAG
	,NULL AS RESTRUCTURE_DATE
	,NULL AS DEFAULT_DATE
	,''CKPN_PMA_DVC_HC'' AS SOURCE_PROCESS
	,NULL AS AYDA
	,NULL AS DESC_JENIS_PENGGUNAAN
	,DIVISIPISAH AS DIVISION_CODE
	,NULL AS ACCRUED_MARGIN
	,TUNGGAKANMARGIN AS MARGIN_PASTDUE
	,TUNGGAKANPOKOK AS OUTSTANDING_PASTDUE
	,NULL AS RATING_CODE
	,NULL AS RATING_AGENCY
	FROM FORM12_SANDIRINCIANPIUTANGQARDH_RPT A
	WHERE FICMISDATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	';	

 EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
 --DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
 COMMIT; 


END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_INSERT_STG_PMA_JFAST
(
    P_RUNID         VARCHAR2,
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS
    -- DATE
    V_CURRDATE   DATE;
    V_PREVDATE   DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID   VARCHAR2(22);
    V_COUNT      NUMBER;

    -- QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY  CLOB;

    -- TABLE LIST
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG  VARCHAR2(100);

    -- CONDITION / LOG
    V_RETURNROWS  NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST   VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST  VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME      VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION   VARCHAR2(100);

    V_QUERYS      CLOB;

BEGIN

	-- set procedure name
    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_INSERT_STG_PMA_JFAST';
    
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- SET CURRDATE
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE_AMORT ipda ;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;
	
   
    V_PREVDATE := V_CURRDATE - 1;
    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
   
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- SET TABLE NAMES
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        V_TABLEINSERT1  := 'IFRS_STG_MASTER_ACCOUNT_' || P_RUNID;
    ELSE
        V_TABLEINSERT1  := 'IFRS_STG_MASTER_ACCOUNT';
    END IF;
   
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- LOG RUN_ID → Oracle tidak bisa CALL, cukup prosedur langsung
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    /*
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG
    (
        V_CURRDATE,
        V_SPNAME,
        P_RUNID,
        SYS_CONTEXT('USERENV','SID'),
        SYSDATE
    );
    COMMIT;
    */
   
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- DELETE EXISTING DATA--
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    V_STR_QUERY := '
            DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '
            WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
			AND SOURCE_PROCESS = ''CKPN_PMA_JFAST''
        ';

	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
    --DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;   
      
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
    -- INSERT DATA FROM CKPN_BSI--
    ------------------------------------------------------------------------
 	V_STR_QUERY := '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '
	(
	 DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,DATA_SOURCE
	,BRANCH_CODE
	,MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID
	,ACCOUNT_NUMBER
	,CUSTOMER_NUMBER
	,CUSTOMER_NAME
	,FACILITY_NUMBER
	,PRODUCT_CODE
	,PRODUCT_TYPE
	,COMMITTED_FLAG
	,SEGMENT
	,COLLATERAL_VALUE_FOR_IMPAIR
	,KODE_JENIS_PENGGUNAAN
	,SEKTOR_INDUSTRI
	,KODE_SEKTOR_EKONOMI
	,CURRENCY
	,EXCHANGE_RATE
	,PLAFOND
	,MARGIN_RATE
	,OUTSTANDING
	,OUTSTANDING_MARGIN
	,ACCOUNT_STATUS
	,LOAN_START_DATE
	,LOAN_DUE_DATE
	,TENOR
	,MARGIN_CALCULATION_CODE
	,DAY_PAST_DUE
	,ORIGINAL_BI_COLLECTABILITY
	,BI_COLLECTABILITY
	,RESTRUCTURED_FLAG
	,RESTRUCTURE_DATE
	,DEFAULT_DATE
	,SOURCE_PROCESS
	,AYDA
	,DESC_JENIS_PENGGUNAAN
	,DIVISION_CODE
	,ACCRUED_MARGIN
	,MARGIN_PASTDUE
	,OUTSTANDING_PASTDUE
	,RATING_CODE
	,RATING_AGENCY
	)
	SELECT
	 A.DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,A.DATA_SOURCE
	,A.BRANCH_CODE
	,A.DATA_SOURCE||A.ACCOUNT_NUMBER AS MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID
	,A.ACCOUNT_NUMBER
	,A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER
	,A.CUSTOMER_NAME
	,A.FACILITY_NUMBER
	,A.PRODUCT_CODE
	,A.PRODUCT_TYPE
	,A.COMMITTED_FLAG
	,A.SEGMENT
	,A.COLLATERAL_VALUE_FOR_IMPAIR
	,A.KODE_JENIS_PENGGUNAAN
	,A.SEKTOR_INDUSTRI
	,A.KODE_SEKTOR_EKONOMI
	,A.CURRENCY
	,A.EXCHANGE_RATE
	,A.PLAFOND
	,A.INTEREST_RATE
	,A.OUTSTANDING_POKOK
	,A.OUTSTANDING_MARGIN
	,A.ACCOUNT_STATUS
	,A.LOAN_START_DATE
	,A.LOAN_DUE_DATE
	,A.TENOR
	,A.INTEREST_CALCULATION_CODE
	,A.DAY_PAST_DUE
	,A.ORIGINAL_COLLECTABILITY
	,A.BI_COLLECTABILITY
	,A.RESTRUCTURED_LOAN_FLAG
	,A.RESTRUCTURE_DATE
	,A.DEFAULT_DATE
	,''CKPN_PMA_JFAST'' AS SOURCE_PROCESS
	,A.AYDA
	,A.DESC_JENIS_PENGGUNAAN
	,NULL AS DIVISION_CODE
	,A.ACCRUED_MARGIN
	,A.TUNGGAKAN_MARGIN
	,A.TUNGGAKAN_POKOK
	,A.RATING_CODE
	,A.RATING_AGENCY
	FROM CKPN_PMA_JFAST A
	WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	';	

 EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
 --DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
 COMMIT; 


END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0', 
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'X'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(8000);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(8000);

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
