    V_TABLESELECT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT3 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT4 VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLECONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA';
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));
 	V_TABLECONFIG := 'IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG ';
	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN 
        --V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'GTMP_LGD_RUNNING_CONFIG_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_DEFAULT_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE 
       -- V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'GTMP_LGD_RUNNING_CONFIG';
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_DEFAULT'; 
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA' ;
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
	----TABLE CONFIG
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT = 0 THEN 
		V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_DATA ild  WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
		END IF;

        
    END IF;
	COMMIT;


	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG ' ; 
		 
	     V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG 
               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG 
               WHERE  IS_DELETED = 0 AND (  
                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_WORKOUT)) IN ( 
                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
                   FROM DUAL
                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
                 )
                 OR :p2 = ''0''
               )'; 
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
 
    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.DEFAULT_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.DEFAULT_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	 AND EXISTS (SELECT * FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG  X WHERE A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = X.SEGMENTATION_ID)'; 
   
    END IF;
     DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
     
   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
   COMMIT;
  
	-- End Clear Session

	-- RESET STATUS WO
	V_STR_QUERY := ''; 
	V_STR_QUERY := 'UPDATE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' A 
	SET ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A'' ,
		A.UPDATEDBY = ''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA'',
		A.UPDATEDDATE = SYSDATE,
		A.WO_DATE = NULL
	WHERE A.WO_DATE >= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND A.DEFAULT_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG  X WHERE A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = X.SEGMENTATION_ID) '
	;
	 

	 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;
 


    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));

	-- RESET STATUS CLOSED
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := 'UPDATE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' A 
	SET ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A'' ,
		A.UPDATEDBY = ''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA'',
		A.UPDATEDDATE = SYSDATE,
		A.CLOSED_DATE = NULL
	WHERE A.CLOSED_DATE >= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND A.DEFAULT_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG  X WHERE A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = X.SEGMENTATION_ID) '
	;
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));

	--POPULATE LGD DATA
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' (
	 LGD_SEGMENT_ID,DEFAULT_DATE , CUSTOMER_NUMBER, FACILITY_NUMBER, MASTERID,
	CURRENCY, ACCOUNT_STATUS, CURE_FLAG, --CURED_DATE, WO_DATE, CLOSED_DATE,
	OS_AT_DEFAULT, EQV_AT_DEFAULT, OS_WO, EQV_WO, EIR_AT_DEFAULT
	 ,CREATEDBY
	 ,CREATEDDATE
	 )
	SELECT B.SEGMENTATION_ID, A.DOWNLOAD_DATE
	 ,A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER
	 ,A.FACILITY_NUMBER, A.MASTERID
	 ,A.CCY_AT_DEFAULT , ''A'', 0--, NULL, NULL, NULL
	 ,A.OS_AT_DEFAULT
	 ,A.EQV_AT_DEFAULT
	,0,0, A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT
	 ,''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA'' CREATEDBY 
	 ,SYSDATE CREATEDDATE 
	FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A 
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG  B ON A.RULE_ID = B.DEFAULT_RULE_ID 
	WHERE A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM  ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT2 || ' C WHERE A.MASTERID = C.MASTERID 
	 AND A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = C.DOWNLOAD_DATE AND C.RULE_ID  =B.SEGMENTATION_ID 
FETCH FIRST 1 ROWS ONLY ) ';

 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;



	-- UPDATE STATUS WO
	V_STR_QUERY := 'UPDATE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' A 
	SET A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''W'',
	A.WO_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''),
	A.UPDATEDBY = ''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA_4'',
	A.UPDATEDDATE = SYSDATE
	WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG  X WHERE A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = X.PKID)
	AND EXISTS (
		SELECT 1 
		FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_WO Y 
		WHERE A.MASTERID = Y.MASTERID 
			AND Y.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''))
	AND A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A''
	AND A.DEFAULT_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	' ; 

 	DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000)); 

	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

	-- UPDATE STATUS CLOSED
	V_STR_QUERY := 'UPDATE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' A 
	SET A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''C'',
	A.CLOSED_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''),
	A.UPDATEDBY = ''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA_4'',
	A.UPDATEDDATE = SYSDATE
	WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG  X WHERE A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = X.PKID)
	AND EXISTS (
		SELECT 1 
		FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_CLOSE Y 
		WHERE A.MASTERID = Y.MASTERID 
			AND Y.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''))
	AND A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A''
	AND A.DEFAULT_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	' ; 


 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== BODY ======

    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TABLEINSERT1;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TABLEINSERT2 || ' WHERE DEFAULT_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA2 (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0', 
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'X'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(8000);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(8000);

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT3 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT4 VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLECONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA';
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));
 	V_TABLECONFIG := 'IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG';
	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN 
        --V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'GTMP_LGD_RUNNING_CONFIG_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_DEFAULT_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE 
       -- V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'GTMP_LGD_RUNNING_CONFIG';
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_DEFAULT';
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA'; 
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
	----TABLE CONFIG
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT = 0 THEN 
		V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_DATA ild  WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
		END IF;

        
    END IF;
	COMMIT;


	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
		 
	     V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
               WHERE LGD_METHOD = ''Expected Recovery'' AND IS_DELETED = 0 AND (  
                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LGD)) IN ( 
                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
                   FROM DUAL
                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
                 )
                 OR :p2 = ''0''
               )';
  DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
 
    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.DEFAULT_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.DEFAULT_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	 AND EXISTS (SELECT * FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)'; 
   
    END IF;
     DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
     
   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
   COMMIT;
  
	-- End Clear Session

	-- RESET STATUS WO
	V_STR_QUERY := ''; 
	V_STR_QUERY := 'UPDATE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' A 
	SET ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A'' ,
		A.UPDATEDBY = ''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA'',
		A.UPDATEDDATE = SYSDATE,
		A.WO_DATE = NULL
	WHERE A.WO_DATE >= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND A.DEFAULT_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID) '
	;
	 

	 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;




    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));

	-- RESET STATUS CLOSED
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := 'UPDATE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' A 
	SET ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A'' ,
		A.UPDATEDBY = ''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA'',
		A.UPDATEDDATE = SYSDATE,
		A.CLOSED_DATE = NULL
	WHERE A.CLOSED_DATE >= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND A.DEFAULT_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID) '
	;
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));

	--POPULATE LGD DATA
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' (
	 LGD_RULE_ID,DEFAULT_DATE , CUSTOMER_NUMBER, FACILITY_NUMBER, MASTERID,
	CURRENCY, ACCOUNT_STATUS, CURE_FLAG, --CURED_DATE, WO_DATE, CLOSED_DATE,
	OS_AT_DEFAULT, EQV_AT_DEFAULT, OS_WO, EQV_WO, EIR_AT_DEFAULT
	 ,CREATEDBY
	 ,CREATEDDATE
	 )
	SELECT B.PKID, A.DOWNLOAD_DATE
	 ,A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER
	 ,A.FACILITY_NUMBER, A.MASTERID
	 ,A.CCY_AT_DEFAULT , ''A'', 0--, NULL, NULL, NULL
	 ,A.OS_AT_DEFAULT
	 ,A.EQV_AT_DEFAULT
	,0,0, A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT
	 ,''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA'' CREATEDBY 
	 ,SYSDATE CREATEDDATE 
	FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A 
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG B ON A.RULE_ID = B.DEFAULT_RULE_ID 
	WHERE A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM  ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT2 || ' C WHERE A.MASTERID = C.MASTERID 
	 AND A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = C.DOWNLOAD_DATE AND C.RULE_ID  =B.SEGMENTATION_ID 
FETCH FIRST 1 ROWS ONLY ) ';

 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

  
	-- UPDATE STATUS WO
	V_STR_QUERY := 'UPDATE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' A 
	SET A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''W'',
	A.WO_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''),
	A.UPDATEDBY = ''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA_4'',
	A.UPDATEDDATE = SYSDATE
	WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
	AND EXISTS (
		SELECT 1 
		FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_WO Y 
		WHERE A.MASTERID = Y.MASTERID 
			AND Y.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''))
	AND A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A''
	AND A.DEFAULT_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	' ; 

 	DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000)); 

	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

	-- UPDATE STATUS CLOSED
	V_STR_QUERY := 'UPDATE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' A 
	SET A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''C'',
	A.CLOSED_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''),
	A.UPDATEDBY = ''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA_4'',
	A.UPDATEDDATE = SYSDATE
	WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
	AND EXISTS (
		SELECT 1 
		FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_CLOSE Y 
		WHERE A.MASTERID = Y.MASTERID 
			AND Y.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''))
	AND A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A''
	AND A.DEFAULT_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	' ; 


 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== BODY ======

    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TABLEINSERT1;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TABLEINSERT2 || ' WHERE DEFAULT_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_DATAx (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0', 
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(22);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(8000);

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT3 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT4 VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLECONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));

	
		V_TABLECONFIG := 'IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG';
	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN 
        --V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'GTMP_LGD_RUNNING_CONFIG_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_DEFAULT_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT3 := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_WO_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT4 := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_CLOSE_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE 
       -- V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'GTMP_LGD_RUNNING_CONFIG';
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_DEFAULT';
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA';
        V_TABLESELECT3 := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_WO';
        V_TABLESELECT4 := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_CLOSE';
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
	----TABLE CONFIG
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT = 0 THEN 
		V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_DATA ild  WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
		END IF;

        
    END IF;
	COMMIT;


	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
		 
	    V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               WHERE LGD_METHOD = ''Expected Recovery'' AND (  
	                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LGD)) IN ( 
	                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
	                   FROM DUAL
	                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
	                 )
	                 OR :p2 IS NULL 
	               )';
	 
	    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
 
    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2 ||' A
    WHERE A.DEFAULT_DATE >= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2 ||' A
    USING ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' B 
    WHERE A.SYSCODE_LGD = B.SYSCODE_LGD AND A.LGD_RULE_ID = B.LGD_RULE_ID
    AND A.DEFAULT_DATE >= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    END IF;
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	-- End Clear Session

	-- RESET STATUS WO
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	MERGE INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2 || ' A 
	USING (
	 SELECT A.MASTERID, A.DEFAULT_DATE
	 FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2 || ' A
	 JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' B ON A.SYSCODE_LGD = B.SYSCODE_LGD AND A.LGD_RULE_ID = B.LGD_RULE_ID
	 WHERE A.WO_DATE >= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	) B ON (A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID AND A.DEFAULT_DATE = B.DEFAULT_DATE) 
	WHEN MATCHED THEN 
	UPDATE SET A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A'',
	A.WO_DATE = NULL,
	A.UPDATEDBY = ''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA'',
	A.UPDATEDATE = SYSDATE()';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));

	-- RESET STATUS CLOSED
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	MERGE INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2 || ' A 
	USING (
	 SELECT A.MASTERID, A.DEFAULT_DATE
	 FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2 || ' A
	 JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' B ON A.SYSCODE_LGD = B.SYSCODE_LGD AND A.LGD_RULE_ID = B.LGD_RULE_ID
	 WHERE A.CLOSED_DATE >= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	) B ON (A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID AND A.DEFAULT_DATE = B.DEFAULT_DATE) 
	WHEN MATCHED THEN 
	UPDATE SET A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A'',
	A.CLOSED_DATE = NULL,
	A.UPDATEDBY = ''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA_1'',
	A.UPDATEDATE = SYSDATE()';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));

	--POPULATE LGD DATA
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2 || ' (
	 DEFAULT_DATE 
	 ,SYSCODE_LGD
	 ,LGD_RULE_ID
	 ,DEFAULT_RULE_ID 
	 ,MASTERID
	 ,FACILITY_NUMBER 
	 ,CUSTOMER_NUMBER 
	 ,EIR_AT_DEFAULT
	 ,CURRENCY
	 ,EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT 
	 ,EQV_OS_INT_AT_DEFAULT 
	 ,OS_AT_DEFAULT  
	 ,OS_INT_AT_DEFAULT
	 ,WO_DATE
	 ,CLOSED_DATE
	 ,ACCOUNT_STATUS
	 ,CREATEDBY
	 ,CREATEDDATE
	 )
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	 ,B.SYSCODE_LGD
	 ,B.LGD_RULE_ID
	 ,A.RULE_ID 
	 ,A.MASTERID  
	 ,C.FACILITY_NUMBER 
	 ,C.CUSTOMER_NUMBER
	 ,A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT
	 ,C.CURRENCY
	 ,A.EQV_AT_DEFAULT 
	 ,A.EQV_OS_INT_AT_DEFAULT 
	 ,A.OS_AT_DEFAULT    
	 ,A.OS_INT_AT_DEFAULT 
	 ,D.DOWNLOAD_DATE AS WO_DATE 
	 ,NULL AS CLOSED_DATE 
	 ,C.ACCOUNT_STATUS  
	 ,''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA'' CREATEDBY 
	 ,SYSDATE() CREATEDDATE 
	FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A 
	INNER JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' B ON A.RULE_ID = B.DEFAULT_RULE_ID 
	INNER JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT2 || ' C ON A.MASTERID = C.MASTERID 
	 AND B.SEGMENTATION_ID = C.RULE_ID 
	 AND C.RULE_TYPE = ''LGD_SEGMENT'' 
	LEFT JOIN IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_WO D ON C.MASTERID = D.MASTERID 
	 AND D.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	WHERE A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
            
	-- UPDATE STATUS WO
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	MERGE INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2 || ' A 
	USING (
	 SELECT A.MASTERID, A.DEFAULT_DATE, C.DOWNLOAD_DATE AS WO_DATE
	 FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2 || ' A
	 JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' B ON A.SYSCODE_LGD = B.SYSCODE_LGD AND A.LGD_RULE_ID = B.LGD_RULE_ID
	 JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT3 || ' C ON A.MASTERID = C.MASTERID
	 WHERE A.DEFAULT_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	  AND A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A''
	  AND C.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	) B ON (A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID AND A.DEFAULT_DATE = B.DEFAULT_DATE) 
	WHEN MATCHED THEN 
	UPDATE SET A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''W'',
	A.WO_DATE = B.WO_DATE,
	A.UPDATEDBY = ''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA_4'',
	A.UPDATEDATE = SYSDATE()';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

	-- UPDATE STATUS CLOSED
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	MERGE INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2 || ' A 
	USING (
	 SELECT A.MASTERID, A.DEFAULT_DATE
	 FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2 || ' A
	 JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' B ON A.SYSCODE_LGD = B.SYSCODE_LGD AND A.LGD_RULE_ID = B.LGD_RULE_ID
	 WHERE A.DEFAULT_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	  AND A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A''
	  AND NOT EXISTS (
	   SELECT * 
	   FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT2 || ' C
	   WHERE C.RULE_TYPE = ''LGD_SEGMENT''
	    AND C.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	    AND C.MASTERID = A.MASTERID
	    AND C.RULE_ID = B.SEGMENTATION_ID
	   FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY
	  )
	OR EXISTS (
	 SELECT * 
	 FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT4 || ' Z
	 WHERE Z.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	  AND Z.MASTERID = A.MASTERID
	 FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY
	)
	) B ON (A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID AND A.DEFAULT_DATE = B.DEFAULT_DATE) 
	WHEN MATCHED THEN 
	UPDATE SET A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''C'',
	A.CLOSED_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''),
	A.UPDATEDBY = ''SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA_3'',
	A.UPDATEDATE = SYSDATE()';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== BODY ======

    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TABLEINSERT2;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, V_RETURNROWS2, P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TABLEINSERT2 || ' WHERE DEFAULT_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, V_RETURNROWS2, P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'X'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(8000);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(8000);

	---- TABLE LIST A
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLECONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));
	
  --  IF V_CURRDATE = V_EOMDATE THEN   
 		V_TABLE_NAME := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY' ;
 --	ELSE 
 	--	V_TABLE_NAME := 'VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT';
 --	END IF ;
 
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN 
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA_' || P_RUNID || '';  
		V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA_' || P_RUNID || '';
    ELSE 
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA';  
		V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA';
    END IF;

    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA';
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
	----TABLE PROCESS
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT = 0 THEN
		V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
		END IF;

        
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
 
 	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
	 V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG
               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG
               WHERE   IS_DELETED = 0 AND (  
                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_WORKOUT)) IN ( 
                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
                   FROM DUAL
                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
                 )
                 OR :p2 = ''0''
               )'; 
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
	   
	    
   
    -------- ====== BODY ======
	-- Clear Session
    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
    V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A 
    WHERE  A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')  
    AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG  X WHERE A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = X.SEGMENTATION_ID)'; 
    END IF;
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;
 
   
    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	-- End Clear Session
   
   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_DEFAULT_LGD';
   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE  GTMP_IFRS_IMA_CURR';  
   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE  GTMP_IFRS_IMA_PREV'; 
   
  	V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_DEFAULT_LGD (DEFAULT_DATE ,LGD_SEGMENT_ID , CUSTOMER_NUMBER,FACILITY_NUMBER, MASTERID,EIR,CCY, OUTSTANDING)
WITH CTE AS (
SELECT DEFAULT_DATE, MASTERID  , LGD_SEGMENT_ID ,
CUSTOMER_NUMBER , FACILITY_NUMBER ,EIR_AT_DEFAULT , CURRENCY  , OS_AT_DEFAULT,
ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY LGD_SEGMENT_ID,MASTERID  ORDER BY DEFAULT_DATE) RN
FROM ' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A  
WHERE DEFAULT_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 fROM  GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG  X WHERE A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = X.SEGMENTATION_ID)
)
SELECT DEFAULT_DATE, LGD_SEGMENT_ID ,CUSTOMER_NUMBER ,FACILITY_NUMBER ,MASTERID ,EIR_AT_DEFAULT , CURRENCY , OS_AT_DEFAULT
FROM CTE 
WHERE RN = 1 
'; 
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
COMMIT;

 

V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_IMA_PREV (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, CCY, OUTSTANDING, PRC_TYPE)
	SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, CURRENCY, OUTSTANDING, ''LGD''
	FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A 
	WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_PREVDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND ACCOUNT_STATUS IN(''A'',''W'')
	AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_DEFAULT_LGD X WHERE A.MASTERID = X.MASTERID FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY)';
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
COMMIT;

V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_IMA_CURR (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, CCY, OUTSTANDING, PRC_TYPE)
	SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, CURRENCY, OUTSTANDING, ''LGD''
	FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A 
	WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND ACCOUNT_STATUS IN(''A'',''W'')
	AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_DEFAULT_LGD X WHERE A.MASTERID = X.MASTERID FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY)';
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));

   

	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' (
	 DOWNLOAD_DATE
	 ,LGD_SEGMENT_ID, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, FACILITY_NUMBER
	 ,MASTERID, CCY,REC_TYPE,SEQ
	 ,REC_OS
	 ,EQV_REC_OS
	 ,CREATEDBY
	 ,CREATEDDATE )
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
		,B.LGD_SEGMENT_ID, B.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, B.FACILITY_NUMBER   
		,B.MASTERID , B.CCY, ''OS'' 
		,TRUNC(MONTHS_BETWEEN(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''),  B.DEFAULT_DATE))
		,C.OUTSTANDING - NVL(A.OUTSTANDING, 0) AS REC_OS    
		,(C.OUTSTANDING - NVL(A.OUTSTANDING, 0)) * E.RATE_AMOUNT AS EQV_REQ_OS     
		,''SP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DETAIL_1''   
		,SYSDATE
	FROM GTMP_IFRS_DEFAULT_LGD B    
		LEFT JOIN GTMP_IFRS_IMA_CURR A ON B.MASTERID = A.MASTERID     
		JOIN GTMP_IFRS_IMA_PREV C ON C.MASTERID = B.MASTERID      
		JOIN IFRS_MASTER_EXCHANGE_RATE E ON B.CCY = E.CURRENCY    
			AND E.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	WHERE B.DEFAULT_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_PREVDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	    

	-- DELETE REC OS = 0 & REC_OS_INT = 0
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' 
	WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE =  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	AND REC_OS <= 0 ';  
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
    -------- ====== BODY ======

    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA2 (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'X'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(8000);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(8000);

	---- TABLE LIST A
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLECONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));
	
  --  IF V_CURRDATE = V_EOMDATE THEN   
 		V_TABLE_NAME := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY' ;
 --	ELSE 
 	--	V_TABLE_NAME := 'VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT';
 --	END IF ;
 
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN 
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA_' || P_RUNID || '';  
		V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_DEFAULT_' || P_RUNID || '';
    ELSE 
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA';  
		V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_DEFAULT';
    END IF;

    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA';
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
	----TABLE PROCESS
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT = 0 THEN
		V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
		END IF;

        
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
 

	 V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
               WHERE LGD_METHOD = ''Expected Recovery'' AND IS_DELETED = 0 AND (  
                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LGD)) IN ( 
                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
                   FROM DUAL
                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
                 )
                 OR :p2 = ''0''
               )';
  DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
	   
	    
   
    -------- ====== BODY ======
	-- Clear Session
    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
    V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A 
    WHERE  A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')  
    AND EXISTS (SELECT * FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.RULE_ID = X.DEFAULT_RULE_ID)'; 
    END IF;
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;
 
   
    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	-- End Clear Session
   
   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_DEFAULT_LGD';
   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE  GTMP_IFRS_IMA_CURR';  
   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE  GTMP_IFRS_IMA_PREV'; 
   
  	V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_DEFAULT_LGD (DEFAULT_DATE , RULE_ID  , CUSTOMER_NUMBER,FACILITY_NUMBER, MASTERID,EIR,CCY, OUTSTANDING)
WITH CTE AS (
SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID  , RULE_ID ,
CUSTOMER_NUMBER , FACILITY_NUMBER ,EIR_AT_DEFAULT , CCY_AT_DEFAULT , OS_AT_DEFAULT,
ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY RULE_ID,MASTERID  ORDER BY DOWNLOAD_DATE) RN
FROM ' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A 
WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 fROM  GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.RULE_ID = X.DEFAULT_RULE_ID)
)
SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, RULE_ID ,CUSTOMER_NUMBER ,FACILITY_NUMBER ,MASTERID ,EIR_AT_DEFAULT , CCY_AT_DEFAULT , OS_AT_DEFAULT
FROM CTE 
WHERE RN = 1 
'; 
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
COMMIT;

 

V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_IMA_PREV (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, CCY, OUTSTANDING, PRC_TYPE)
	SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, CURRENCY, OUTSTANDING, ''LGD''
	FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A 
	WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_PREVDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND ACCOUNT_STATUS IN(''A'',''W'')
	AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_DEFAULT_LGD X WHERE A.MASTERID = X.MASTERID FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY)';
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
COMMIT;

V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_IMA_CURR (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, CCY, OUTSTANDING, PRC_TYPE)
	SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, CURRENCY, OUTSTANDING, ''LGD''
	FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A 
	WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND ACCOUNT_STATUS IN(''A'',''W'')
	AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_DEFAULT_LGD X WHERE A.MASTERID = X.MASTERID FETCH FIRST 1 ROW ONLY)';
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));


	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' (
	 DOWNLOAD_DATE
	 ,RULE_ID, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, FACILITY_NUMBER
	 ,MASTERID, CCY,REC_TYPE,SEQ
	 ,REC_OS
	 ,EQV_REC_OS
	 ,CREATEDBY
	 ,CREATEDDATE )
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
		,B.RULE_ID, B.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, B.FACILITY_NUMBER   
		,B.MASTERID , B.CCY, ''OS'' 
		,TRUNC(MONTHS_BETWEEN(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''),  B.DEFAULT_DATE))
		,C.OUTSTANDING - NVL(A.OUTSTANDING, 0) AS REC_OS    
		,(C.OUTSTANDING - NVL(A.OUTSTANDING, 0)) * E.RATE_AMOUNT AS EQV_REQ_OS     
		,''SP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DETAIL_1''   
		,SYSDATE
	FROM GTMP_IFRS_DEFAULT_LGD B    
		LEFT JOIN GTMP_IFRS_IMA_CURR A ON B.MASTERID = A.MASTERID     
		JOIN GTMP_IFRS_IMA_PREV C ON C.MASTERID = B.MASTERID      
		JOIN IFRS_MASTER_EXCHANGE_RATE E ON B.CCY = E.CURRENCY    
			AND E.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	WHERE B.DEFAULT_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_PREVDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	    

	-- DELETE REC OS = 0 & REC_OS_INT = 0
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' 
	WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE =  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	AND REC_OS <= 0 ';  
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
    -------- ====== BODY ======

    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_RESULT (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'X'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(22);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(32767);

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLELGDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_RESULT';
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));
	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN 
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_RESULT_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_HEADER_' || P_RUNID || '';
    ELSE 
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_RESULT';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_HEADER'; 
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT = 0 THEN
		 

        V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_RESULT WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
       END IF ;
    END IF;
	COMMIT;

	 EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG ';

     V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               WHERE LGD_METHOD = ''Expected Recovery'' AND IS_DELETED = 0  AND (  
	                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LGD)) IN ( 
	                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
	                   FROM DUAL
	                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
	                 )
	                 OR :p2 = 0 
	               )';
	 
	    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
	   
	    -------- ====== BODY ======
	-- Clear Session
    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
    V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
     WHERE  A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND EXISTS (sELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)	';
    END IF;
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;
   

   
	-- CALCULATE LGD RATE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1|| ' ( 
	 LGD_RULE_ID, 
	 EFF_DATE, 
	 UR, 
	 LGD,
	 CREATEDBY, 
	 CREATEDDATE)  
	SELECT A.LGD_RULE_ID, 
	 TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') EFF_DATE, 
	 NVL(A.UR,0) UR,  
	 1 - NVL(A.UR,0) LGD,
	 ''SP_IFRS_LGD_RESULT1'' AS CREATEDBY,
	 SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE 
	FROM ' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A  
	WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND EXISTS (sELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
	';

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

    -------- ====== BODY ======

    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-'; 
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AND (LGD_RULE_ID = ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' OR ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' = ''0'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
AS 
 
BEGIN
     
    
    MERGE INTO IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG a
    USING (
    
    	 SELECT * 
	 FROM (
	 
SELECT A."syscode_lgd_config" ,
	A."lgd_name", A."lgd_method", B.PKID AS SEGMENTATION_ID,
	"start_historical_date", "calculation_method", "historical_data",
	"workout_period", C.PKID AS DEFAULT_RULE_ID, NVL(A."is_deleted",1) AS IS_DELETED,
	ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY a."syscode_lgd_config" ORDER BY a."pkid" desc) RN
FROM "LgdConfiguration"@DBCONFIGLINK a 
	JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING b ON a."segment_code" = b.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION
	JOIN IFRS_DEFAULT_CRITERIA  C ON A."default_criteria_code" = c.SYSCODE_DEFAULT_CRITERIA ) x 
	WHERE x.rn = 1 
    ) b
    ON (a.SYSCODE_LGD = b."syscode_lgd_config" )  
    
      
    WHEN MATCHED THEN
        UPDATE SET   
            a.UPDATED_BY              = 'SP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG',
            a.UPDATED_DATE            = sysdate,
            a.IS_DELETED              = B.IS_DELETED 
    
    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
        INSERT (
            SYSCODE_LGD, 
		    LGD_RULE_NAME, 
		    LGD_METHOD, 
		    SEGMENTATION_ID, 
		    START_HISTORICAL_DATE, 
		    CALCULATION_METHOD, 
		    HISTORICAL_DATA, 
		    WORKOUT_PERIOD, 
		    DEFAULT_RULE_ID, 
		    IS_DELETED, 
		    CREATED_BY, 
		    CREATED_DATE)
        VALUES (
            b."syscode_lgd_config", b."lgd_name", b."lgd_method",
		b.segmentation_id, b."start_historical_date", b."calculation_method", b."historical_data", 
		b."workout_period", b.default_rule_id,   B.IS_DELETED,
		'SP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG',sysdate
        );
        
        commit;
     
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0', 
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'X'
) 
AUTHID CURRENT_USER
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE; 
	V_EOMDATE DATE ;  

	---- PROCESS
	V_COUNT NUMBER;
	V_RULE_ID VARCHAR2(10);
	V_ID NUMBER DEFAULT 0; 
	V_MAX_ID NUMBER DEFAULT 0; 
	V_DATADATE VARCHAR(20); 
    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY CLOB;
	V_STR_SQL_RULE CLOB;

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLELGDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);
 
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CASE 
        		WHEN CURRDATE = LAST_DAY(CURRDATE) THEN CURRDATE
        		ELSE LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(CURRDATE, -1))
    		END, LAST_DAY(CURRDATE)
        INTO V_CURRDATE,V_EOMDATE 
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;
 
 	IF V_CURRDATE = V_EOMDATE THEN   
 		V_TABLE_NAME := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY' ;
 	ELSE 
 		V_TABLE_NAME := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY';
 	END IF ;
 	 V_TABLELGDCONFIG := 'GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG';
 	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN 

        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE 

        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA'; 
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, 'SP_IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA', P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
	 
    V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG
               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG
               WHERE    IS_DELETED = 0 AND (  
                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_WORKOUT)) IN ( 
                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
                   FROM DUAL
                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
                 )
                 OR :p2 = ''0''
               )';
  DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
        

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
	----TABLE CONFIG
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1); 
        
		IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN 
		 V_STR_QUERY := '';
         V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
		END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
        
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'CREATE INDEX IDX_' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ON ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '(DOWNLOAD_DATE, RULE_ID , MASTERID)';
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
        
    V_STR_QUERY := 'TRUNCATE TABLE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1;
   
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY) ; 

	  
    
    V_STR_QUERY := 'SELECT MAX(PKID) 
	FROM IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING A 
	WHERE EXISTS (SELECT * FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE X.SEGMENTATION_ID = A.PKID) ';

    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY INTO V_MAX_ID;
    
    V_ID := 0 ;

    WHILE V_ID < V_MAX_ID LOOP
	    V_STR_QUERY := '
        SELECT MIN(PKID) 
		FROM IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING A 
		WHERE EXISTS (SELECT * FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE X.SEGMENTATION_ID = A.PKID) 
        AND A.PKID > :V_ID';

    	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY
        INTO V_ID
        USING V_ID;
		
    	V_STR_QUERY :=
        'SELECT PKID, MERGE_SQL_CONDITIONS, TO_CHAR(:dt, ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
         FROM IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING
         WHERE PKID = :x';

    	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY
        INTO V_RULE_ID, V_STR_SQL_RULE, V_DATADATE
        USING V_CURRDATE,V_ID;
    	
    	COMMIT;
        -----------------------------------------------------------------
        -- BUILD FINAL DYNAMIC SQL
        -----------------------------------------------------------------
        V_STR_QUERY :=
            'INSERT INTO ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' (' ||
            'DOWNLOAD_DATE, RULE_ID, MASTERID, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, FACILITY_NUMBER,' ||
			'ACCOUNT_STATUS,OUTSTANDING, ' ||
            'IMPAIRED_FLAG, LOAN_START_DATE, LOAN_DUE_DATE, CREATED_DATE, CREATED_BY) ' ||

            'SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, ' || V_RULE_ID || ', MASTERID, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, FACILITY_NUMBER,' ||
            'ACCOUNT_STATUS, OUTSTANDING, ' ||
            'IMPAIRED_FLAG, LOAN_START_DATE, LOAN_DUE_DATE, SYSDATE, ''SP_IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA'' ' ||
            'FROM ' || V_TABLE_NAME ||   
            ' IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT WHERE ACCOUNT_STATUS IN (''A'',''W'') ' ||
            '  AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || V_DATADATE || ''' ' ||
            '  AND (' || V_STR_SQL_RULE || ')';

     
       DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
         EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;

    END LOOP;
    
    
     

    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TABLEINSERT1;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_STR_QUERY := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_STR_QUERY, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA2 (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0', 
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'X'
) 
AUTHID CURRENT_USER
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE; 
	V_EOMDATE DATE ;  

	---- PROCESS
	V_COUNT NUMBER;
	V_RULE_ID VARCHAR2(10);
	V_ID NUMBER DEFAULT 0; 
	V_MAX_ID NUMBER DEFAULT 0; 
	V_DATADATE VARCHAR(20); 
    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY CLOB;
	V_STR_SQL_RULE CLOB;

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLELGDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);
 
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CASE 
        		WHEN CURRDATE = LAST_DAY(CURRDATE) THEN CURRDATE
        		ELSE LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(CURRDATE, -1))
    		END, LAST_DAY(CURRDATE)
        INTO V_CURRDATE,V_EOMDATE 
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;
 
 	IF V_CURRDATE = V_EOMDATE THEN   
 		V_TABLE_NAME := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY' ;
 	ELSE 
 		V_TABLE_NAME := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY';
 	END IF ;
 	 V_TABLELGDCONFIG := 'GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG';
 	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN 

        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE

    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, 'SP_IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA', P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
	 
    V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
               WHERE LGD_METHOD = ''Expected Recovery'' AND IS_DELETED = 0 AND (  
                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LGD)) IN ( 
                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
                   FROM DUAL
                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
                 )
                 OR :p2 = ''0''
               )';
  DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
        

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
	----TABLE CONFIG
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1); 
        
		IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN 
		 V_STR_QUERY := '';
         V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
		END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
        
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'CREATE INDEX IDX_' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ON ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '(DOWNLOAD_DATE, RULE_ID , MASTERID)';
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
        
    V_STR_QUERY := 'TRUNCATE TABLE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1;
   
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY) ; 

	  
    
    V_STR_QUERY := 'SELECT MAX(PKID) 
	FROM IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING A 
	WHERE EXISTS (SELECT * FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE X.SEGMENTATION_ID = A.PKID) ';

    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY INTO V_MAX_ID;
    
    V_ID := 0 ;

    WHILE V_ID < V_MAX_ID LOOP
	    V_STR_QUERY := '
        SELECT MIN(PKID) 
		FROM IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING A 
		WHERE EXISTS (SELECT * FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE X.SEGMENTATION_ID = A.PKID) 
        AND A.PKID > :V_ID';

    	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY
        INTO V_ID
        USING V_ID;

        'SELECT PKID, MERGE_SQL_CONDITIONS, TO_CHAR(:dt, ''YYYY-MM-DD'')

        USING V_CURRDATE,V_ID;
    	
    	COMMIT;
        -----------------------------------------------------------------

        -----------------------------------------------------------------

			'ACCOUNT_STATUS,OUTSTANDING, ' ||
            'IMPAIRED_FLAG, LOAN_START_DATE, LOAN_DUE_DATE, CREATED_DATE, CREATED_BY) ' ||

            'SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, ' || V_RULE_ID || ', MASTERID, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, FACILITY_NUMBER,' ||
            'ACCOUNT_STATUS, OUTSTANDING, ' ||
            'IMPAIRED_FLAG, LOAN_START_DATE, LOAN_DUE_DATE, SYSDATE, ''SP_IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA'' ' ||
            'FROM ' || V_TABLE_NAME ||   
            ' IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT WHERE ACCOUNT_STATUS IN (''A'',''W'') ' ||
            '  AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || V_DATADATE || ''' ' ||
            '  AND (' || V_STR_SQL_RULE || ')';

     
       DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(V_STR_QUERY);
         EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;

    END LOOP;
    
    
     

    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TABLEINSERT1;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA';

	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_STR_QUERY := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_STR_QUERY, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_UR_DETAIL (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'X'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(22);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(32767);

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLELGDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_UR_DETAIL';
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));
	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_DETAIL_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_DETAIL';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL'; 
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
 
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT = 0 THEN
		 V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_UR_DETAIL WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
		END IF;

        
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
 
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG ';

     V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               WHERE LGD_METHOD = ''Expected Recovery'' AND is_deleted = 0 and (  
	                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LGD)) IN ( 
	                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
	                   FROM DUAL
	                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
	                 )
	                 OR :p2 = 0 
	               )';
	 
	    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 

    -------- ====== BODY ======
	-- Clear Session
    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
    V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
     WHERE  A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND EXISTS (sELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)	';
    END IF;
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	-- End Clear Session
	   
   
	-- SUM TOTAL RECOVERY AND NPV RECOVERY
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ( 
	 EFF_DATE,
	 LGD_RULE_ID, 
	 DEFAULT_DATE,
	 FACILITY_NUMBER,
	 CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
	 MASTERID,
	 EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 EQV_REC_OS, 
	 --NPV_EQV_REC_OS, 
	 OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 REC_OS, 
	-- NPV_REC_OS, 
CCY, EXCHANGE_RATE,
	 CREATEDBY,
	 CREATEDDATE)  
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AS EFF_DATE, 
	 A.LGD_RULE_ID,  
	 A.DEFAULT_DATE,  
	 A.FACILITY_NUMBER,  
	 A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, 
	 A.MASTERID,  
	 MAX(A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT), 
	 MAX(A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT),  
	 SUM(A.EQV_REC_OS),  
	-- SUM(A.NPV_EQV_REC_OS) NPV_EQV_REC_OS, 
	 MAX(A.OS_AT_DEFAULT), 
	 SUM(A.REC_OS), 
	-- SUM(A.NPV_REC_OS) NPV_REC_OS, 
A.CCY, MAX(A.EXCHANGE_RATE),
	 ''SP_IFRS_LGD_UR_DETAIL1'' CREATEDBY,
	 SYSDATE CREATEDDATE 
	FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A  
	WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
	GROUP BY A.LGD_RULE_ID,   
	 A.DEFAULT_DATE,  
	 A.FACILITY_NUMBER,   
	 A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, 
	 A.MASTERID, A.CCY ';
	
    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;

    -------- ====== BODY ======

    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-'; 
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, nvl(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2 || ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AND (LGD_RULE_ID = ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' OR ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' = ''0'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_UR_HEADER (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'X'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(22);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(32767);

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLELGDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_UR_HEADER';
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));
	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_HEADER_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_DETAIL_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_HEADER';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_DETAIL'; 
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
 
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT = 0 THEN
		V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_UR_HEADER WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
		END IF;
 
    END IF;
	COMMIT;

	 EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG ';

     V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               WHERE LGD_METHOD = ''Expected Recovery'' AND IS_DELETED = 0  AND (  
	                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LGD)) IN ( 
	                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
	                   FROM DUAL
	                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
	                 )
	                 OR :p2 = 0 
	               )';
	 
	    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           
    -------- ====== BODY ======
	-- Clear Session
    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
    V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
     WHERE  A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	AND EXISTS (sELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)	';
    END IF;
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;


    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	-- End Clear Session
	
   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_UR_HEADER' ;
   
	-- SUM TOTAL RECOVERY AND NPV RECOVERY PER FACILITY_NUMBER (UNIQUE BY MASTERID/FACNO/CUSTNO)
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_UR_HEADER ( 
	 EFF_DATE,
	 LGD_RULE_ID, 
	 LGD_UNIQUE_ID,
	 EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 EQV_REC_OS ,
	-- NPV_EQV_REC_OS, 
	 OS_AT_DEFAULT , 
	 REC_OS --, 
	-- NPV_REC_OS 
) 
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AS EFF_DATE, 
	 A.LGD_RULE_ID,  
	 CASE B.CALCULATION_METHOD WHEN ''FAC'' THEN  A.FACILITY_NUMBER WHEN ''CUS'' THEN A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER ELSE A.MASTERID END,
	 SUM(A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT), 
	 SUM(A.EQV_REC_OS), 
	-- SUM(A.NPV_EQV_REC_OS), 
	 SUM(A.OS_AT_DEFAULT), 
	 SUM(A.REC_OS)
	-- SUM(A.NPV_REC_OS), 
	FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A 
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG B ON A.LGD_RULE_ID = B.PKID  
	WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	GROUP BY A.LGD_RULE_ID,  CASE B.CALCULATION_METHOD WHEN ''FAC'' THEN  A.FACILITY_NUMBER WHEN ''CUS'' THEN A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER ELSE A.MASTERID END ';

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));	

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;


	-- SUM TOTAL RECOVERY AND NPV RECOVERY PER AVERAGE METHOD (SIMPLE / WEIGHTED)
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ( 
	 EFF_DATE,
	 LGD_RULE_ID, 
	 EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 EQV_REC_OS, 
	-- NPV_EQV_REC_OS, 
	 OS_AT_DEFAULT , 
	 REC_OS , 
--	 NPV_REC_OS , 
	 UR,
	 CREATEDBY,
	 CREATEDDATE)  
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AS EFF_DATE,  
	 A.LGD_RULE_ID,  
	 SUM(A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT), 
	 SUM(A.EQV_REC_OS), 
	 --SUM(A.NPV_EQV_REC_OS), 
	 SUM(A.OS_AT_DEFAULT), 
	 SUM(A.REC_OS), 
	 --SUM(A.NPV_REC_OS), 
	 --CASE WHEN B.AVERAGE_METHOD = ''WEIGHTED''
	--  THEN  
	   CASE WHEN SUM(A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT)  = 0 THEN 0 
	    ELSE CAST (SUM(A.EQV_REC_OS)  AS FLOAT) / SUM(A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT)  
	 --  END
	--  ELSE AVG(CASE WHEN ((A.OS_AT_DEFAULT) + (A.OS_INT_AT_DEFAULT)) = 0 THEN 0 
	--    ELSE CAST (((A.NPV_REC_OS) + (A.NPV_REC_OS_INT)) AS FLOAT) / ((A.OS_AT_DEFAULT) + (A.OS_INT_AT_DEFAULT))
	--   END)
	 END UR,
	 ''SP_IFRS_LGD_UR_HEADER'' CREATEDBY,
	 SYSDATE CREATEDDATE
	FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_UR_HEADER A 
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG B ON A.LGD_RULE_ID = B.PKID
	WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	GROUP BY A.LGD_RULE_ID' ; -- B.AVERAGE_METHOD ';
 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));	

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== BODY ======

    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT2;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-'; 
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, nvl(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AND (LGD_RULE_ID = ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' OR ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' = ''0'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'x'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(22);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(32767);

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLELGDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL';
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));
	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA';
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA';  
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
 

	----TABLE PROCESS
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT =  0 THEN 
		 
        V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
       END IF ; 
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======

	 

   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
  
	 V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               WHERE LGD_METHOD = ''Expected Recovery'' AND IS_DELETED = 0  AND  (  
	                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LGD)) IN ( 
	                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
	                   FROM DUAL
	                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
	                 )
	                 OR :p2 = 0 
	               )';
	 
	    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
 
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL';
	 
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1';

    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
    V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE  EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
    AND A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    END IF;
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	-- End Clear Session

   
V_STR_QUERY := '
INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, LGD_SEGMENT_ID, LGD_RULE_ID, CCY, EXCHANGE_RATE)
WITH CTE AS (SELECT MIN(DEFAULT_DATE) DOWNLOAD_DATE,
	MASTERID, LGD_SEGMENT_ID, X.PKID LGD_RULE_ID, CURRENCY CCY
	FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A	
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X 
	ON  A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = X.SEGMENTATION_ID
	WHERE  A.DEFAULT_DATE BETWEEN LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''), -1*(X.HISTORICAL_DATA + X.WORKOUT_PERIOD))) 
	AND LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''), -1*(x.WORKOUT_PERIOD))) 
 	GROUP BY MASTERID, LGD_SEGMENT_ID,CURRENCY,X.PKID)
SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE, A.MASTERID, A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID, LGD_RULE_ID, A.CCY, B.RATE_AMOUNT 
FROM CTE A 
	JOIN IFRS_MASTER_EXCHANGE_RATE    B ON A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE  AND A.CCY = B.CURRENCY ' ; 
 
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	 

 

V_STR_QUERY := ' 	
INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1 (DOWNLOAD_DATE, LGD_SEGMENT_ID,LGD_RULE_ID,MASTERID, CCY,EXCHANGE_RATE)
WITH CTE AS(
