SELECT MAX(DOWNLOAD_DATE) DOWNLOAD_DATE,  LGD_SEGMENT_ID ,X.PKID LGD_RULE_ID  ,  MASTERID, CCY
	FROM IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA A 
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG x  
	ON X.SEGMENTATION_ID = A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID 
	 
	GROUP BY MASTERID ,CCY, LGD_SEGMENT_ID, X.PKID
)
SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE,A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID, A.LGD_RULE_ID , A.MASTERID,  A.CCY, B.RATE_AMOUNT 
FROM CTE A 
	JOIN IFRS_MASTER_EXCHANGE_RATE    B ON A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE  AND A.CCY = B.CURRENCY ' ; 
-- EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);

    
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO  GTMP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL (
	EFF_DATE, 
	 LGD_RULE_ID,
	 DEFAULT_DATE,
	 FACILITY_NUMBER,
	 CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
	 MASTERID,
	 EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 RECOVERY_DATE,
	 EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT,
	 EQV_REC_OS,
	 SUM_EQV_REC_OS,
	 OS_AT_DEFAULT,
	 REC_OS,
	 SUM_REC_OS,
CCY)
-- ,EXCHANGE_RATE)
/*
WITH CTE AS ( 
SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, CCY, MASTERID, EXCHANGE_RATE, LGD_RULE_ID
FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1 A 
UNION
SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, CCY, MASTERID, EXCHANGE_RATE, LGD_RULE_ID
FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 B
WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1 X WHERE B.MASTERID = X.MASTERID AND B.LGD_RULE_ID = X.LGD_RULE_ID)
)
*/
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') , C.PKID, 
	 A.DEFAULT_DATE,
	 A.FACILITY_NUMBER,
	 A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
	 A.MASTERID,
	 A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 B.DOWNLOAD_DATE AS RECOVERY_DATE,
	 A.EQV_AT_DEFAULT, -- A.OS_AT_DEFAULT * D.EXCHANGE_RATE ,
	 B.EQV_REC_OS,  --  NVL(B.REC_OS * D.EXCHANGE_RATE  ,0), 
	 --SUM(NVL(B.REC_OS * D.EXCHANGE_RATE  ,0)) OVER (PARTITION BY C.PKID, A.MASTERID ORDER BY B.DOWNLOAD_DATE), 
	SUM(NVL(B.EQV_REC_OS,0)) OVER (PARTITION BY C.PKID, A.MASTERID ORDER BY B.DOWNLOAD_DATE),  
	A.OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 NVL(B.REC_OS,0), 
	 SUM(NVL(B.REC_OS,0)) OVER (PARTITION BY C.PKID, A.MASTERID ORDER BY B.DOWNLOAD_DATE) , A.CURRENCY --, D.EXCHANGE_RATE
	FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A	
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG C ON A.LGD_sEGMENT_ID = C.SEGMENTATION_ID
	 LEFT JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT2 || ' B ON A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID AND B.DOWNLOAD_DATE BETWEEN LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(A.DEFAULT_DATE,1)) AND TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	 AND A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = B.LGD_SEGMENT_ID
 --JOIN CTE D ON A.MASTERID = D.MASTERID  AND C.PKID = D.LGD_RULE_ID
	WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 X WHERE A.MASTERID = X.MASTERID AND C.PKID = X.LGD_RULE_ID  AND A.DEFAULT_DATE = X.DOWNLOAD_DATE) ';
	
DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);

COMMIT;

 
	  
	-- CAP SUM_OS <= OS_AT_DEFAULT
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ( 
	 EFF_DATE,
	 LGD_RULE_ID, 
	 DEFAULT_DATE,
	 FACILITY_NUMBER,
	 CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
	 MASTERID,
	 EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 RECOVERY_DATE,
	 SEQ , 
	 EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 EQV_REC_OS, 
	 OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 REC_OS, 
CCY , -- EXCHANGE_RATE,
	 CREATEDBY,
	 CREATEDDATE)  
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AS EFF_DATE, 
	 A.LGD_RULE_ID,  
	 A.DEFAULT_DATE,  
	 A.FACILITY_NUMBER, 
	 A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, 
	 A.MASTERID,  
	 A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 A.RECOVERY_DATE,
	TRUNC(MONTHS_BETWEEN(a.RECOVERY_DATE, a.DEFAULT_DATE)),
	 A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 CASE 
	  WHEN A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT - A.SUM_EQV_REC_OS > 0 
	   THEN A.EQV_REC_OS
	  ELSE 
	   CASE 
	    WHEN A.SUM_EQV_REC_OS - A.EQV_REC_OS > A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT THEN 0 
	    ELSE A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT - (A.SUM_EQV_REC_OS - A.EQV_REC_OS) 
	   END
	 END EQV_REC_OS, 
	 A.OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 CASE 
	  WHEN A.OS_AT_DEFAULT - A.SUM_REC_OS > 0 
	   THEN A.REC_OS
	  ELSE 
	   CASE 
	    WHEN A.SUM_REC_OS - A.REC_OS > A.OS_AT_DEFAULT THEN 0 
	    ELSE A.OS_AT_DEFAULT - (A.SUM_REC_OS - A.REC_OS) 
	   END
	 END REC_OS, 
CCY, -- EXCHANGE_RATE,
	 ''SP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL1'' CREATEDBY,
	 SYSDATE CREATEDDATE
	FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL A ';


    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;
 
 
   /*
	-- CALCULATE NPV RECOVERY
	V_STR_QUERY := 'UPDATE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||  ' A SET  
	 	A.NPV_REC_OS = FUTIL_PV(  
		  (A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT / 12) / 100,   
		  MONTHS_BETWEEN(TO_DATE(A.DEFAULT_DATE, ''YYYY-MM-DD''), TO_DATE(NVL(A.RECOVERY_DATE, A.DEFAULT_DATE), ''YYYY-MM-DD'')),  
		  A.REC_OS),
		  A.NPV_EQV_REC_OS = FUTIL_PV(  
		  (A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT / 12) / 100,   
		  MONTHS_BETWEEN(TO_DATE(A.DEFAULT_DATE, ''YYYY-MM-DD''), TO_DATE(NVL(A.RECOVERY_DATE, A.DEFAULT_DATE), ''YYYY-MM-DD'')), 
		  A.EQV_REC_OS)  
		  WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
			AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)' ;
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;
	*/
 

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
   
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1; 
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AND (LGD_RULE_ID = ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' OR ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' = ''0'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL2 (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'x'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(22);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(32767);

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLELGDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL';
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));
	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL2_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA2_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA2_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL2';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA2';
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA2';  
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
 

	----TABLE PROCESS
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT =  0 THEN 
		 
        V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
       END IF ; 
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======

	 

   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
  
	 V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               WHERE LGD_METHOD = ''Expected Recovery'' AND IS_DELETED = 0  AND  (  
	                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LGD)) IN ( 
	                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
	                   FROM DUAL
	                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
	                 )
	                 OR :p2 = 0 
	               )';
	 
	    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
 
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL';
	 
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1';

    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
    V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE  EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
    AND A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    END IF;
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	-- End Clear Session

   
V_STR_QUERY := '
INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, LGD_RULE_ID, CCY, EXCHANGE_RATE)
WITH CTE AS (SELECT MIN(DEFAULT_DATE) DOWNLOAD_DATE,
	MASTERID, LGD_RULE_ID, CURRENCY CCY
	FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A	
	WHERE EXISTS (
	sELECT 1 
	FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X 
	WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID
	AND A.DEFAULT_DATE BETWEEN LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''), -1*(X.HISTORICAL_DATA + X.WORKOUT_PERIOD))) 
	AND LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''), -1*(x.WORKOUT_PERIOD)))) 
 	GROUP BY MASTERID, LGD_RULE_ID,CURRENCY)
SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE, A.MASTERID, A.LGD_RULE_ID, A.CCY, B.RATE_AMOUNT 
FROM CTE A 
	JOIN IFRS_MASTER_EXCHANGE_RATE    B ON A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE  AND A.CCY = B.CURRENCY ' ; 
 
 EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	 


V_STR_QUERY := ' 	
INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1 (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, CCY,EXCHANGE_RATE)
WITH CTE AS(
SELECT MAX(DOWNLOAD_DATE) DOWNLOAD_DATE,  MASTERID, CCY
	FROM ' || V_TABLESELECT2 || '  A 
	WHERE EXISTS (
	SELECT 1 
	FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 X 
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG Y ON X.LGD_RULE_ID  = Y.PKID
	WHERE X.MASTERID = A.MASTERID AND Y.DEFAULT_RULE_ID = A.RULE_ID
	FETCH FIRST 1 ROWS ONLY) 
	GROUP BY MASTERID ,CCY
)
SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE, A.MASTERID,  A.CCY, B.RATE_AMOUNT 
FROM CTE A 
	JOIN IFRS_MASTER_EXCHANGE_RATE    B ON A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE  AND A.CCY = B.CURRENCY ' ; 
 EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);

    
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO  GTMP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL (
	EFF_DATE, 
	 LGD_RULE_ID,
	 DEFAULT_DATE,
	 FACILITY_NUMBER,
	 CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
	 MASTERID,
	 EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 RECOVERY_DATE,
	 EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT,
	 EQV_REC_OS,
	 SUM_EQV_REC_OS,
	 OS_AT_DEFAULT,
	 REC_OS,
	 SUM_REC_OS,
CCY,
EXCHANGE_RATE)
WITH CTE AS (
SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, CCY, MASTERID, EXCHANGE_RATE
FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1 A 
UNION
SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, CCY, MASTERID, EXCHANGE_RATE
FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 B
WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1 X WHERE B.MASTERID = X.MASTERID)
)
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') , A.LGD_RULE_ID, 
	 A.DEFAULT_DATE,
	 A.FACILITY_NUMBER,
	 A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
	 A.MASTERID,
	 A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 B.DOWNLOAD_DATE AS RECOVERY_DATE,
	 A.OS_AT_DEFAULT * D.EXCHANGE_RATE ,
	  NVL(B.REC_OS * D.EXCHANGE_RATE  ,0), 
	 SUM(NVL(B.REC_OS * D.EXCHANGE_RATE  ,0)) OVER (PARTITION BY A.LGD_RULE_ID, A.MASTERID ORDER BY B.DOWNLOAD_DATE), 
	 A.OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 NVL(B.REC_OS,0), 
	 SUM(NVL(B.REC_OS,0)) OVER (PARTITION BY A.LGD_RULE_ID, A.MASTERID ORDER BY B.DOWNLOAD_DATE) , d.CCY, D.EXCHANGE_RATE
	FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A	
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG C ON A.LGD_RULE_ID = C.PKID
	 LEFT JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT2 || ' B ON A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID AND B.DOWNLOAD_DATE BETWEEN LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(A.DEFAULT_DATE,1)) AND TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	 AND C.DEFAULT_RULE_ID = B.RULE_ID
 JOIN CTE D ON A.MASTERID = D.MASTERID 
	WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 X WHERE A.MASTERID = X.MASTERID AND A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.LGD_RULE_ID  AND A.DEFAULT_DATE = X.DOWNLOAD_DATE)';
	
DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;


    
	  
	-- CAP SUM_OS <= OS_AT_DEFAULT
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ( 
	 EFF_DATE,
	 LGD_RULE_ID, 
	 DEFAULT_DATE,
	 FACILITY_NUMBER,
	 CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
	 MASTERID,
	 EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 RECOVERY_DATE,
	 SEQ , 
	 EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 EQV_REC_OS, 
	 OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 REC_OS, 
CCY, EXCHANGE_RATE,
	 CREATEDBY,
	 CREATEDDATE)  
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AS EFF_DATE, 
	 A.LGD_RULE_ID,  
	 A.DEFAULT_DATE,  
	 A.FACILITY_NUMBER, 
	 A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, 
	 A.MASTERID,  
	 A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 A.RECOVERY_DATE,
	TRUNC(MONTHS_BETWEEN(a.RECOVERY_DATE, a.DEFAULT_DATE)),
	 A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 CASE 
	  WHEN A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT - A.SUM_EQV_REC_OS > 0 
	   THEN A.EQV_REC_OS
	  ELSE 
	   CASE 
	    WHEN A.SUM_EQV_REC_OS - A.EQV_REC_OS > A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT THEN 0 
	    ELSE A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT - (A.SUM_EQV_REC_OS - A.EQV_REC_OS) 
	   END
	 END EQV_REC_OS, 
	 A.OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 CASE 
	  WHEN A.OS_AT_DEFAULT - A.SUM_REC_OS > 0 
	   THEN A.REC_OS
	  ELSE 
	   CASE 
	    WHEN A.SUM_REC_OS - A.REC_OS > A.OS_AT_DEFAULT THEN 0 
	    ELSE A.OS_AT_DEFAULT - (A.SUM_REC_OS - A.REC_OS) 
	   END
	 END REC_OS, 
CCY, EXCHANGE_RATE,
	 ''SP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL1'' CREATEDBY,
	 SYSDATE CREATEDDATE
	FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL A ';


    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;
 
 
   /*
	-- CALCULATE NPV RECOVERY
	V_STR_QUERY := 'UPDATE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||  ' A SET  
	 	A.NPV_REC_OS = FUTIL_PV(  
		  (A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT / 12) / 100,   
		  MONTHS_BETWEEN(TO_DATE(A.DEFAULT_DATE, ''YYYY-MM-DD''), TO_DATE(NVL(A.RECOVERY_DATE, A.DEFAULT_DATE), ''YYYY-MM-DD'')),  
		  A.REC_OS),
		  A.NPV_EQV_REC_OS = FUTIL_PV(  
		  (A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT / 12) / 100,   
		  MONTHS_BETWEEN(TO_DATE(A.DEFAULT_DATE, ''YYYY-MM-DD''), TO_DATE(NVL(A.RECOVERY_DATE, A.DEFAULT_DATE), ''YYYY-MM-DD'')), 
		  A.EQV_REC_OS)  
		  WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
			AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)' ;
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;
	*/
 

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
   
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1; 
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AND (LGD_RULE_ID = ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' OR ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' = ''0'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'x'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(1000);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(32767);

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLELGDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL';
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));
	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA';
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA';  
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
 
 

	----TABLE PROCESS
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT =  0 THEN 
		 
        V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
       END IF ; 
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======



   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
  
	 V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG
	               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG
	               WHERE  IS_DELETED = 0  AND  (  
	                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_WORKOUT)) IN ( 
	                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
	                   FROM DUAL
	                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
	                 )
	                 OR :p2 = ''0'' 
	               )';
	 
	    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
 
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1';
	 

    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
    V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE  EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
    AND A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    END IF;
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	-- End Clear Session
  
   


V_STR_QUERY := '
INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, LGD_SEGMENT_ID, CCY, EXCHANGE_RATE)
WITH CTE AS (SELECT MIN(DEFAULT_DATE) DOWNLOAD_DATE,
	MASTERID, A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID, CURRENCY CCY
	FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG B ON 
	A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = B.SEGMENTATION_ID
	AND A.DEFAULT_DATE BETWEEN LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''), -1*(B.HISTORICAL_DATA ))) 
	AND  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 	
	GROUP BY MASTERID, A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID ,CURRENCY)
SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE, A.MASTERID, A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID, A.CCY, B.RATE_AMOUNT 
FROM CTE A 
	JOIN IFRS_MASTER_EXCHANGE_RATE    B ON A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE  AND A.CCY = B.CURRENCY ' ; 
 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
 EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);


V_STR_QUERY := ' 	
INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1 (DOWNLOAD_DATE, LGD_SEGMENT_ID,MASTERID, CCY,EXCHANGE_RATE)
WITH CTE AS(
SELECT MAX(DOWNLOAD_DATE) DOWNLOAD_DATE,  LGD_SEGMENT_ID, MASTERID, CCY
	FROM IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA A 
	WHERE EXISTS (
	SELECT 1 
	FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG x  
	WHERE X.SEGMENTATION_ID = A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID 
	FETCH FIRST 1 ROWS ONLY) 
	GROUP BY MASTERID ,CCY, LGD_SEGMENT_ID
)
SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE,A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID, A.MASTERID,  A.CCY, B.RATE_AMOUNT 
FROM CTE A 
	JOIN IFRS_MASTER_EXCHANGE_RATE    B ON A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE  AND A.CCY = B.CURRENCY ' ; 
 EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	

	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO  GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL (
	EFF_DATE, 
	 WORKOUT_RULE_ID,
	 DEFAULT_DATE,
	 FACILITY_NUMBER,
	 CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
	 MASTERID,
	 EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 RECOVERY_DATE,
	 EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT,
	 EQV_REC_OS,
	 SUM_EQV_REC_OS,
	 OS_AT_DEFAULT,
	 REC_OS,
	 SUM_REC_OS,
CCY,
EXCHANGE_RATE)
WITH CTE AS (
SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, CCY, MASTERID, EXCHANGE_RATE, LGD_SEGMENT_ID
FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1 A 
UNION
SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, CCY, MASTERID, EXCHANGE_RATE, LGD_SEGMENT_ID
FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 B
WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1 X WHERE B.MASTERID = X.MASTERID AND B.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = X.LGD_SEGMENT_ID)
)
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') , C.PKID WORKOUT_RULE_ID, 
	 A.DEFAULT_DATE,
	 A.FACILITY_NUMBER,
	 A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
	 A.MASTERID,
	 A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 B.DOWNLOAD_DATE AS RECOVERY_DATE,
	 A.OS_AT_DEFAULT * D.EXCHANGE_RATE ,
	  NVL(B.REC_OS * D.EXCHANGE_RATE  ,0), 
	 SUM(NVL(B.REC_OS * D.EXCHANGE_RATE  ,0)) OVER (PARTITION BY A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID, A.MASTERID ORDER BY B.DOWNLOAD_DATE), 
	 A.OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 NVL(B.REC_OS,0), 
	 SUM(NVL(B.REC_OS,0)) OVER (PARTITION BY A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID, A.MASTERID ORDER BY B.DOWNLOAD_DATE) , d.CCY, D.EXCHANGE_RATE
	FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A	
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG C ON A.LGD_sEGMENT_ID = C.SEGMENTATION_ID
	 LEFT JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT2 || ' B ON A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID 
		AND A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = B.LGD_SEGMENT_ID
		AND B.DOWNLOAD_DATE BETWEEN LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(A.DEFAULT_DATE,1)) AND TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	  JOIN CTE D ON A.MASTERID = D.MASTERID AND A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = D.LGD_SEGMENT_ID
	WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 X WHERE A.MASTERID = X.MASTERID AND A.LGD_SEGMENT_ID = X.LGD_SEGMENT_ID  AND A.DEFAULT_DATE = X.DOWNLOAD_DATE)
		';
DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;


    
	  
	-- CAP SUM_OS <= OS_AT_DEFAULT
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ( 
	 EFF_DATE,
	 WORKOUT_RULE_ID, 
	 DEFAULT_DATE,
	 FACILITY_NUMBER,
	 CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
	 MASTERID,
	 EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 RECOVERY_DATE,
	 SEQ , 
	 EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 EQV_REC_OS, 
	 OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 REC_OS, 
CCY, EXCHANGE_RATE,
	 CREATEDBY,
	 CREATEDDATE)  
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AS EFF_DATE, 
	 A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID,  
	 A.DEFAULT_DATE,  
	 A.FACILITY_NUMBER, 
	 A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, 
	 A.MASTERID,  
	 A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 A.RECOVERY_DATE,
	TRUNC(MONTHS_BETWEEN(a.RECOVERY_DATE, a.DEFAULT_DATE)),
	 A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 CASE 
	  WHEN A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT - A.SUM_EQV_REC_OS > 0 
	   THEN A.EQV_REC_OS
	  ELSE 
	   CASE 
	    WHEN A.SUM_EQV_REC_OS - A.EQV_REC_OS > A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT THEN 0 
	    ELSE A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT - (A.SUM_EQV_REC_OS - A.EQV_REC_OS) 
	   END
	 END EQV_REC_OS, 
	 A.OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 CASE 
	  WHEN A.OS_AT_DEFAULT - A.SUM_REC_OS > 0 
	   THEN A.REC_OS
	  ELSE 
	   CASE 
	    WHEN A.SUM_REC_OS - A.REC_OS > A.OS_AT_DEFAULT THEN 0 
	    ELSE A.OS_AT_DEFAULT - (A.SUM_REC_OS - A.REC_OS) 
	   END
	 END REC_OS,  CCY, EXCHANGE_RATE,
	 ''SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL1'' CREATEDBY,
	 SYSDATE CREATEDDATE
	FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL A ';


    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;
 
  
 

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
   
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1; 
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AND (WORKOUT_RULE_ID = ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' OR ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' = ''0'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL2 (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'x'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(22);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(32767);

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLELGDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL';
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));
	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_DATA';
        V_TABLESELECT2 := 'IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA';  
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
 

	----TABLE PROCESS
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT =  0 THEN 
		 
        V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
       END IF ; 
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======



   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
  
	 V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               WHERE LGD_METHOD = ''Expected Recovery'' AND IS_DELETED = 0  AND  (  
	                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LGD)) IN ( 
	                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
	                   FROM DUAL
	                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
	                 )
	                 OR :p2 = 0 
	               )';
	 
	    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
 
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1';
	 

    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
    V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE  EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
    AND A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    END IF;
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	-- End Clear Session

 

V_STR_QUERY := '
INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, LGD_RULE_ID, CCY, EXCHANGE_RATE)
WITH CTE AS (SELECT MIN(DEFAULT_DATE) DOWNLOAD_DATE,
	MASTERID, LGD_RULE_ID, CURRENCY CCY
	FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A	
	WHERE EXISTS (
	sELECT 1 
	FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X 
	WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID
	AND A.DEFAULT_DATE BETWEEN LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''), -1*(X.HISTORICAL_DATA ))) 
	AND  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')) 
 	GROUP BY MASTERID, LGD_RULE_ID,CURRENCY)
SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE, A.MASTERID, A.LGD_RULE_ID, A.CCY, B.RATE_AMOUNT 
FROM CTE A 
	JOIN IFRS_MASTER_EXCHANGE_RATE    B ON A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE  AND A.CCY = B.CURRENCY ' ; 
 
 EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	 


V_STR_QUERY := ' 	
INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1 (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, CCY,EXCHANGE_RATE)
WITH CTE AS(
SELECT MAX(DOWNLOAD_DATE) DOWNLOAD_DATE,  MASTERID, CCY
	FROM IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA A 
	WHERE EXISTS (
	SELECT 1 
	FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 X 
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG Y ON X.LGD_RULE_ID  = Y.PKID
	WHERE X.MASTERID = A.MASTERID AND Y.DEFAULT_RULE_ID = A.RULE_ID
	FETCH FIRST 1 ROWS ONLY) 
	GROUP BY MASTERID ,CCY
)
SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE, A.MASTERID,  A.CCY, B.RATE_AMOUNT 
FROM CTE A 
	JOIN IFRS_MASTER_EXCHANGE_RATE    B ON A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = B.DOWNLOAD_DATE  AND A.CCY = B.CURRENCY ' ; 
 EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	

	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO  GTMP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL (
	EFF_DATE, 
	 LGD_RULE_ID,
	 DEFAULT_DATE,
	 FACILITY_NUMBER,
	 CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
	 MASTERID,
	 EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 RECOVERY_DATE,
	 EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT,
	 EQV_REC_OS,
	 SUM_EQV_REC_OS,
	 OS_AT_DEFAULT,
	 REC_OS,
	 SUM_REC_OS,
CCY,
EXCHANGE_RATE)
WITH CTE AS (
SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, CCY, MASTERID, EXCHANGE_RATE
FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1 A 
UNION
SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, CCY, MASTERID, EXCHANGE_RATE
FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 B
WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA1 X WHERE B.MASTERID = X.MASTERID)
)
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') , A.LGD_RULE_ID, 
	 A.DEFAULT_DATE,
	 A.FACILITY_NUMBER,
	 A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
	 A.MASTERID,
	 A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 B.DOWNLOAD_DATE AS RECOVERY_DATE,
	 A.OS_AT_DEFAULT * D.EXCHANGE_RATE ,
	  NVL(B.REC_OS * D.EXCHANGE_RATE  ,0), 
	 SUM(NVL(B.REC_OS * D.EXCHANGE_RATE  ,0)) OVER (PARTITION BY A.LGD_RULE_ID, A.MASTERID ORDER BY B.DOWNLOAD_DATE), 
	 A.OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 NVL(B.REC_OS,0), 
	 SUM(NVL(B.REC_OS,0)) OVER (PARTITION BY A.LGD_RULE_ID, A.MASTERID ORDER BY B.DOWNLOAD_DATE) , d.CCY, D.EXCHANGE_RATE
	FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A	
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG C ON A.LGD_RULE_ID = C.PKID
	 LEFT JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT2 || ' B ON A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID AND B.DOWNLOAD_DATE BETWEEN LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(A.DEFAULT_DATE,1)) AND TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	 AND C.DEFAULT_RULE_ID = B.RULE_ID
	  JOIN CTE D ON A.MASTERID = D.MASTERID 
	WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_DATA1 X WHERE A.MASTERID = X.MASTERID AND A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.LGD_RULE_ID  AND A.DEFAULT_DATE = X.DOWNLOAD_DATE)
		';
DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;


    
	  
	-- CAP SUM_OS <= OS_AT_DEFAULT
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || '
	INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ( 
	 EFF_DATE,
	 WORKOUT_RULE_ID, 
	 DEFAULT_DATE,
	 FACILITY_NUMBER,
	 CUSTOMER_NUMBER,
	 MASTERID,
	 EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 RECOVERY_DATE,
	 SEQ , 
	 EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 EQV_REC_OS, 
	 OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 REC_OS, 
CCY, EXCHANGE_RATE,
	 CREATEDBY,
	 CREATEDDATE)  
	SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AS EFF_DATE, 
	 A.LGD_RULE_ID,  
	 A.DEFAULT_DATE,  
	 A.FACILITY_NUMBER, 
	 A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, 
	 A.MASTERID,  
	 A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT,
	 A.RECOVERY_DATE,
	TRUNC(MONTHS_BETWEEN(a.RECOVERY_DATE, a.DEFAULT_DATE)),
	 A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 CASE 
	  WHEN A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT - A.SUM_EQV_REC_OS > 0 
	   THEN A.EQV_REC_OS
	  ELSE 
	   CASE 
	    WHEN A.SUM_EQV_REC_OS - A.EQV_REC_OS > A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT THEN 0 
	    ELSE A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT - (A.SUM_EQV_REC_OS - A.EQV_REC_OS) 
	   END
	 END EQV_REC_OS, 
	 A.OS_AT_DEFAULT, 
	 CASE 
	  WHEN A.OS_AT_DEFAULT - A.SUM_REC_OS > 0 
	   THEN A.REC_OS
	  ELSE 
	   CASE 
	    WHEN A.SUM_REC_OS - A.REC_OS > A.OS_AT_DEFAULT THEN 0 
	    ELSE A.OS_AT_DEFAULT - (A.SUM_REC_OS - A.REC_OS) 
	   END
	 END REC_OS,  CCY, EXCHANGE_RATE,
	 ''SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL1'' CREATEDBY,
	 SYSDATE CREATEDDATE
	FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_UR_REC_DETAIL A ';


    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;
 
 
   /*
	-- CALCULATE NPV RECOVERY
	V_STR_QUERY := 'UPDATE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||  ' A SET  
	 	A.NPV_REC_OS = FUTIL_PV(  
		  (A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT / 12) / 100,   
		  MONTHS_BETWEEN(TO_DATE(A.DEFAULT_DATE, ''YYYY-MM-DD''), TO_DATE(NVL(A.RECOVERY_DATE, A.DEFAULT_DATE), ''YYYY-MM-DD'')),  
		  A.REC_OS),
		  A.NPV_EQV_REC_OS = FUTIL_PV(  
		  (A.EIR_AT_DEFAULT / 12) / 100,   
		  MONTHS_BETWEEN(TO_DATE(A.DEFAULT_DATE, ''YYYY-MM-DD''), TO_DATE(NVL(A.RECOVERY_DATE, A.DEFAULT_DATE), ''YYYY-MM-DD'')), 
		  A.EQV_REC_OS)  
		  WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
			AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)' ;
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;
	*/
 

 

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
   
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1; 
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AND (LGD_RULE_ID = ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' OR ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' = ''0'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_HEADER (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'x'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(1000);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(32767);

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLELGDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_HEADER';
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));
	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_HEADER_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_HEADER';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL'; 
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
 

	----TABLE PROCESS
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT =  0 THEN 
		 
        V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_HEADER WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
       END IF ; 
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======

	 

   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
  
	 V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG
	               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG
	               WHERE  IS_DELETED = 0  AND  (  
	                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_WORKOUT)) IN ( 
	                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
	                   FROM DUAL
	                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
	                 )
	                 OR :p2 = ''0'' 
	               )';
	 
	    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
  
	 

    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
    V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE  EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
    AND A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    END IF;
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	-- End Clear Session

   

   
	-- POPULATE RECOVERY FROM DEFAULT ACCOUNTS
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := 
'INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ( 
    EFF_DATE,
    WORKOUT_RULE_ID,
    EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT,
    SEQ,
    EQV_REC_OS,
    CUM_REC_OS,
    MARGINAL_REC,
    CUM_REC,
    CREATEDBY,
    CREATEDDATE
) 
WITH cte AS (
SELECT EFF_DATE,WORKOUT_RULE_ID , MASTERID ,MAX(EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT)EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT  
FROM '   || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A	
WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
    AND A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
GROUP BY EFF_DATE,WORKOUT_RULE_ID ,MASTERID
),
cte2 AS (
SELECT EFF_DATE, WORKOUT_RULE_ID ,SUM(EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT)EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT  
FROM  CTE
GROUP BY EFF_DATE ,WORKOUT_RULE_ID 
),
 CTE_SEQ(EFF_DATE, WORKOUT_RULE_ID, SEQ,MAXSEQ) AS (
   SELECT EFF_DATE, WORKOUT_RULE_ID , 1 SEQ ,MAX(SEQ )MAXSEQ 
	FROM '   || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A	 
	WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
	    AND A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	GROUP BY EFF_DATE,WORKOUT_RULE_ID 
    UNION ALL 
   SELECT EFF_DATE, WORKOUT_RULE_ID , SEQ+1 ,MAXSEQ
   FROM CTE_SEQ
   WHERE SEQ < MAXSEQ
),
CTE3 AS (
SELECT B.EFF_DATE, B.WORKOUT_RULE_ID ,B.SEQ ,sum(NVL(A.EQV_REC_OS,0))EQV_REC_OS  
FROM '   || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A	
	RIGHT JOIN CTE_SEQ B ON A.SEQ = B.SEQ AND A.EFF_DATE = B.EFF_DATE AND A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID = B.WORKOUT_RULE_ID
WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE B.WORKOUT_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
    AND B.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
GROUP BY B.EFF_DATE,B.WORKOUT_RULE_ID ,B.SEQ 
)
,CTE4 AS (
SELECT A.EFF_DATE, A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID, A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, B.SEQ, B.EQV_REC_OS,
	SUM(B.EQV_REC_OS) OVER (PARTITION BY A.EFF_DATE, A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID ORDER BY B.SEQ) AS MARGINAL_REC_OS
FROM CTE2 A 
	JOIN CTE3 B ON A.EFF_DATE = B.EFF_DATE AND A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID = B.WORKOUT_RULE_ID)

SELECT   A.EFF_DATE, A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID, A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, A.SEQ, A.EQV_REC_OS,
	A.MARGINAL_REC_OS,
	EQV_REC_OS / EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT AS MARGINAL_REC, 
	MARGINAL_REC_OS/EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT AS CUM_REC,
	''SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_HEADER'',
	SYSDATE
FROM CTE4 A 
ORDER BY  EFF_DATE,  WORKOUT_RULE_ID,  SEQ 
	';
	
	
	 
DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;


     
   
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1; 
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AND (WORKOUT_RULE_ID = ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' OR ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' = ''0'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_HEADER2 (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'x'
) 
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE;
    V_PREVDATE DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID VARCHAR2(22);
	V_COUNT NUMBER;

    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY VARCHAR2(32767);

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLELGDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_HEADER';
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- RESULT
    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
        INTO V_CURRDATE
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');
	V_PREVDATE := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(V_CURRDATE, - 1));
	
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_HEADER_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_HEADER';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_DETAIL'; 
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
 

	----TABLE PROCESS
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1);
        
		IF V_COUNT =  0 THEN 
		 
        V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_HEADER WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
       END IF ; 
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======

	 

   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
  
	 V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG
	               WHERE LGD_METHOD = ''Expected Recovery'' AND IS_DELETED = 0  AND  (  
	                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LGD)) IN ( 
	                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
	                   FROM DUAL
	                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
	                 )
	                 OR :p2 = 0 
	               )';
	 
	    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
  
	 

    IF V_MODEL_ID = '0' THEN 
    V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    ELSE
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
    V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DELETE FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' A
    WHERE  EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LGD_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
    AND A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    END IF;
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
    COMMIT;

    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	-- End Clear Session

   

   
	-- POPULATE RECOVERY FROM DEFAULT ACCOUNTS
	V_STR_QUERY := '';
	V_STR_QUERY := 
'INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ( 
    EFF_DATE,
    WORKOUT_RULE_ID,
    EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT,
    SEQ,
    EQV_REC_OS,
    CUM_REC_OS,
    MARGINAL_REC,
    CUM_REC,
    CREATEDBY,
    CREATEDDATE
) 
WITH cte AS (
SELECT EFF_DATE,WORKOUT_RULE_ID , MASTERID ,MAX(EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT)EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT  
FROM '   || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A	
WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
    AND A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
GROUP BY EFF_DATE,WORKOUT_RULE_ID ,MASTERID
),
cte2 AS (
SELECT EFF_DATE, WORKOUT_RULE_ID ,SUM(EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT)EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT  
FROM  CTE
GROUP BY EFF_DATE ,WORKOUT_RULE_ID 
),
 CTE_SEQ(EFF_DATE, WORKOUT_RULE_ID, SEQ,MAXSEQ) AS (
   SELECT EFF_DATE, WORKOUT_RULE_ID , 1 SEQ ,MAX(SEQ )MAXSEQ 
	FROM '   || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A	 
	WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
	    AND A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	GROUP BY EFF_DATE,WORKOUT_RULE_ID 
    UNION ALL 
   SELECT EFF_DATE, WORKOUT_RULE_ID , SEQ+1 ,MAXSEQ
   FROM CTE_SEQ
   WHERE SEQ < MAXSEQ
),
CTE3 AS (
SELECT B.EFF_DATE, B.WORKOUT_RULE_ID ,B.SEQ ,sum(NVL(A.EQV_REC_OS,0))EQV_REC_OS  
FROM '   || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' A	
	RIGHT JOIN CTE_SEQ B ON A.SEQ = B.SEQ AND A.EFF_DATE = B.EFF_DATE AND A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID = B.WORKOUT_RULE_ID
WHERE EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LGD_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE B.WORKOUT_RULE_ID = X.PKID)
    AND B.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
GROUP BY B.EFF_DATE,B.WORKOUT_RULE_ID ,B.SEQ 
)
,CTE4 AS (
SELECT A.EFF_DATE, A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID, A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, B.SEQ, B.EQV_REC_OS,
	SUM(B.EQV_REC_OS) OVER (PARTITION BY A.EFF_DATE, A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID ORDER BY B.SEQ) AS MARGINAL_REC_OS
FROM CTE2 A 
	JOIN CTE3 B ON A.EFF_DATE = B.EFF_DATE AND A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID = B.WORKOUT_RULE_ID)

SELECT   A.EFF_DATE, A.WORKOUT_RULE_ID, A.EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT, A.SEQ, A.EQV_REC_OS,
	A.MARGINAL_REC_OS,
	EQV_REC_OS / EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT AS MARGINAL_REC, 
	MARGINAL_REC_OS/EQV_OS_AT_DEFAULT AS CUM_REC,
	''SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_HEADER'',
	SYSDATE
FROM CTE4 A 
ORDER BY  EFF_DATE,  WORKOUT_RULE_ID,  SEQ 
	';
	
	
	 
DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
	COMMIT;


     
   
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1; 
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') AND (LGD_RULE_ID = ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' OR ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' = ''0'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG
AS 
 
BEGIN
     
    MERGE INTO IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG a
    USING (
    
    	 SELECT * 
	 FROM (
	 

SELECT a."workout_period_configuration_name",A."syscode_workout_period_config" ,
	B.PKID AS SEGMENTATION_ID, 
	a."start_period",  a."historical_month",
	NVL(A."is_deleted",0) AS IS_DELETED,
	ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY a."syscode_workout_period_config" ORDER BY a."pkid" desc) RN
	FROM "NTT_PSAK413_IMPAIRMENT"."WorkoutPeriodConfiguration"@DBCONFIGLINK a 
	JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING b ON a."segment_code" = b.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION  ) x 
	WHERE x.rn = 1 
    ) b
    ON (a.SYSCODE_workout = b."syscode_workout_period_config" )  
    WHEN MATCHED THEN
        UPDATE SET   
            a.UPDATED_BY              = 'SP_IFRS_LGD_WORKOUT_RULES_CONFIG',
            a.UPDATED_DATE            = sysdate,
            a.IS_DELETED              = B.IS_DELETED
    
    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
        INSERT ( 
		    syscode_workout,
		    workout_rule_name,
		    segmentation_id,
		    historical_month,
		    start_period,
		    is_deleted,
		      created_by ,
		    created_date
		  
		    )
        VALUES (
            b."syscode_workout_period_config",b."workout_period_configuration_name" ,
		b.SEGMENTATION_ID, 
	b."historical_month", b."start_period",     B.IS_DELETED,
		'SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG',sysdate
        );
        
        commit;
     
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_DATA (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0', 
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
) 
AUTHID CURRENT_USER
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE; 
	V_EOMDATE DATE ;  

	---- PROCESS
	V_COUNT NUMBER;
	V_RULE_ID VARCHAR2(10);
	V_ID NUMBER DEFAULT 0; 
	V_MAX_ID NUMBER DEFAULT 0; 
	V_DATADATE VARCHAR(20); 
    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY CLOB;
	V_STR_SQL_RULE CLOB;

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLECONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);
 
BEGIN
   
	
    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_DATA';
    V_DATADATE := TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD');
    
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CASE 
        		WHEN CURRDATE = LAST_DAY(CURRDATE) THEN CURRDATE
        		ELSE LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(CURRDATE, -1))
    		END, LAST_DAY(CURRDATE)
        INTO V_CURRDATE,V_EOMDATE 
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;
  
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN 
        V_TABLECONFIG := 'GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_RULE_DATA_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    	 	V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_DATA_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE 
        V_TABLECONFIG := 'GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_RULE_DATA'; 
    	 	V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_DATA' ; 
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
	----TABLE CONFIG
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1); 
        
		IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN 
		 V_STR_QUERY := '';
         V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
		END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '
		 AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LIFETIME_DATA  A 
		WHERE EXISTS (SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LIFETIME_RULE_ID = X.PKID)    ';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
        COMMIT ;
        
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'CREATE INDEX IDX_' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ON ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '(LIFETIME_RULE_ID , MASTERID)';
  
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
        
 EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
	 
    V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG
               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG
               WHERE  IS_DELETED = 0 AND START_HISTORICAL_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
				AND (  
                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LIFETIME)) IN ( 
                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
                   FROM DUAL
                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
                 )
                 OR :p2 = 0 
               )'; 
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;

   	V_STR_QUERY := 
	'DELETE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' A  
	 WHERE    LAST_DAY(LIFETIME_START_DATE) = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')  
AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG  X WHERE A.LIFETIME_RULE_ID = X.PKID) ' ; 
	
	
	
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;

COMMIT; 
	
   
	V_STR_QUERY := 
	'UPDATE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' A  SET ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A'' , CLOSE_DATE = NULL  ' || 
	' WHERE    CLOSE_DATE >= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')  AND ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''C''  
AND EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG  X WHERE A.LIFETIME_RULE_ID = X.PKID) ' ; 
	
	
	
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;

COMMIT; 
	 
	V_STR_QUERY :=
    'INSERT INTO  ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' (' ||
    '  LIFETIME_START_DATE, LIFETIME_RULE_ID, FACILITY_NUMBER, MASTERID, ' ||
    '  CUSTOMER_NUMBER, LOAN_START_DATE, LOAN_DUE_DATE, CLOSE_DATE, ' ||
    '  ACCOUNT_STATUS, CREATED_BY, CREATED_DATE' ||
    ') ' ||
    'SELECT ' ||
    '  A.LOAN_DUE_DATE, B.PKID , A.FACILITY_NUMBER, A.MASTERID, ' ||
    '  A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, A.LOAN_START_DATE, A.LOAN_DUE_DATE, NULL, ' ||
    '  A.ACCOUNT_STATUS, ''' || V_SPNAME || ''', SYSDATE ' ||
    'FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' ' || ' A ' ||
    ' JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG B ON A.RULE_ID = B.SEGMENTATION_ID ' || 
	' WHERE A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A'' ' ||
    '  AND LAST_DAY(A.LOAN_DUE_DATE) = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ' ||
    '  AND NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || 
    ' X WHERE  B.PKID = X.LIFETIME_RULE_ID AND A.MASTERID = X.MASTERID)  ' ; 
	

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
COMMIT ;

	V_STR_QUERY := 
	'UPDATE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' A SET A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''C'' , A.CLOSE_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')   ' || 
	' WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' X 
	JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG Y ON X.RULE_ID = Y.SEGMENTATION_ID 
	WHERE A.MASTERID = X.MASTERID AND  Y.PKID = A.LIFETIME_RULE_ID)
	AND A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A''
	AND A.LIFETIME_START_DATE <=  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ' ;
	

	
 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
COMMIT; 

    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TABLEINSERT1;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_STR_QUERY := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE LIFETIME_START_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_STR_QUERY, V_SPNAME, nvl(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_DETAIL (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0', 
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'x'
) 
AUTHID CURRENT_USER
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE; 
	V_EOMDATE DATE ;  

	---- PROCESS
	V_COUNT NUMBER;
	V_RULE_ID VARCHAR2(10);
	V_ID NUMBER DEFAULT 0; 
	V_MAX_ID NUMBER DEFAULT 0; 
	V_DATADATE VARCHAR(20); 
    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY CLOB;
	V_STR_SQL_RULE CLOB;

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLECONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);
 
BEGIN
   
	
    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_DETAIL';
    V_DATADATE := TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD');
    
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CASE 
        		WHEN CURRDATE = LAST_DAY(CURRDATE) THEN CURRDATE
        		ELSE LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(CURRDATE, -1))
    		END, LAST_DAY(CURRDATE)
        INTO V_CURRDATE,V_EOMDATE 
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;
  
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN 
        V_TABLECONFIG := 'GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG_' || P_RUNID || '';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_DATA_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    	 	V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_DETAIL_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE 
        V_TABLECONFIG := 'GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG';
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_DATA'; 
    	 	V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_DETAIL' ; 
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
	----TABLE CONFIG
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1); 
        
		IF V_COUNT = 0 THEN 
		  V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '
		 AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LIFETIME_DETAIL  A 
		WHERE EXISTS (SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLECONFIG || ' X WHERE A.LIFETIME_RULE_ID = X.PKID)    ';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
		END IF;

        
        COMMIT ;
        
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'CREATE INDEX IDX_' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ON ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '(EFF_DATE,LIFETIME_RULE_ID )';
  
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
        
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
	 
    V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG
               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG
               WHERE  IS_DELETED = 0 AND START_HISTORICAL_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
				AND (  
                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LIFETIME)) IN ( 
                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
                   FROM DUAL
                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
                 )
                 OR :p2 = 0 
               )';
 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
	 
	V_STR_QUERY := 
	'DELETE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '  A 
	 WHERE    A.EFF_DATE =  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	 AND EXISTS (SELECT * FROM GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LIFETIME_RULE_ID = X.PKID) ' ; 
	
	
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;

	COMMIT; 
	 
	V_STR_QUERY :=
    'INSERT INTO  ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' (' ||
    '  EFF_DATE, LIFETIME_RULE_ID, FACILITY_NUMBER, MASTERID, ' ||
    '  CUSTOMER_NUMBER, LIFETIME_START_DATE, LIFETIME_END_DATE, LIFETIME, ' ||
    '  CREATED_BY, CREATED_DATE )'  ||
    'SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') , B.PKID , A.FACILITY_NUMBER, A.MASTERID, ' ||
    '  A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, A.LIFETIME_START_DATE, A.CLOSE_DATE, CEIL(MONTHS_BETWEEN(A.CLOSE_DATE, A.LIFETIME_START_DATE)), ' ||
    '  ''' || V_SPNAME || ''', SYSDATE ' ||
    'FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' ' || ' A ' ||
    ' JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG B ON A.LIFETIME_RULE_ID = B.PKID ' || 
	' WHERE LAST_DAY(A.LIFETIME_START_DATE) BETWEEN  LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''),(-1 *B.HISTORICAL_MONTH))) 
	AND LAST_DAY(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD''))
	AND A.CLOSE_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ' ;
	

 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
COMMIT ;


    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TABLEINSERT1;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_STR_QUERY := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_STR_QUERY, V_SPNAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_HEADER (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0', 
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'X'
) 
AUTHID CURRENT_USER
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE; 
	V_EOMDATE DATE ;  

	---- PROCESS
	V_COUNT NUMBER;
	V_RULE_ID VARCHAR2(10);
	V_ID NUMBER DEFAULT 0; 
	V_MAX_ID NUMBER DEFAULT 0; 
	V_DATADATE VARCHAR(20); 
    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY CLOB;
	V_STR_SQL_RULE CLOB;

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLECONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);
 
BEGIN
   
	
    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_HEADER';
    V_DATADATE := TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD');
    
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CASE 
        		WHEN CURRDATE = LAST_DAY(CURRDATE) THEN CURRDATE
        		ELSE LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(CURRDATE, -1))
    		END, LAST_DAY(CURRDATE)
        INTO V_CURRDATE,V_EOMDATE 
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;
  
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN  
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_DETAIL_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    	 	V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_HEADER_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE  
        V_TABLESELECT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_DETAIL'; 
    	 	V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_HEADER' ; 
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SPNAME, P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
	----TABLE CONFIG
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1); 
        
		IF V_COUNT = 0 THEN 
		  V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '
		 AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LIFETIME_HEADER  A WHERE 1 = 0 ' ;  
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
		END IF;

        
        
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'CREATE INDEX IDX_' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ON ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '(EFF_DATE,LIFETIME_RULE_ID )';
  
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
        
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
	 
    V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG
               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG
               WHERE  IS_DELETED = 0 AND START_HISTORICAL_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
				AND (  
                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LIFETIME)) IN ( 
                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
                   FROM DUAL
                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
                 )
                 OR :p2 = 0 
               )'; 
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
 
	 
	V_STR_QUERY := 
	'DELETE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '  A 
	 WHERE    A.EFF_DATE =  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
	 AND EXISTS (SELECT * FROM GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE A.LIFETIME_RULE_ID = X.PKID)  ' ; 
	
	
 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;

	COMMIT; 
	 
	V_STR_QUERY :=
    'INSERT INTO  ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' (' ||
    '  EFF_DATE, LIFETIME_RULE_ID,  LIFETIME, CREATED_BY, CREATED_DATE )' ||
    'SELECT TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'')  , B.PKID , CEIL(AVG(A.LIFETIME)) , '' SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_HEADER '', SYSDATE ' ||
    'FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLESELECT1 || ' ' || ' A ' ||
    ' JOIN GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG B ON A.LIFETIME_RULE_ID= B.PKID ' || 
	' WHERE A.EFF_DATE =  TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
GROUP BY B.PKID' ; 
	

 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
COMMIT ;


    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TABLEINSERT1;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_STR_QUERY := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_STR_QUERY, V_SPNAME,NVL( V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG
AS 
 
BEGIN
     
    
    MERGE INTO IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG a
    USING (
    
    	 SELECT * 
	 FROM (
	 

SELECT a."lifetime_name",A."syscode_lifetime_config" ,
	B.PKID AS SEGMENTATION_ID,A."method", 
	a."start_historical_date", a."calculation_method", a."historical_month",
	NVL(A."is_deleted",0) AS IS_DELETED,
	ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY a."syscode_lifetime_config" ORDER BY a."pkid" desc) RN
FROM "LifetimeConfiguration"@DBCONFIGLINK a 
	JOIN IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING b ON a."segment_code" = b.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION  ) x 
	WHERE x.rn = 1 
    ) b
    ON (a.SYSCODE_Lifetime = b."syscode_lifetime_config" )  
    WHEN MATCHED THEN
        UPDATE SET   
            a.UPDATED_BY              = 'SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG',
            a.UPDATED_DATE            = sysdate,
            a.IS_DELETED              = B.IS_DELETED
    
    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
        INSERT (
            LIFETIME_RULE_NAME,
		    SYSCODE_LIFETIME,
		    SEGMENTATION_ID,
		    LIFETIME_METHOD,
		    START_HISTORICAL_DATE,
		    CALCULATION_METHOD,
		    HISTORICAL_MONTH,
		    IS_DELETED,
		    CREATED_BY,
		    CREATED_DATE
		    )
        VALUES (
            b."lifetime_name",b."syscode_lifetime_config" ,
		b.SEGMENTATION_ID,b."method", 
	b."start_historical_date", b."calculation_method", b."historical_month",   B.IS_DELETED,
		'SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG',sysdate
        );
        
        commit;
     
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG_GTMP (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0', 
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
) 
AUTHID CURRENT_USER
AS
	V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLELGDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
	
	V_COUNT NUMBER; 

    V_QUERYS CLOB;
BEGIN
    
	V_TABLELGDCONFIG := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG'  ;
	  
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN 
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE 
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG';
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(P_DOWNLOAD_DATE, 'SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG_GTMP', P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
	----TABLE CONFIG
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1); 
        
		IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN 
		 V_QUERYS := '';
         V_QUERYS := V_QUERYS || 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_QUERYS);
		END IF;

        V_QUERYS := '';
        V_QUERYS := V_QUERYS || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_QUERYS);
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
        
   V_QUERYS := 'TRUNCATE TABLE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1;
   
   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_QUERYS) ; 
         
    V_QUERYS := 'INSERT INTO ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '
               SELECT * FROM ' || V_TABLELGDCONFIG || '
               WHERE (  
                 UPPER(TRIM(syscode_lifetime)) IN ( 
                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
                   FROM DUAL
                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
                 )
                 OR :p2 IS NULL 
               )';
 
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_QUERYS USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
        
  	COMMIT ; 
  

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULE_DATA (
 P_RUNID		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
 P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE, 
 P_SYSCODE		 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0', 
 P_PRC			 IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
) 
AUTHID CURRENT_USER
AS
	---- DATE   
    V_CURRDATE DATE; 
	V_EOMDATE DATE ;  

	---- PROCESS
	V_COUNT NUMBER;
	V_RULE_ID VARCHAR2(10);
	V_ID NUMBER DEFAULT 0; 
	V_MAX_ID NUMBER DEFAULT 0; 
	V_DATADATE VARCHAR(20); 
    ---- QUERY  
    V_STR_QUERY CLOB;
	V_STR_SQL_RULE CLOB;

	---- TABLE LIST 
	V_TAB_OWNER CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEINSERT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEINSERT2 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLESELECT1 VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLELGDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_TABLE_NAME VARCHAR2(100);

    ---- CONDITION
    V_RETURNROWS NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2 NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SPNAME VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION VARCHAR2(100);
 
BEGIN
   
	-- Handle default values for P_DOWNLOAD_DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CASE 
        		WHEN CURRDATE = LAST_DAY(CURRDATE) THEN CURRDATE
        		ELSE LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(CURRDATE, -1))
    		END, LAST_DAY(CURRDATE)
        INTO V_CURRDATE,V_EOMDATE 
        FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;
 
 	IF V_CURRDATE = V_EOMDATE THEN   
 		V_TABLE_NAME := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY' ;
 	ELSE 
 		V_TABLE_NAME := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY';
 	END IF ;
 	 
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_RULE_DATA_' || P_RUNID || ''; 
    ELSE  
        V_TABLEINSERT1 := 'IFRS_LIFETIME_RULE_DATA'; 
    END IF;

    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, 'SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULE_DATA', P_RUNID, 0, CURRENT_DATE); 
	COMMIT;
    -------- RECORD RUN_ID --------

    -------- ====== PRE SIMULATION TABLE ======
	----TABLE CONFIG
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
		SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
		FROM ALL_TABLES
		WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER 
		 AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEINSERT1); 
        
		IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN 
		 V_STR_QUERY := '';
         V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
		END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := '';
        V_STR_QUERY := V_STR_QUERY || 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_LIFETIME_RULE_DATA WHERE 0=1';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY);
        
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'CREATE INDEX IDX_' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' ON ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || '(DOWNLOAD_DATE, RULE_ID , MASTERID)';
    END IF;
	COMMIT;
        
    V_STR_QUERY := 'TRUNCATE TABLE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1;
   
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE (V_STR_QUERY) ; 
	
   EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG' ; 
	 
    V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG
               SELECT * FROM IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG
               WHERE  IS_DELETED = 0 AND START_HISTORICAL_DATE <= TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') 
				AND (  
                 UPPER(TRIM(SYSCODE_LIFETIME)) IN ( 
                   SELECT UPPER(TRIM(REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL)))
                   FROM DUAL
                   CONNECT BY REGEXP_SUBSTR(:p1, ''[^;]+'', 1, LEVEL) IS NOT NULL
                 )
                 OR :p2 = 0 
               )';
 DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY USING P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE, P_SYSCODE;
	  
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE ' || V_TABLEINSERT1  ; 
    
    V_STR_QUERY := 'SELECT MAX(PKID) 
	FROM IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING A 
	WHERE EXISTS (SELECT * FROM GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE X.SEGMENTATION_ID = A.PKID) ';

    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY INTO V_MAX_ID;
    
    V_ID := 0 ;

    WHILE V_ID < V_MAX_ID LOOP
	    V_STR_QUERY := '
        SELECT MIN(PKID) 
		FROM IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING A 
		WHERE EXISTS (SELECT * FROM GTMP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULES_CONFIG X WHERE X.SEGMENTATION_ID = A.PKID) 
        AND A.PKID > :V_ID';

    	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY
        INTO V_ID
        USING V_ID;
		
    	V_STR_QUERY :=
        'SELECT PKID, MERGE_SQL_CONDITIONS, TO_CHAR(:dt, ''YYYY-MM-DD'')
         FROM IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING
         WHERE PKID = :x';

    	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY
        INTO V_RULE_ID, V_STR_SQL_RULE, V_DATADATE
        USING V_CURRDATE,V_ID;
    	
    	COMMIT;
        -----------------------------------------------------------------
        -- BUILD FINAL DYNAMIC SQL
        -----------------------------------------------------------------
        V_STR_QUERY :=
            'INSERT INTO ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 ||' (' ||
            'DOWNLOAD_DATE, RULE_ID, MASTERID, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, FACILITY_NUMBER,' ||
			'ACCOUNT_STATUS, BI_COLLECTABILITY, RATING_CODE, EXT_RATING_CODE, DAY_PAST_DUE, DPD_CIF, ' ||
            'IMPAIRED_FLAG, LOAN_START_DATE, LOAN_DUE_DATE, CREATED_DATE, CREATED_BY) ' ||

            'SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, ' || V_RULE_ID || ', MASTERID, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, FACILITY_NUMBER,' ||
            'ACCOUNT_STATUS, BI_COLLECTABILITY, RATING_CODE, EXT_RATING_CODE, DAY_PAST_DUE, DPD_CIF, ' ||
            'IMPAIRED_FLAG, LOAN_START_DATE, LOAN_DUE_DATE, SYSDATE, ''SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULE_DATA'' ' ||
            'FROM ' || V_TABLE_NAME ||   
            ' IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT WHERE ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A'' ' ||
            '  AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || V_DATADATE || ''' ' ||
            '  AND (' || V_STR_SQL_RULE || ')';

     
       
    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
     EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
    END LOOP;
    
    
    
     

    -------- ====== LOG ======
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TABLEINSERT1;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_SPNAME := 'SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_RULE_DATA';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
    
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SPNAME, V_OPERATION, nvl(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== LOG ======

    -------- ====== RESULT ======
    V_STR_QUERY := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TABLEINSERT1 || ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''', ''YYYY-MM-DD'') ';
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_STR_QUERY, V_SPNAME, nvl(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
	COMMIT;
    -------- ====== RESULT ======

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_LOOPING_ADAM
IS
    v_loop INTEGER := 0;
BEGIN
    WHILE v_loop < 71 LOOP
--	WHILE v_loop < 1 LOOP
        -- Panggil prosedur lain
        SP_IFRS_MASTERID;

        -- Update tanggal
        UPDATE IFRS_PRC_DATE
        SET CURRDATE = LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(CURRDATE, 1)),
            PREVDATE = LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(PREVDATE, 1));

        -- Increment counter
        v_loop := v_loop + 1;
    END LOOP;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_MASTERID
AS

	V_CURRDATE DATE;
	V_PREVDATE DATE;
	
BEGIN
       

	 SELECT 
	 	 CURRDATE
	 	,PREVDATE 
	 	INTO 
	 	 V_CURRDATE
	 	,V_PREVDATE
	 FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE_AMORT;
     

	INSERT INTO IFRS_MASTER_ID 
	(
		MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE
	   ,ACCOUNT_NUMBER
	   ,IAS_CLASS
	   ,EFFDATE
	   ,CREATED_DATE
	)
	SELECT
		MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID,
		ACCOUNT_NUMBER,
		'A' AS IAS_CLASS,
		V_CURRDATE,
		SYSDATE
	FROM IFRS_STG_MASTER_ACCOUNT isma 
	WHERE 
	DOWNLOAD_DATE = V_CURRDATE
	AND
	NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM IFRS_MASTER_ID B WHERE isma.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID = B.MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE)
