AS
    -- Dates / counters
	
    V_CURRDATE      DATE;
    V_PREVDATE      DATE;
    V_MODEL_ID      VARCHAR2(22);
    V_COUNT         NUMBER;
	V_COUNTER   	NUMBER := 1;
    V_EXPLIFE   	NUMBER := 0;

    -- Dynamic SQL
    V_STR_QUERY     CLOB;

    -- Table names
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
	V_GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG VARCHAR2(100);
    	V_TMP_MEV VARCHAR2(100);
    	V_TMP_AVG_STDEV_ME VARCHAR2(100);
    	V_TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1 VARCHAR2(100);
    	V_IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE VARCHAR2(100);
    	V_IFRS_ME_FORECAST_SCN VARCHAR2(100);
    	V_IFRS_MACRO_ECONOMIC_INTRPOLATE VARCHAR2(100);

    -- misc
    V_RETURNROWS    NUMBER;
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100);
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);

    -- result query
    V_QUERYS        CLOB;
BEGIN
    -- set procedure name
    V_SP_NAME := 'SP_IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE';
    
    -- handle default download date
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE
          INTO V_CURRDATE
          FROM PSAK413.IFRS_PRC_DATE; 
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := NVL(P_SYSCODE, '0');

    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
    	V_GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG := 'GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG_' || P_RUNID;
        V_TABLEPDCONFIG := 'IFRS_PD_RULES_CONFIG_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_TMP_MEV := 'TMP_MEV_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_TMP_AVG_STDEV_ME := 'TMP_AVG_STDEV_ME_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1 := 'TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE := 'IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_IFRS_ME_FORECAST_SCN := 'IFRS_ME_FORECAST_SCN_' || P_RUNID;
    	V_IFRS_MACRO_ECONOMIC_INTRPOLATE := 'IFRS_MACRO_ECONOMIC_INTRPOLATE_' || P_RUNID;
    
    ELSE
        V_GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG := 'GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG';
        V_TABLEPDCONFIG := 'IFRS_PD_RULES_CONFIG';
    	V_TMP_MEV := 'TMP_MEV';
    	V_TMP_AVG_STDEV_ME := 'TMP_AVG_STDEV_ME';
    	V_TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1 := 'TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1';
    	V_IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE := 'IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE';
    	V_IFRS_ME_FORECAST_SCN := 'IFRS_ME_FORECAST_SCN';
    	V_IFRS_MACRO_ECONOMIC_INTRPOLATE := 'IFRS_MACRO_ECONOMIC_INTRPOLATE';
    
    END IF;

   PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, P_RUNID, 0, SYSDATE);
   COMMIT;

    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    -- PRE-SIMULATION TABLE: create/drop temp tables if P_PRC = 'S'
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        -- drop table if exists
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM ALL_TABLES
        WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER
          AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TMP_MEV);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_MEV;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_MEV ||
                       ' AS SELECT *  FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.TMP_MEV WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;

        -- second table
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM ALL_TABLES
        WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER
          AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TMP_AVG_STDEV_ME);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_AVG_STDEV_ME;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_AVG_STDEV_ME ||
                       ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.TMP_AVG_STDEV_ME WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        
        -- table V_TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM ALL_TABLES
        WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER
          AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1 ||
                       ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1 WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        
       	-- table V_IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM ALL_TABLES
        WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER
          AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE ||
                       ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        
        -- config
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM ALL_TABLES
        WHERE OWNER = V_TAB_OWNER
          AND TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_TABLEPDCONFIG);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEPDCONFIG;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEPDCONFIG ||
                       ' AS SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.IFRS_PD_RULES_CONFIG WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
    ELSE 
    	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG';
    	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE TMP_MEV';
    	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE TMP_AVG_STDEV_ME';
    	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1';
        
        -- delete existing rows in target for this eff_date and model filter
	    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'DELETE FROM IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
	      AND (PD_RULE_ID = ' || V_MODEL_ID || ' OR ' || V_MODEL_ID || ' = 0)';
    END IF;
    COMMIT;
        
-- populate GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG
    V_STR_QUERY := ' INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG || ' (
        PD_RULE_ID, BUCKET_GROUP, INCREMENT_PERIOD, CURR_DATE, CUT_OFF_DATE,
        ME_CODE, CALC_METHOD, EXPECTED_LIFE, PERIOD_START, PERIOD_END
    )
    SELECT
        A.PKID, A.BUCKET_GROUP, A.INCREMENT_PERIOD, TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') AS CURR_DATE,
        A.CUT_OFF_DATE, A.ME_CODE, A.CALC_METHOD, A.EXPECTED_LIFE,
        LAST_DAY(
            ADD_MONTHS(
                TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD''),
                -1 * A.INCREMENT_PERIOD * A.HISTORICAL_DATA
            )
        ) AS PERIOD_START,
        TO_DATE(''31-12-'' || TO_CHAR(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD''),''YYYY''), ''DD-MM-YYYY'') AS PERIOD_END
    FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TABLEPDCONFIG || ' A
    WHERE NVL(A.ACTIVE_FLAG,0) = 1
      AND A.PD_METHOD = ''VAS''
      AND (A.PKID = ' || V_MODEL_ID || ' OR ' || V_MODEL_ID || ' = 0)';
	
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
    COMMIT;
    
    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
    
    -- populate TMP_MEV from IFRS_ME_FORECAST_SCN (distinct)
    V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_MEV || ' (ME_PERIOD, ME_CODE, SCENARIO_NO, ME_VAL)
    SELECT DISTINCT LAST_DAY(A.ME_PERIOD), A.ME_CODE, A.SCENARIO_NO, A.ME_VALUE
    FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_ME_FORECAST_SCN || ' A
    WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
      AND EXISTS (
          SELECT 1 FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG || ' B WHERE B.ME_CODE = A.ME_CODE
      )';
    
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
    COMMIT;
	
    -- populate TMP_MEV also from IFRS_MACRO_ECONOMIC_INTRPOLATE for matching ME_CODE/SCENARIO_NO not present yet
    V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_MEV || ' (ME_PERIOD, ME_CODE, SCENARIO_NO, ME_VAL)
    SELECT LAST_DAY(A.ME_PERIOD), A.ME_CODE, B.SCENARIO_NO, A.ME_VALUE
    FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_MACRO_ECONOMIC_INTRPOLATE || ' A
    JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT ME_CODE, SCENARIO_NO FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_MEV || ') B ON A.ME_CODE = B.ME_CODE
    WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
      AND A.ME_PERIOD <= LAST_DAY(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD''))
      AND NOT EXISTS (
          SELECT 1 FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_MEV || ' X
          WHERE X.ME_CODE = A.ME_CODE
            AND B.SCENARIO_NO = X.SCENARIO_NO
            AND LAST_DAY(A.ME_PERIOD) = LAST_DAY(X.ME_PERIOD)
      )';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
    COMMIT;
    
    -- compute AVG and STDEV per PD_RULE_ID, ME_CODE
    V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_AVG_STDEV_ME || ' (PD_RULE_ID, ME_CODE, AVG_ME_VAL, STDEV_ME_VAL)
    SELECT
        B.PD_RULE_ID,
        B.ME_CODE,
        AVG(A.ME_VALUE) AS AVG_ME_VAL,
        STDDEV(A.ME_VALUE) AS STDEV_ME_VAL
    FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_MACRO_ECONOMIC_INTRPOLATE || ' A
    JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG || ' B ON A.ME_CODE = B.ME_CODE
    WHERE A.EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
      AND A.ME_PERIOD BETWEEN LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(B.PERIOD_START, -1)) AND TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
    GROUP BY B.PD_RULE_ID, B.ME_CODE';
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
    COMMIT;
    
    -- get expected life (assume same for all rows; original T-SQL used SELECT into variable)
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE ' SELECT EXPECTED_LIFE 
    FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG || '
    WHERE ROWNUM = 1'
    INTO V_EXPLIFE ;

  	-- loop to insert into TMP_PD_EXT_ZSCORE1 with yearly offsets as in original
    WHILE V_COUNTER <= NVL(V_EXPLIFE,0) LOOP
       EXECUTE IMMEDIATE ' INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1 || ' (PD_RULE_ID, ME_CODE, PERIOD, SCENARIO_NO, ME_VAL)
        SELECT B.PD_RULE_ID,
               A.ME_CODE,
               A.ME_PERIOD,
               A.SCENARIO_NO,
               NVL(A.ME_VAL,0)
        FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_MEV || ' A
        JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG || ' B ON A.ME_CODE = B.ME_CODE
        WHERE A.ME_PERIOD >= B.PERIOD_END
          AND LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(B.PERIOD_END, 12 * ' || V_COUNTER || ')) = A.ME_PERIOD';
  	
        V_COUNTER := V_COUNTER + 1;
    END LOOP;
	COMMIT;
        
    -- recursive CTE to generate periods similar to CTEDATE in T-SQL
    V_STR_QUERY := 'WITH CTEDATE (PD_RULE_ID, PERIOD, INCREMENT_PERIOD, MAXDATE) AS (
        SELECT
            PD_RULE_ID,
            TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') AS PERIOD,
            INCREMENT_PERIOD,
            LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD''), (EXPECTED_LIFE * INCREMENT_PERIOD))) AS MAXDATE
        FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG || '
        UNION ALL
        SELECT
            PD_RULE_ID,
            LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(PERIOD, INCREMENT_PERIOD)),
            INCREMENT_PERIOD,
            MAXDATE
        FROM CTEDATE
        WHERE LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(PERIOD, INCREMENT_PERIOD)) <= MAXDATE
    ),
    CTERN AS (
        SELECT DISTINCT PD_RULE_ID, EXTRACT(YEAR FROM PERIOD) AS YEAR_PERIOD,
               ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY PD_RULE_ID ORDER BY EXTRACT(YEAR FROM PERIOD)) RN
        FROM CTEDATE
        WHERE EXTRACT(YEAR FROM PERIOD) > EXTRACT(YEAR FROM TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD''))
    )
INSERT INTO ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE || ' (
        EFF_DATE, BASE_DATE, FL_SEQ, PD_RULE_ID, ME_CODE, SCENARIO_NO,
        ODR, MEAN_ODR, STDEV_ODR, ZSCORE, CREATEDBY, CREATEDDATE
    )
SELECT
        TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') AS EFF_DATE,
        A.PERIOD AS BASE_DATE,
        F.RN - 1 AS FL_SEQ,
        A.PD_RULE_ID,
        C.ME_CODE,
        C.SCENARIO_NO,
        NVL(D.ME_VAL, C.AVG_VAL) AS ODR,
        E.AVG_ME_VAL AS MEAN_ODR,
        E.STDEV_ME_VAL AS STDEV_ODR,
        0 AS ZSCORE,
        ''SP_IFRS_PD_MAA_ZSCORE'' AS CREATEDBY,
        SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE
    FROM CTEDATE A
    JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG || ' B ON A.PD_RULE_ID = B.PD_RULE_ID
    JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_AVG_STDEV_ME || ' E ON B.PD_RULE_ID = E.PD_RULE_ID
    JOIN (
        SELECT PD_RULE_ID, ME_CODE, SCENARIO_NO, AVG(ME_VAL) AS AVG_VAL
        FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1 || '
        GROUP BY PD_RULE_ID, ME_CODE, SCENARIO_NO
    ) C ON B.PD_RULE_ID = C.PD_RULE_ID
       AND B.ME_CODE = C.ME_CODE
    LEFT JOIN ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_TMP_PD_VAS_ZSCORE1 || ' D
       ON A.PERIOD = D.PERIOD
      AND B.ME_CODE = D.ME_CODE
      AND C.SCENARIO_NO = D.SCENARIO_NO
      AND B.PD_RULE_ID = D.PD_RULE_ID
    LEFT JOIN CTERN F ON EXTRACT(YEAR FROM A.PERIOD) = F.YEAR_PERIOD
                     AND A.PD_RULE_ID = F.PD_RULE_ID
    WHERE A.PERIOD > TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')';
	
    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(SUBSTR(V_STR_QUERY, 1, 30000));
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
    COMMIT;
     
    -- update ZSCOREs
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE '
	    UPDATE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE || ' dest
	       SET dest.ZSCORE = (dest.ODR - dest.MEAN_ODR) / dest.STDEV_ODR
	     WHERE dest.EFF_DATE = :v1
	       AND EXISTS (
	           SELECT 1 
	             FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_GTMP_PD_ZSCORE_CONFIG || ' b 
	            WHERE dest.PD_RULE_ID = b.PD_RULE_ID
	       )'
    USING V_CURRDATE;
	COMMIT;
    
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_PD_VAS_ZSCORE ||
                ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')' ||
                ' AND (PD_RULE_ID = ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' OR ''' || V_MODEL_ID || ''' = ''0'')';

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV
(
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE    IN DATE DEFAULT NULL,
    P_QUERYS           IN CLOB DEFAULT NULL,
    P_SOURCE_OBJECT    IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL,
    P_AFFECTED_RECORD  IN NUMBER DEFAULT 0,
    P_RUNID            IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000'
)
AS
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO IFRS_RESULT_PREVIEW
        (DOWNLOAD_DATE,
         QUERY_RESULT,
         SOURCE_OBJECT,
         AFFECTED_RECORD,
         RUN_ID,
         PROCESS_DATE)
    VALUES
        (P_DOWNLOAD_DATE,
         P_QUERYS,
         P_SOURCE_OBJECT,
         P_AFFECTED_RECORD,
         P_RUNID,
         SYSTIMESTAMP);

    -- Pengganti RAISE NOTICE di Oracle
    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('QUERY RESULT : ' || P_QUERYS);
END SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG
(
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE DEFAULT NULL,
    P_STORENAME     IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL,
    P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    P_PROCESS_ID    IN NUMBER DEFAULT NULL,
    P_PROCESS_DATE  IN DATE DEFAULT NULL
)
AS
BEGIN
    INSERT INTO IFRS_RUNNING_LOGS 
    (
        DOWNLOAD_DATE, SP_NAME, RUN_ID, PROCESS_ID, PROCESS_DATE
    )
    VALUES 
    (
        P_DOWNLOAD_DATE,
        P_STORENAME,
        P_RUNID,
        NVL(P_PROCESS_ID, NULL),   -- Atau misal ingin runtime PID → SYS_CONTEXT
        SYSTIMESTAMP
    );
END SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413."SP_IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING" 
AS 

    V_MAXLV NUMBER(2,0);
    
BEGIN
    
        
    SELECT TO_NUMBER("value")
    into V_MAXLV
    FROM "MstConfigParams"@DBCONFIGLINK
    WHERE "api_project_name" = 'PSAK413_Impairment'
        and "name" = 'MaxSegmentLevelPsak413' ;
    
    MERGE INTO IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING a
    USING (
            
    selecT "pkid",
        "syscode_segmentation_lv1", "segment_name_lv1",
        "syscode_segmentation_lv2", "segment_name_lv2",
        "syscode_segmentation_lv3", "segment_name_lv3",
        "syscode_segmentation_lv4", "segment_name_lv4",
        "syscode_segmentation_lv5", "segment_name_lv5",
        "syscode_segmentation_lv6", "segment_name_lv6",
        "syscode_segmentation_lv7", "segment_name_lv7",
        "syscode_segmentation_lv8", "segment_name_lv8",
        "syscode_segmentation_lv9", "segment_name_lv9",
        "syscode_segmentation_lv10", "segment_name_lv10",
        "is_deleted","merge_sql_conditions",
        CASE WHEN V_MAXLV = 1 THEN "syscode_segmentation_lv1"
            WHEN V_MAXLV = 2 THEN "syscode_segmentation_lv2"
            WHEN V_MAXLV = 3 THEN "syscode_segmentation_lv3"
            WHEN V_MAXLV = 4 THEN "syscode_segmentation_lv4"
            WHEN V_MAXLV = 5 THEN "syscode_segmentation_lv5"
            WHEN V_MAXLV = 6 THEN "syscode_segmentation_lv6"
            WHEN V_MAXLV = 7 THEN "syscode_segmentation_lv7"
            WHEN V_MAXLV = 8 THEN "syscode_segmentation_lv8"
            WHEN V_MAXLV = 9 THEN "syscode_segmentation_lv9"
            WHEN V_MAXLV = 10 THEN "syscode_segmentation_lv10"
        END AS "syscode_segmentation",
        CASE WHEN "segment_type" = 'ALL' THEN 'PORTFOLIO'
        ELSE 
        "segment_type"
        END AS "segment_type"
    from "SegmentationMapping"@DBCONFIGLINK a 
    where "pkid" in (
        select max("pkid")
        from "SegmentationMapping"@DBCONFIGLINK 
        group by "syscode_segmentation_lv1",
            nvl("syscode_segmentation_lv2",' '),
            nvl("syscode_segmentation_lv3",' '),
            nvl("syscode_segmentation_lv4",' '),
            nvl("syscode_segmentation_lv5",' '),
            nvl("syscode_segmentation_lv6",' '),
            nvl("syscode_segmentation_lv7",' '),
            nvl("syscode_segmentation_lv8",' '),
            nvl("syscode_segmentation_lv9",' '),
            nvl("syscode_segmentation_lv10", ' '),
            "segment_type")
    ) b
    ON (a.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV1 = b."syscode_segmentation_lv1"
        and nvl(a.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV2,' ') = nvl(b."syscode_segmentation_lv2",' ')
        and nvl(a.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV3,' ') = nvl(b."syscode_segmentation_lv3",' ')
        and nvl(a.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV4,' ') = nvl(b."syscode_segmentation_lv4",' ')
        and nvl(a.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV5,' ') = nvl(b."syscode_segmentation_lv5",' ')
        and nvl(a.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV6,' ') = nvl(b."syscode_segmentation_lv6",' ')
        and nvl(a.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV7,' ') = nvl(b."syscode_segmentation_lv7",' ')
        and nvl(a.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV8,' ') = nvl(b."syscode_segmentation_lv8",' ')
        and nvl(a.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV9,' ') = nvl(b."syscode_segmentation_lv9",' ')
        and nvl(a.SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV10,' ') = nvl(b."syscode_segmentation_lv10" ,' ')
        )  
     
    WHEN MATCHED THEN
        UPDATE SET  
            a.MERGE_SQL_CONDITIONS    = b."merge_sql_conditions",
            a.UPDATED_BY              = 'SP_IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING',
            a.UPDATED_DATE            = sysdate,
            a.IS_DELETED              = b."is_deleted"
 
    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
        INSERT (
            SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV1, SEGMENT_NAME_LV1,
            SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV2, SEGMENT_NAME_LV2,
            SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV3, SEGMENT_NAME_LV3,
            SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV4, SEGMENT_NAME_LV4,
            SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV5, SEGMENT_NAME_LV5,
            SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV6, SEGMENT_NAME_LV6,
            SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV7, SEGMENT_NAME_LV7,
            SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV8, SEGMENT_NAME_LV8,
            SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV9, SEGMENT_NAME_LV9,
            SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION_LV10, SEGMENT_NAME_LV10,
            MERGE_SQL_CONDITIONS,
            CREATED_BY, CREATED_DATE, 
            IS_DELETED,
            SYSCODE_SEGMENTATION, SEGMENT_TYPE
        )
        VALUES (
            b."syscode_segmentation_lv1", b."segment_name_lv1",
            b."syscode_segmentation_lv2", b."segment_name_lv2",
            b."syscode_segmentation_lv3", b."segment_name_lv3",
            b."syscode_segmentation_lv4", b."segment_name_lv4",
            b."syscode_segmentation_lv5", b."segment_name_lv5",
            b."syscode_segmentation_lv6", b."segment_name_lv6",
            b."syscode_segmentation_lv7", b."segment_name_lv7",
            b."syscode_segmentation_lv8", b."segment_name_lv8",
            b."syscode_segmentation_lv9", b."segment_name_lv9",
            b."syscode_segmentation_lv10", b."segment_name_lv10",
            b."merge_sql_conditions",
            'SP_IFRS_SEGMENTATION_MAPPING', sysdate, 
            nvl(b."is_deleted",0),
            b."syscode_segmentation",nvl(b."segment_type",'PORTFOLIO')
        );
        
        commit;
     
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413."SP_IFRS_STAGE_CONFIG" 
AS 
    
BEGIN
	
	
     MERGE INTO IFRS_STAGE_CONFIG a
	    USING (
	    
		    SELECT b."pkid",x."syscode_staging" AS syscode_header, b."syscode_staging" AS syscode_detail,x."staging_name" AS group_name,
		    		b."staging_name" AS detail_name,TO_CHAR(b."sql_conditions") AS sql_conditions,
		    		b."is_deleted", b."is_sicr", b."is_publish"
		    FROM (
			    selecT A."pkid", A."syscode_staging",
			       A."staging_name" 
			    from "Staging"@DBCONFIGLINK A
			    WHERE "level" = 1 AND "is_publish"= 1 ) x 
			    LEFT JOIN "Staging"@DBCONFIGLINK b ON x."syscode_staging" = b."parent_code_level_0" AND b."level" = 2
		    
	    ) b
	    ON ( a.SYSCODE_STAGE_HEADER = b.syscode_header 
	    	AND a.SYSCODE_STAGE_DETAIL = b.syscode_detail ) 
	    WHEN MATCHED THEN
	        UPDATE SET  
	            a.UPDATEDBY              = 'SP_IFRS_STAGE_CONFIG',
	            a.UPDATEDDATE            = sysdate,
	            a.IS_DELETE              = b."is_deleted",
	            a.IS_SICR 				 = b."is_sicr",
	            a.SQL_CONDITIONS		 = b.sql_conditions
	    WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
	        INSERT (
	            SYSCODE_STAGE_HEADER, SYSCODE_STAGE_DETAIL, STAGE_HEADER, STAGE_DETAIL,
	            SQL_CONDITIONS, IS_DELETE,IS_SICR , UPDATEDBY, UPDATEDDATE
	        )
	        VALUES (
	            b.syscode_header, b.syscode_detail,
	            b.group_name,b.detail_name,b.sql_conditions, b."is_deleted",b."is_sicr" , 'SP_IFRS_STAGE_CONFIG', sysdate 
	        );
	        
	        commit;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_SYNC_PARAM
(
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE    DATE DEFAULT '01 JAN 1990',
    P_TABLE_DEST       VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL,
    P_COLUMN_DEST      VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL,
    P_STORENAME        VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL,
    P_OPERATION        VARCHAR2 DEFAULT NULL,
    P_AFFECTED_RECORD  NUMBER DEFAULT NULL,
    P_RUNID            VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000'
)
AS

BEGIN

EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'truncate table SegmentationMapping';
	
insert into SegmentationMapping 
(
	 "pkid"
	,"syscode_segmentation_lv1"
--	,"version"
	,"segment_name_lv1"
	,"syscode_segmentation_lv2"
	,"segment_name_lv2"
	,"syscode_segmentation_lv3"
	,"segment_name_lv3"
	,"syscode_segmentation_lv4"
	,"segment_name_lv4"
	,"syscode_segmentation_lv5"
	,"segment_name_lv5"
	,"syscode_segmentation_lv6"
	,"segment_name_lv6"
	,"syscode_segmentation_lv7"
	,"segment_name_lv7"
	,"syscode_segmentation_lv8"
	,"segment_name_lv8"
	,"syscode_segmentation_lv9"
	,"segment_name_lv9"
	,"syscode_segmentation_lv10"

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_UPDATE_IMA_RESULT (
    p_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
	p_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    p_PRC           IN CHAR DEFAULT 'M'
)
AS
    v_RULE_ID        VARCHAR2(250);
    v_TABLE_NAME     VARCHAR2(100);
    v_STR_SQL        CLOB;
    v_GROUP_SEGMENT  VARCHAR2(250);
    v_SEGMENT        VARCHAR2(250);
    v_SUB_SEGMENT    VARCHAR2(250);
    v_CONDITION      VARCHAR2(4000);
    v_CURRDATE       DATE;
    v_EXCEPT_ID      VARCHAR2(50);
    v_ERROR_FLAG     NUMBER(1) := 0;
    v_TABLENAME      VARCHAR2(100);
BEGIN
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    -- INIT
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    IF p_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO v_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        v_CURRDATE := p_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;


    v_TABLENAME :=
        CASE
            WHEN p_PRC = 'M' THEN 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY'
            ELSE 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY_' || p_RUNID ||''
        END;

    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    -- RESET SEGMENT DATA (DYNAMIC UPDATE)
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    v_STR_SQL :=
        'UPDATE ' || v_TABLENAME || ' A                
			 SET A.EIL_AMOUNT = 0
			  ,A.BUCKET_ID = 0                
			  ,A.LIFETIME = 0
			  ,A.LT_RULE_ID = 0               
			  ,A.LGD_RULE_ID = 0          
			  ,A.PD_RULE_ID = 0          
			  ,A.PD_ME_MODEL_ID = 0              
			  ,A.EAD_RULE_ID = 0           
			  ,A.EIL_MODEL_ID = 0
			  ,A.EIL_MARGIN = 0
			  ,A.EIL_POKOK = 0
			  ,A.EAD_AMOUNT = 0
			  ,A.MARGIN_ACCRUED = 0
			  ,A.PD_RATE = 0
			  ,A.LGD_RATE = 0               
			 WHERE A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A''                  
			  AND A.IS_IMPAIRED = 1
			  AND A.IMPAIRED_FLAG = ''C''                  
			  AND A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(v_currdate,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'') '; 
			 
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_STR_SQL;
    COMMIT;

    v_STR_SQL := 'MERGE INTO ' || v_TABLENAME || ' t
				USING (
				  SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, EIL_AMOUNT, BUCKET_ID, LT_RULE_ID, LIFETIME,
				         LGD_RULE_ID, LGD_SEGMENT, PD_RULE_ID, PD_ME_MODEL_ID, PD_SEGMENT,
				         EAD_RULE_ID, EAD_SEGMENT, EIL_MODEL_ID, EIL_MARGIN, EIL_PRINCIPAL,
				         PD, LGD, EAD_AMOUNT, MARGIN_ACCRUED
				  FROM IFRS_EIL_RESULT_HEADER s
				  WHERE s.DOWNLOAD_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(v_currdate,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')
				) s
				ON (s.MASTERID = t.MASTERID AND s.DOWNLOAD_DATE = t.DOWNLOAD_DATE)
				WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE SET
				   t.EIL_AMOUNT     = s.EIL_AMOUNT,
				   t.BUCKET_ID      = s.BUCKET_ID,
				   t.LT_RULE_ID     = s.LT_RULE_ID,
				   t.LIFETIME       = s.LIFETIME,
				   t.LGD_RULE_ID    = s.LGD_RULE_ID,
				   t.PD_RULE_ID     = s.PD_RULE_ID,
				   t.PD_ME_MODEL_ID = s.PD_ME_MODEL_ID,
				   t.EAD_RULE_ID    = s.EAD_RULE_ID,
				   t.EIL_MODEL_ID   = s.EIL_MODEL_ID,
				   t.EIL_MARGIN     = s.EIL_MARGIN,
				   t.EIL_POKOK      = s.EIL_PRINCIPAL,
				   t.PD_RATE        = s.PD,
				   t.LGD_RATE       = s.LGD,
				   t.EAD_AMOUNT     = s.EAD_AMOUNT,
				   t.MARGIN_ACCRUED = s.MARGIN_ACCRUED';
   
	DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE(v_STR_SQL);
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_STR_SQL;
	COMMIT;

EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN SP_IFRS_UPDATE_IMA_RESULT: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_IFRS_UPDATE_STAGE (
	p_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE
)
AS
    v_RULE_ID        VARCHAR2(250);
    v_STAGE_DETAIL     VARCHAR2(100);
    v_STR_SQL        VARCHAR2(4000);
    v_IS_SICR  		 NUMBER;
    v_CONDITION      VARCHAR2(4000);
    v_CURRDATE       DATE;
    v_TABLENAME      VARCHAR2(100);
BEGIN
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    -- INIT
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    IF p_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO v_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        v_CURRDATE := p_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    v_TABLENAME := 'IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY';
  
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    -- RESET STAGE (DYNAMIC UPDATE)
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    v_STR_SQL :=
        'UPDATE ' || v_TABLENAME || ' A ' ||
        'SET A.STAGE = NULL ' ||
        'WHERE A.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A'' AND A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(v_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || '''';

    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_STR_SQL;
    COMMIT;
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    -- CURSOR LOOP
    ----------------------------------------------------------------
    FOR rec IN (
        SELECT PKID , STAGE_DETAIL ,IS_SICR  , SQL_CONDITIONS 
        FROM IFRS_STAGE_CONFIG
        WHERE IS_DELETE = 0 AND IS_SICR = 0
    )
    LOOP
        v_RULE_ID        := rec.PKID;
        v_STAGE_DETAIL   := rec.STAGE_DETAIL;
        v_IS_SICR		 := rec.IS_SICR;
        v_CONDITION      := rec.SQL_CONDITIONS;

        v_STR_SQL :=
            'UPDATE ' || v_TABLENAME || ' ifrs_master_account ' ||
            ' SET ifrs_master_account.STAGE = CASE WHEN ''' || v_STAGE_DETAIL || ''' = ''Stage 1'' THEN 1 ' ||
            ' WHEN ''' || v_STAGE_DETAIL || ''' = ''Stage 2'' THEN 2 END, ' ||
            ' SICR_FLAG = 0 ' ||
            ' WHERE (' || v_CONDITION || ') ' ||
            ' AND ifrs_master_account.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A'' AND ifrs_master_account.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(v_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || '''';

        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_STR_SQL;
    END LOOP;

    COMMIT;
   
   --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   	FOR rec IN (
        SELECT PKID , STAGE_DETAIL ,IS_SICR  , SQL_CONDITIONS 
        FROM IFRS_STAGE_CONFIG
        WHERE IS_DELETE = 0 AND IS_SICR = 1
    	)
    LOOP
   		v_RULE_ID        := rec.PKID;
        v_STAGE_DETAIL   := rec.STAGE_DETAIL;
        v_IS_SICR		 := rec.IS_SICR;
        v_CONDITION      := rec.SQL_CONDITIONS;

	   	v_STR_SQL :=
	            'UPDATE ' || v_TABLENAME || ' ifrs_master_account ' ||
	            ' SET ifrs_master_account.STAGE = 2 , SICR_FLAG = 1 ' ||
	            ' WHERE (' || v_CONDITION || ') ' ||
	            ' AND ifrs_master_account.ACCOUNT_STATUS = ''A'' AND ifrs_master_account.STAGE = 1 AND ifrs_master_account.DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(v_CURRDATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD') || '''';
	
	    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE v_STR_SQL;
    END LOOP;
   
    COMMIT;
   
   	C_SP_IFRS_STAGE_BENCANA(v_CURRDATE);
   
EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN SP_IFRS_UPDATE_STAGE: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_LGD_SEQ
AS
--declare
dtcurr DATE;
dtprev DATE;
BEGIN
	
	dtcurr := '31-JAN-2021';

 	--EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE IFRS_LGD_DATA';
	--EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA';
  
    --COMMIT;
	 
	WHILE  dtcurr <=   '31-DEC-2025'
	LOOP 
		
		SP_IFRS_LGD_RULE_DATA('S_00000_0000', dtcurr, 'WPC-20260211-000000006;WPC-20260211-000000014', 'M');
		
		SP_IFRS_LGD_DATA('S_00000_0000', dtcurr, 'WPC-20260211-000000006;WPC-20260211-000000014', 'M');
		
		SP_IFRS_LGD_REC_DATA('S_00000_0000', dtcurr, 'WPC-20260211-000000006;WPC-20260211-000000014', 'M');
		
		 
	dbms_output.put_line(dtcurr);
	UPDATE PSAK413.X_IFRS_PRCDATE  SET CURRDATE  = dtcurr ; COMMIT ;
	dtcurr := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(dtcurr, 1));

END LOOP;

END;

--declare

	WHILE  dtcurr <=   '31-DEC-2025'

		SP_IFRS_LIFETIME_DATA('S_00000_0000', dtcurr, '0', 'M');

	dbms_output.put_line(dtcurr);
	UPDATE PSAK413.X_IFRS_PRCDATE  SET CURRDATE  = dtcurr ; COMMIT ;
	dtcurr := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(dtcurr, 1));

END LOOP;

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_MULTIJASA
AS
BEGIN
	
	
		INSERT INTO IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
		(
			 DOWNLOAD_DATE
			,MASTERID
			,MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE
			,DATA_SOURCE
			,PRODUCT_TYPE 
			,PRODUCT_CODE 
			,BRANCH_CODE 
			,ACCOUNT_STATUS 
			,ACCOUNT_NUMBER 
			,CUSTOMER_NUMBER 
			,CUSTOMER_NAME 
			,CURRENCY 
			,EXCHANGE_RATE 
			,OUTSTANDING 
			,PLAFOND 
			,MARGIN_RATE 
			,EIR 
			,FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT 
			,DAY_PAST_DUE 
			,DPD_CIF 
			,BI_COLLECTABILITY 
			,BI_COLLECT_CIF 
			,STAFF_LOAN_FLAG 
			,COLL_AMOUNT 
			,UNAMORT_FEE_AMT 
			,UNAMORT_COST_AMT 
			,MARGIN_TYPE 
			,DEFAULT_DATE 
			,LOAN_START_DATE 
			,LOAN_DUE_DATE 
			,DIVISION_CODE 
			,RESTRUCTURE_FLAG 
			,OUTSTANDING_PAST_DUE 
			,MARGIN_PAST_DUE 
		)
		
		
		SELECT 
			 TO_DATE(FICMISDATE, 'DD/MM/YYYY HH24:MI:SS')  AS DOWNLOAD_DATE
			,IMI.MASTERID
			,'MULTIJASA_'||NOMORREKENING AS MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE
			,'MULTIJASA' AS DATA_SOURCE
			,'IJARAH' AS PRODUCT_TYPE 
			,LOANTYPECODE AS PRODUCT_CODE 
			,KODECABANG AS BRANCH_CODE 
			,'A' AS ACCOUNT_STATUS 
			,NOMORREKENING AS ACCOUNT_NUMBER 
			,NOMORNASABAH AS CUSTOMER_NUMBER 
			,NAMANASABAH AS CUSTOMER_NAME 
			,JENISVALUTA AS CURRENCY 
			,1 AS EXCHANGE_RATE 
			,NOMINAL AS OUTSTANDING 
			,NULL AS PLAFOND 
			,NULL AS MARGIN_RATE 
			,NULL AS EIR 
			,NOMINAL AS FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT 
			,TUNGGAKAN_HARI AS DAY_PAST_DUE 
			,TUNGGAKAN_HARI AS DPD_CIF 
			,KUALITAS AS BI_COLLECTABILITY 
			,KUALITAS AS BI_COLLECT_CIF 
			,NULL AS STAFF_LOAN_FLAG 
			,NULL AS COLL_AMOUNT 
			,NULL AS UNAMORT_FEE_AMT 
			,NULL AS UNAMORT_COST_AMT 
			,NULL AS MARGIN_TYPE 
			,NULL AS DEFAULT_DATE 
			,TO_DATE(JANGKAWAKTU_MULAI , 'DD/MM/YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS LOAN_START_DATE 
			,TO_DATE(JANGKAWAKTU_JATUHTEMPO , 'DD/MM/YYYY HH24:MI:SS') AS LOAN_DUE_DATE 
			,DIVISIPISAH AS DIVISION_CODE 
			,CASE WHEN SIFATPEMBIAYAAN IN ('1', '5') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END RESTRUCTURE_FLAG
			,TUNGGAKAN_POKOK AS OUTSTANDING_PAST_DUE
			,TUNGGAKAN_IMBALAN AS MARGIN_PAST_DUE
		FROM 
		IMPORT_MULTIJASA_DEC pmam 
		LEFT JOIN
		IFRS_MASTER_ID IMI
		ON
		'MULTIJASA'||TRIM(NOMORREKENING) = IMI.MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE;

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.SP_shu_check
AS 
BEGIN
	
/*
/*
 * 
 * 
CREATE TABLE IFRS_FL_MODEL_RESULT AS 
WITH CTE AS (
SELECT DISTINCT  "workflow_header_draft_pkid" MODEL_ID, "PdName" PD_NAME
FROM "NTT_RISK_MODELLING"."VW_MODEL_COEFFICIENT"@DBCONFIGLINK A)
SELECT A."workflow_header_draft_pkid" MODEL_ID, 
	A."model_seq" MODEL_SEQ,
	C.PKID AS PD_RULE_ID,
	A."avg_pdrate_mape" AVG_MAPE,
	A."pdrate_mape" MAPE,
	A."adj_r_squared" ADJ_R 
FROM "NTT_RISK_MODELLING"."VW_MODEL_RESULT"@DBCONFIGLINK A 
	JOIN CTE B ON B.MODEL_ID = A."workflow_header_draft_pkid"
	JOIN  IFRS_PD_RULES_CONFIG  C ON B.PD_NAME = C.PD_RULE_NAME 
WHERE  "model_name" LIKE '%1003%' OR "model_name" LIKE '%SMOOTH%'

INSERT INTO IFRS_FL_MODEL_DATA (MODEL_ID, MODEL_SEQ, COEFF_NAME, COEFF_VAL, PD_RULE_ID)
SELECT  A."workflow_header_draft_pkid" MODEL_ID, A."model_seq" MODEL_SEQ,
"coeff_name", "estimate_val", b.PKID 
FROM "NTT_RISK_MODELLING"."VW_MODEL_COEFFICIENT"@DBCONFIGLINK A
	JOIN  IFRS_PD_RULES_CONFIG  B ON A."PdName" = b.PD_RULE_NAME 
WHERE  "model_name" LIKE '%1003%' OR "model_name" LIKE '%SMOOTH%'
 
 SELECT *
 FROM IFRS_FL_MODEL_DATA  
 WHERE   IS_SELECTED = 1
-- PD_RULE_ID  IN (12, 10,8,7,13,5,71)
 --	AND MODEL_ID  = PD_RULE_ID 
 ORDER BY PD_RULE_ID  , MODEL_SEQ 
 
  
 
TRUNCATE TABLE IFRS_PD_NORMINV;
 
INSERT INTO IFRS_PD_NORMINV  (EFF_DATE, PD_RULE_ID, BUCKET_FROM, BUCKET_TO, NORMINV_MMULT)
 
WITH cte AS (
SELECT EFF_DATE , PD_RULE_ID ,BUCKET_FROM , BUCKET_TO , MMULT 
FROM IFRS_PD_MAA_MMULT  A 
	JOIN VW_IFRS_MAX_BUCKET B ON A.BUCKET_GROUP = B.BUCKET_GROUP
WHERE EFF_DATE  = '31 DEC 2025'
	AND FL_SEQ  = 0 
	AND BUCKET_FROM  <> B.MAX_BUCKET_ID AND BUCKET_TO  <> 1 
)  , cte2 AS (
SELECT A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.BUCKET_FROM, A.BUCKET_TO,  
	 (SUM(B.MMULT)) MMULT
FROM CTE A 
	JOIN CTE B ON A.PD_RULE_ID = B.PD_RULE_ID AND A.BUCKET_FROM = B.BUCKET_FROM 
WHERE A.BUCKET_TO <= B.BUCKET_TO 
GROUP BY  A.EFF_DATE,A.PD_RULE_ID, A.BUCKET_FROM, A.BUCKET_TO 
) 
SELECT A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.BUCKET_FROM, A.BUCKET_TO,  FN_NORMINV( MMULT  )
FROM cte2  a  
 

TRUNCATE TABLE IFRS_PD_NORMDIST;

 

INSERT INTO IFRS_PD_NORMDIST (EFF_DATE, PD_RULE_ID , MODEL_ID, MODEL_SEQ, scenario_no,seq, BUCKET_FROM, BUCKET_TO,NORMDIST_MMULT )

WITH 
cte2 as (

selecT a.pd_rule_id,a.model_id, a.model_seq,scenario_no , EXTRACT(YEAR FROM me_period) - 2026 seq, max(a.coeff_val )+ sum(b.coeff_val * c.me_val ) odr
from IFRS_FL_MODEL_DATA a 
	join IFRS_FL_MODEL_DATA b on a.model_id = b.model_id and a.model_seq = b.model_seq 
	join IFRS_MEV_FORECAST C ON B.COEFF_NAme = c.me_code 
where EXTRACT(MONTH FROM ME_PERIOD) = 12
	and a.coeff_name = 'const' and b.coeff_name <> 'const' 
	and nvl(a.is_selected,0) = 1 
 group by a.model_id, a.model_seq, EXTRACT(YEAR FROM me_period) - 2026, scenario_no, a.pd_rule_id
),
CTE AS (
SELECT a.EFF_DATE , a.PD_RULE_ID , b.MODEL_ID, b.MODEL_SEQ  ,b.scenario_no,b.seq,
	a.BUCKET_FROM , a.BUCKET_TO ,FN_NORMDIST(a.NORMINV_MMULT +  b.odr)  NORMDIST_MMULT
FROM IFRS_PD_NORMINV A 
	join cte2 b on a.pd_rule_id = b.pd_rule_id
), CTE3 AS (
SELECT A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ,a.scenario_no, a.seq, A.BUCKET_FROM, A.BUCKET_TO ,  A.NORMDIST_MMULT, 
	LEAD( A.NORMDIST_MMULT,1,0) OVER (PARTITION BY A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ,a.scenario_no, a.seq, A.BUCKET_FROM 
		ORDER BY A.BUCKET_TO) LEADNORM
FROM CTE  A) , 
CTE4 AS (
SELECT A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ,a.scenario_no, a.seq, A.BUCKET_FROM, A.BUCKET_TO ,  
MAX(A.NORMDIST_MMULT) - SUM(NVL(B.NORMDIST_MMULT,0) - NVL(B.LEADNORM,0) )
FROM CTE3  A 
 LEFT JOIN CTE3 B ON A.EFF_DATE = B.EFF_DATE AND A.PD_RULE_ID = B.PD_RULE_ID
		AND A.MODEL_ID = B.MODEL_ID AND A.MODEL_SEQ = B.MODEL_SEQ 
		AND A.BUCKET_FROM = B.BUCKET_FROM 
		AND A.scenario_no = B.scenario_no
		AND A.SEQ = B.SEQ
		AND A.BUCKET_TO < B.BUCKET_TO 
GROUP BY A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ, A.BUCKET_FROM, A.BUCKET_TO , a.scenario_no, a.seq
) 
SELECT * FROM CTE4 A 
 
-- PD NORMDIST BUCKET TO 1 

INSERT INTO IFRS_PD_NORMDIST
SELECT  A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ,SCENARIO_NO,SEQ, A.BUCKET_FROM, 1  ,  1- SUM(A.NORMDIST_MMULT) 
FROM IFRS_PD_NORMDIST A 
GROUP BY A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ, A.BUCKET_FROM, SCENARIO_NO,SEQ


-- PD NORMDIST BUCKET DEFAULT 


INSERT INTO IFRS_PD_NORMDIST
SELECT DISTINCT  A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ, SCENARIO_NO,SEQ, 2, 1  ,0 
FROM IFRS_PD_NORMDIST A 
WHERE PD_RULE_ID IN (8,71)
UNION ALL 
SELECT DISTINCT  A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ, SCENARIO_NO,SEQ,2, 2  ,1
FROM IFRS_PD_NORMDIST A 
WHERE PD_RULE_ID IN (8,71)
UNION ALL 
SELECT DISTINCT   A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ, SCENARIO_NO,SEQ,5, 1  ,0 
FROM IFRS_PD_NORMDIST A 
WHERE PD_RULE_ID NOT IN (8,71)
UNION ALL 
SELECT DISTINCT  A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ, SCENARIO_NO,SEQ,5, 2  ,0 
FROM IFRS_PD_NORMDIST A 
WHERE PD_RULE_ID NOT IN (8,71)
UNION ALL 
SELECT DISTINCT  A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ, SCENARIO_NO,SEQ,5, 3  ,0 
FROM IFRS_PD_NORMDIST A 
WHERE PD_RULE_ID NOT IN (8,71)
UNION ALL 
SELECT DISTINCT  A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ,SCENARIO_NO,SEQ, 5, 4  ,0 
FROM IFRS_PD_NORMDIST A 
WHERE PD_RULE_ID NOT IN (8,71)
UNION ALL 
SELECT DISTINCT  A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ, SCENARIO_NO,SEQ,5, 5  ,1 
FROM IFRS_PD_NORMDIST A 
WHERE PD_RULE_ID NOT IN (8,71)
  ORDER BY PD_RULE_ID
   

-- CPD   
  
TRUNCATE TABLE IFRS_PD_MMULT_FL ;

INSERT INTO IFRS_PD_MMULT_FL (EFF_DATE, PD_RULE_ID, MODEL_ID, MODEL_SEQ, SCENARIO_NO,SEQ, BUCKET_FROM, BUCKET_TO,MMULT)
	SELECT EFF_DATE, PD_RULE_ID, MODEL_ID, MODEL_SEQ, SCENARIO_NO,SEQ,BUCKET_FROM, BUCKET_TO,NORMDIST_MMULT 
	FROM IFRS_PD_NORMDIST 
	WHERE SEQ = 0 ; 


DECLARE V_SEQ NUMBER ; 
 
BEGIN  
	
	V_SEQ := 0 ;

	WHILE V_SEQ < 30 
	LOOP 
		INSERT INTO IFRS_PD_MMULT_FL (EFF_DATE, PD_RULE_ID, MODEL_ID, MODEL_SEQ, SCENARIO_NO,SEQ, BUCKET_FROM, BUCKET_TO,MMULT)
		SELECT A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ,A.SCENARIO_NO, V_SEQ + 1,  A.BUCKET_FROM , B.BUCKET_TO ,  SUM(A.MMULT * B.NORMDIST_MMULT ) 
		FROM IFRS_PD_MMULT_FL A 
			JOIN IFRS_PD_NORMDIST B ON A.EFF_DATE = B.EFF_DATE AND A.PD_RULE_ID = B.PD_RULE_ID 
				AND A.MODEL_ID = B.MODEL_ID 
				AND A.MODEL_SEQ = B.MODEL_SEQ 
				AND B.BUCKET_FROM = A.BUCKET_TO  
				AND A.SCENARIO_NO = B.SCENARIO_NO
		WHERE A.SEQ = V_SEQ
			AND B.SEQ =    V_SEQ +1 
		GROUP BY A.EFF_DATE, A.PD_RULE_ID, A.MODEL_ID, A.MODEL_SEQ, a.BUCKET_FROM, b.BUCKET_TO ,1 ,A.SCENARIO_NO ; 
		
	      V_SEQ := V_SEQ + 1;

		
	END LOOP;	
END ;  



-- MPD 

TRUNCATE TABLE IFRS_PD_MMULT_FL_MPD

INSERT INTO IFRS_PD_MMULT_FL_MPD (EFF_DATE, PD_RULE_ID, MODEL_ID, MODEL_SEQ,scenario_no,seq , BUCKET_FROM, BUCKET_TO, MPD)
SELECT EFF_DATE, PD_RULE_ID, MODEL_ID, MODEL_SEQ,scenario_no, seq ,BUCKET_FROM, BUCKET_TO, 
	MMULT - LAG(MMULT,1,0) OVER (PARTITION BY EFF_DATE, PD_RULE_ID, MODEL_ID, MODEL_SEQ, BUCKET_FROM, scenario_no  ORDER BY SEQ ) MPD  
FROM IFRS_PD_MMULT_FL
WHERE BUCKET_TO = CASE WHEN PD_RULE_ID IN (8,71) THEN 2 ELSE 5 END 
ORDER BY PD_RULE_ID, BUCKET_FROM , SEQ 


 -- PD TERM STRUCTURE PER SKENARIO

 
 TRUNCATE TABLE IFRS_PD_TERM_FL
 
INSERT INTO IFRS_PD_TERM_FL (EFF_DATE, PD_RULE_ID, MODEL_ID, MODEL_SEQ, SCENARIO_NO, SEQ, BUCKET_FROM, BUCKET_TO,FL_YEAR,FL_MONTH, PD)
WITH CTE (MON) AS (
SELECT 1 AS MON FROM DUAL 
UNION ALL 
SELECT MON+1  
FROM CTE 
WHERE MON < 12 
) 
SELECT EFF_DATE, PD_RULE_ID, MODEL_ID, MODEL_SEQ,  SCENARIO_NO, 
	((SEQ * 12) + (MON  -1)) SEQ,
	BUCKET_FROM, BUCKET_TO,SEQ + 1 FL_YEAR,MON , 
	1- POWER(1 - MPD, (MON/ 12)) - CASE WHEN MON = 1 THEN 0 ELSE 1- POWER(1 - MPD, ((MON-1) / 12)) END
FROM IFRS_PD_MMULT_FL_MPD A 
	JOIN CTE B ON 1=1 
	  ;
	 
	 TRUNCATE TABLE IFRS_PD_TERM_FL_WEIGHT

INSERT INTO IFRS_PD_TERM_FL_WEIGHT  (EFF_DATE, PD_RULE_ID, MODEL_ID, MODEL_SEQ, SEQ, BUCKET_FROM, BUCKET_TO,FL_YEAR,FL_MONTH, PD)
SELECT EFF_DATE, PD_RULE_ID, MODEL_ID, MODEL_SEQ,   SEQ, 
	BUCKET_FROM, BUCKET_TO,FL_YEAR,FL_MONTH, SUM(CASE WHEN SCENARIO_NO = 2 THEN 0.5 ELSE 0.25 END * PD ) PD 
FROM IFRS_PD_TERM_FL A 
GROUP BY EFF_DATE, PD_RULE_ID, MODEL_ID, MODEL_SEQ, SEQ, BUCKET_FROM, BUCKET_TO,FL_YEAR,FL_MONTH
 


INSERT INTO PSAK413.IFRS_PD_TERM_STRUCTURE (
     EFF_DATE,
    BASE_DATE,
    SCENARIO_NO,
    PD_RULE_ID,
    PD_RULE_NAME,
    MODEL_ID,
    BUCKET_GROUP,
    BUCKET_ID,
    FL_SEQ,
    FL_YEAR,
    FL_MONTH,
    PD,
    PD_OVERRIDE,
    PD_METHOD,
    CREATEDBY,
    CREATEDDATE,
    CREATEDHOST,
    UPDATEDBY,
    UPDATEDDATE,
    UPDATEDHOST
)  
SELECT EFF_DATE , LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(EFF_DATE , 12 * FL_YEAR)) BASE_DATE , 0 AS SCENARIO_NO , PD_RULE_ID , '' ,
MODEL_ID , 'DPD_5_2' , BUCKET_FROM , SEQ, FL_YEAR, FL_MONTH, PD, PD, 'MAA', 'MIGRASI', SYSDATE, 'LOCALHOST', NULL, NULL, NULL   
FROM IFRS_PD_TERM_FL_WEIGHT


 
	WITH CTE AS (
	SELECT PD_RULE_ID ,SUM(MMULT)  PD,
		MAX(CASE WHEN BUCKET_FROM = 1 THEN MMULT ELSE 0 END) B1,
		MAX(CASE WHEN BUCKET_FROM = 2 THEN MMULT ELSE 0 END) B2,
		MAX(CASE WHEN BUCKET_FROM = 3 THEN MMULT ELSE 0 END) B3,
		MAX(CASE WHEN BUCKET_FROM = 4 THEN MMULT ELSE 0 END) B4,
		MAX(CASE WHEN BUCKET_FROM = 5 THEN MMULT ELSE 0 END) B5
	FROM IFRS_PD_MAA_MMULT
	WHERE EFF_DATE  = '31 DEC 2025'
		AND BUCKET_TO  = CASE WHEN PD_RULE_ID  NOT IN (8,71) THEN 5 ELSE 2 END
		AND FL_SEQ  = 0 
		GROUP BY PD_RULE_ID 
	),CTE2 AS (
	 SELECt PD_RULE_ID , MODEL_ID , MODEL_SEQ  , BUCKET_FROM ,
	 	SUM(CASE WHEN SCENARIO_NO = 2 THEN 0.5 ELSE 0.25 END * MPD)   AFL
	 FROM IFRS_PD_MMULT_FL_MPD
	 WHERE SEQ = 0  
	 GROUP BY  PD_RULE_ID , MODEL_ID , MODEL_SEQ , BUCKET_FROM  ),
	 CTE3 AS (
	 SELECt PD_RULE_ID , MODEL_ID , MODEL_SEQ ,
	 	SUM(AFL)  AFL,
	 	MAX(CASE WHEN BUCKET_FROM = 1 THEN AFL ELSE 0 END) AFL1,
		MAX(CASE WHEN BUCKET_FROM = 2 THEN AFL ELSE 0 END) AFL2,
		MAX(CASE WHEN BUCKET_FROM = 3 THEN AFL ELSE 0 END) AFL3,
		MAX(CASE WHEN BUCKET_FROM = 4 THEN AFL ELSE 0 END) AFL4,
		MAX(CASE WHEN BUCKET_FROM = 5 THEN AFL ELSE 0 END) AFL5
	 FROM CTE2 
	 GROUP BY  PD_RULE_ID , MODEL_ID , MODEL_SEQ  
	 
	 ),
	 cte4 AS (
	  SELECT MODEL_ID, model_seq,
       LISTAGG(COEFF_NAME , '+') WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY COEFF_NAME ) AS FORMULA
FROM IFRS_FL_MODEL_DATA
WHERE COEFF_NAME  <> 'const'
GROUP BY model_seq,MODEL_ID 
	 )
	 
	 SELECT B.PD_RULE_ID, d.PD_RULE_NAME  ,B.MODEL_SEQ,c.formula, B.AFL / A.PD AS FL_IMPACT , B1,AFL1, B2,AFL2, B3,AFL3,B4,AFL4,B5,AFL5 
	 FROM CTE A JOIN CTE3 B ON A.PD_RULE_ID = B.PD_RULE_ID 
	 	JOIN cte4 c ON b.model_id = c.model_id AND    b.model_seq = c.model_seq
	 	JOIN ifrs_pd_rules_config d ON a.pd_rule_id = d.PKID 
	 	 --WHERE b.pd_rule_id = 4 --  AND b.model_seq = 999
	 ORDER BY A.PD_RULE_ID, b.MODEL_ID, b.MODEL_SEQ 
	  


 
 
 
	 
*/	 
	INSERT INTO X_IMA_NONPAYM (masterid)
	SELECT 1 FROM dual  ; 
	
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.sp_testing_oracle (
    p_runid         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    p_download_date IN DATE     DEFAULT NULL,
    p_prc           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S',
    p_model_id      IN NUMBER   DEFAULT 0
)
IS
BEGIN
    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('Stored Procedure testing berhasil dijalankan!');
    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('p_runid         = ' || p_runid);
    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('p_download_date = ' || p_download_date);
    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('p_prc           = ' || p_prc);
    DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('p_model_id      = ' || p_model_id);
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.XSP_IFRS_EAD_RESULT2 (
    P_RUNID         IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S_00000_0000',
    P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IN DATE,
    P_SYSCODE       IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT '0',
    P_PRC           IN VARCHAR2 DEFAULT 'S'
)
AS 
    V_CURRDATE       DATE;
    V_DATADATE       VARCHAR2(20);
    V_TABLE_NAME     VARCHAR2(50);
    V_COUNT          NUMBER;
	V_MODEL_ID       NUMBER;

-- DYNAMIC NAMES / QUERY
    V_STR_QUERY      CLOB;

    -- TABLE NAMES
    V_TAB_OWNER     CONSTANT 		VARCHAR2(30) := 'PSAK413';
    V_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_ALL 			VARCHAR2(100);
    V_IFRS_EIL_IMA					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_TABLEPDCONFIG					VARCHAR2(100);
    V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT				VARCHAR2(100);

    -- LOG / RESULT
    V_TABLEDEST     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_COLUMNDEST    VARCHAR2(100);
    V_SP_NAME       VARCHAR2(100) := 'SP_IFRS_EAD_RESULT';
    V_OPERATION     VARCHAR2(100);
    V_QUERYS        VARCHAR2(8000);
    V_RETURNROWS2   NUMBER;
    
    V_STR_SQL        CLOB;
    V_STR_SQL_RULE   CLOB;
    V_RULE_ID        VARCHAR2(250);
    V_ID             NUMBER := 0;
    V_MAX_ID         NUMBER := 0;
    V_SEQUENCE       VARCHAR2(50);
    
BEGIN
	-- HANDLE DEFAULT DOWNLOAD DATE
    IF P_DOWNLOAD_DATE IS NULL THEN
        SELECT CURRDATE INTO V_CURRDATE FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;
    ELSE
        V_CURRDATE := P_DOWNLOAD_DATE;
    END IF;

    V_MODEL_ID := 0;

    -- CHOOSE TABLE NAMES BASED ON MODE
    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN 
        V_IFRS_EIL_IMA  		:= 'IFRS_EIL_IMA_' || P_RUNID;
        V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT		:= 'IFRS_EAD_RESULT_' || P_RUNID; 
    ELSE 
        V_IFRS_EIL_IMA  		:= 'IFRS_EIL_IMA'; 
    	V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT		:= 'IFRS_EAD_RESULT';
    END IF;

    BEGIN
        SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_SP_NAME, P_RUNID, 0, SYSTIMESTAMP);
    EXCEPTION
        WHEN OTHERS THEN
            DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('WARNING: SP_IFRS_RUNNING_LOG FAILED: ' || SQLERRM);
    END;
    COMMIT;

    IF P_PRC = 'S' THEN
        
        -- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS (OWNED BY CURRENT SCHEMA)
        SELECT COUNT(*) INTO V_COUNT
        FROM USER_TABLES
        WHERE TABLE_NAME = UPPER(V_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_ALL);

        IF V_COUNT > 0 THEN
            V_STR_QUERY := 'DROP TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_ALL;
            EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        END IF;

        V_STR_QUERY := 'CREATE TABLE ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_ALL || ' AS SELECT * FROM IFRS_EAD_RESULT WHERE 1=0';
        EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
        
    ELSE
    	    
	   	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'DELETE FROM ' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT || ' WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = DATE ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' ' ;
   
    END IF;
   
    EXECUTE IMMEDIATE 'TRUNCATE TABLE GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD' ; 
    COMMIT;
   
    V_STR_QUERY := '
	INSERT INTO GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD (DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, PMTDATE, SEQ, PRINCIPAL, SUM_PRINCIPAL)
		WITH CTE_INIT AS ( ' ||
		'	SELECT MAX(DOWNLOAD_DATE) AS DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID ' ||
		'	FROM IFRS_INITIAL_PAYM_SCHD ' ||
		'	WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE <= ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''' 
			GROUP BY MASTERID ' ||
		'), 
		CTE AS ( ' ||
		'SELECT A.DOWNLOAD_DATE , A.MASTERID ,A.PMTDATE ,MONTHS_BETWEEN(LAST_DAY(A.PMTDATE),A.DOWNLOAD_DATE) AS SEQ ,A.PRINCIPAL , ' ||
		'	SUM(A.PRINCIPAL) OVER (PARTITION BY A.MASTERID, A.DOWNLOAD_DATE ORDER BY A.PMTDATE) SUM_PRINCIPAL ' ||
		'	FROM IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_ALL A ' ||
		'	WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE  <= ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || '''
				AND PMTDATE > ''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || '''
				AND EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM CTE_INIT X WHERE X.DOWNLOAD_DATE = A.DOWNLOAD_DATE AND X.MASTERID = A.MASTERID)
			GROUP BY A.DOWNLOAD_DATE , A.MASTERID ,A.PMTDATE ,MONTHS_BETWEEN(LAST_DAY(A.PMTDATE),A.DOWNLOAD_DATE) ,A.PRINCIPAL
		SELECT DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, PMTDATE,SEQ, PRINCIPAL, SUM_PRINCIPAL
		FROM CTE ';
				
	EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
	COMMIT;

	V_STR_QUERY := 'INSERT INTO IFRS_EAD_RESULT(DOWNLOAD_DATE, MASTERID, GROUP_SEGMENT, SEGMENT, SUB_SEGMENT, RATING_CODE, DAY_PAST_DUE, BI_COLLECTABILITY,
					 ACCOUNT_NUMBER, ACCOUNT_STATUS, CUSTOMER_NUMBER, CUSTOMER_NAME, EXCHANGE_RATE, IMPAIRED_FLAG, OUTSTANDING, BUCKET_ID, REVOLVING_FLAG, 
					 PRODUCT_CODE, PRODUCT_TYPE, PLAFOND, LOAN_START_DATE, DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, EIR, LOAN_DUE_DATE, MARGIN_PAST_DUE, SEGMENTATION_ID,
					 LT_RULE_ID, CUSTOMER_GRADE, PRODUCT_ENTITY, DATA_SOURCE, PRODUCT_GROUP, IS_IMPAIRED, IFRS9_CLASS, PD_SEGMENT, LGD_SEGMENT, EAD_SEGMENT, BUCKET_GROUP,
					 LIFETIME, STAGE, UNAMORT_COST_AMT, UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, MARGIN_ACCRUED, FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, EAD_BALANCE, EAD_MARGIN, EIL_MODEL_ID, EAD_RULE_ID, LGD_RULE_ID,
					 LGD_ME_MODEL_ID, PD_RULE_ID, PD_ME_MODEL_ID, CURRENCY, EIL_AMOUNT, FLAG_VAS, UNUSED_AMOUNT, EAD_TYPE, SEQ, EAD_PRINCIPAL, CREATEDBY, CREATEDDATE)
					WITH CTE_SEQ AS (
					SELECT 1 SEQ , 600 MAX_SEQ FROM DUAL 
					UNION ALL 
					SELECT SEQ+1, MAX_SEQ 
					FROM CTE 
					WHERE SEQ+1 < MAX_SEQ
					),
					
					SELECT B.DOWNLOAD_DATE, B.MASTERID, B.GROUP_SEGMENT, B.SEGMENT, B.SUB_SEGMENT, B.RATING_CODE, B.DAY_PAST_DUE, B.BI_COLLECTABILITY, B.ACCOUNT_NUMBER,
					 B.ACCOUNT_STATUS, B.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, B.CUSTOMER_NAME, B.EXCHANGE_RATE, B.IMPAIRED_FLAG, B.OUTSTANDING, B.BUCKET_ID, B.REVOLVING_FLAG, B.PRODUCT_CODE,
					 B.PRODUCT_TYPE, B.PLAFOND, B.LOAN_START_DATE, B.DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, B.RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, B.EIR, B.LOAN_DUE_DATE, B.MARGIN_PAST_DUE, B.SEGMENTATION_ID,
					 B.LT_RULE_ID, B.CUSTOMER_GRADE, B.PRODUCT_ENTITY, B.DATA_SOURCE, B.PRODUCT_GROUP, B.IS_IMPAIRED, B.IFRS9_CLASS, B.PD_SEGMENT, B.LGD_SEGMENT,
					 B.EAD_SEGMENT, B.BUCKET_GROUP, B.LIFETIME, B.STAGE, B.UNAMORT_COST_AMT, B.UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, B.MARGIN_ACCRUED, B.FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, B.EAD_BALANCE,
					 B.EAD_MARGIN, B.EIL_MODEL_ID, B.EAD_RULE_ID, B.LGD_RULE_ID, B.LGD_ME_MODEL_ID, B.PD_RULE_ID, B.PD_ME_MODEL_ID, B.CURRENCY, B.EIL_AMOUNT,
					 B.FLAG_VAS, B.UNUSED_AMOUNT, B.EAD_TYPE,0 SEQ, B.EAD_PRINCIPAL, ''SP_IFRS_EAD_RESULT'' AS CREATEDBY, SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE
					FROM IFRS_EIL_IMA B 
					UNION ALL 
					SELECT B.DOWNLOAD_DATE, B.MASTERID, B.GROUP_SEGMENT, B.SEGMENT, B.SUB_SEGMENT, B.RATING_CODE, B.DAY_PAST_DUE, B.BI_COLLECTABILITY, B.ACCOUNT_NUMBER,
					 B.ACCOUNT_STATUS, B.CUSTOMER_NUMBER, B.CUSTOMER_NAME, B.EXCHANGE_RATE, B.IMPAIRED_FLAG, B.OUTSTANDING, B.BUCKET_ID, B.REVOLVING_FLAG, B.PRODUCT_CODE,
					 B.PRODUCT_TYPE, B.PLAFOND, B.LOAN_START_DATE, B.DAY_PAST_DUE_CIF, B.RESTRUCTURE_FLAG, B.EIR, B.LOAN_DUE_DATE, B.MARGIN_PAST_DUE, B.SEGMENTATION_ID,
					 B.LT_RULE_ID, B.CUSTOMER_GRADE, B.PRODUCT_ENTITY, B.DATA_SOURCE, B.PRODUCT_GROUP, B.IS_IMPAIRED, B.IFRS9_CLASS, B.PD_SEGMENT, B.LGD_SEGMENT,
					 B.EAD_SEGMENT, B.BUCKET_GROUP, B.LIFETIME, B.STAGE, B.UNAMORT_COST_AMT, B.UNAMORT_FEE_AMT, B.MARGIN_ACCRUED, B.FAIR_VALUE_AMOUNT, B.EAD_BALANCE,
					 A.EAD_MARGIN, B.EIL_MODEL_ID, B.EAD_RULE_ID, B.LGD_RULE_ID, B.LGD_ME_MODEL_ID, B.PD_RULE_ID, B.PD_ME_MODEL_ID, B.CURRENCY, B.EIL_AMOUNT,
					 B.FLAG_VAS, B.UNUSED_AMOUNT, B.EAD_TYPE, A.SEQ, A.EAD_PRINCIPAL, ''SP_IFRS_EAD_RESULT'' AS CREATEDBY, SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE
					FROM IFRS_EIL_IMA A 
					INNER JOIN CTE_SEQ C ON A.LIFETIME >= C.SEQ
					LEFT  JOIN GTMP_IFRS_PAYM_SCHD_EAD B ON A.MASTERID = B.MASTERID  AND B.SEQ = C.SEQ
					WHERE  ((C.SEQ <= 12 AND A.STAGE = 1 ) OR A.STAGE = 2 )';
					
		EXECUTE IMMEDIATE V_STR_QUERY;
		COMMIT;
        -----------------------------
	    -- Log & insert final data
	    -----------------------------
    V_TABLEDEST := V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT;
    V_COLUMNDEST := '-';
    V_OPERATION := 'INSERT';
 
    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_EXEC_AND_LOG(V_CURRDATE, V_TABLEDEST, V_COLUMNDEST, V_SP_NAME, V_OPERATION, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;  
   
    V_QUERYS := 'SELECT * FROM ' || V_TAB_OWNER || '.' || V_IFRS_EAD_RESULT ||
                ' WHERE EFF_DATE = TO_DATE(''' || TO_CHAR(V_CURRDATE,'YYYY-MM-DD') || ''',''YYYY-MM-DD'')' ;

    PSAK413.SP_IFRS_RESULT_PREV(V_CURRDATE, V_QUERYS, V_SP_NAME, NVL(V_RETURNROWS2,0), P_RUNID);
    COMMIT;

EXCEPTION
    WHEN OTHERS THEN
        -- ROLLBACK TO SAFE STATE AND RE-RAISE
        ROLLBACK;
        DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('ERROR IN SP_IFRS_PD_RULE_DATA: ' || SQLERRM);
        RAISE;
END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.X_IFRS_POPULATE_IMAM_FROM_PMAM
AS
   V_CURRDATE  DATE;
   V_PREVDATE  DATE; 
BEGIN

SELECT CURRDATE, PREVDATE INTO V_CURRDATE, V_PREVDATE
FROM IFRS_PRC_DATE;

DELETE FROM IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
WHERE DOWNLOAD_DATE = V_CURRDATE;

INSERT INTO IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
(
	 DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,MASTERID
	,MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE
	,DATA_SOURCE
	,GLOBAL_CUSTOMER_NUMBER
	,CUSTOMER_NUMBER
	,CUSTOMER_NAME
	,FACILITY_NUMBER
	,ACCOUNT_NUMBER
	,PREVIOUS_ACCOUNT_NUMBER
	,ACCOUNT_STATUS
	,MARGIN_RATE
	,MARKET_RATE
	,PRODUCT_GROUP
	,PRODUCT_TYPE
	,PRODUCT_CODE
	,PRODUCT_ENTITY
	,GL_CONSTNAME
	,BRANCH_CODE
	,BRANCH_CODE_OPEN
	,CURRENCY
	,EXCHANGE_RATE
	,OUTSTANDING
	,OUTSTANDING_PASTDUE
	,PLAFOND
	,MARGIN_ACCRUED
	,LOAN_START_DATE
	,LOAN_DUE_DATE
	,TENOR
	,PAYMENT_CODE
	,PAYMENT_TERM
	,MARGIN_CALCULATION_CODE
	,MARGIN_PAYMENT_Term
	,RESTRUCTURE_DATE
	,RESTRUCTURE_FLAG
	,ORIGINAL_COLLECTABILITY
	,BI_COLLECTABILITY
	,DAY_PAST_DUE
	,GROUP_SEGMENT
	,SEGMENT
	,SUB_SEGMENT
	,STAGE
	,UNAMORT_COST_AMT
	,UNAMORT_FEE_AMT
	,CREATEDDATE
	,CREATEDBY
	,STAFF_LOAN_FLAG
)
SELECT
	 A.DOWNLOAD_DATE
	,A.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID AS MASTERID
	,A.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID AS MASTER_ACCOUNT_CODE
	,A.DATA_SOURCE
	,NULL GLOBAL_CUSTOMER_NUMBER
	,A.CUSTOMER_NUMBER
	,A.CUSTOMER_NAME
	,NULL FACILITY_NUMBER
	,A.ACCOUNT_NUMBER
	,NULL PREVIOUS_ACCOUNT_NUMBER
	,A.ACCOUNT_STATUS
	,A.INTEREST_RATE AS MARGIN_RATE
	,NULL MARKET_RATE
	,A.PRODUCT_GROUP
	,A.PRODUCT_TYPE
	,A.PRODUCT_CODE
	,NULL AS PRODUCT_ENTITY
	,NULL AS GL_CONSTNAME
	,A.BRANCH_CODE
	,NULL AS BRANCH_CODE_OPEN
	,A.CURRENCY
	,A.EXCHANGE_RATE
	,A.OUTSTANDING
	,NULL AS OUTSTANDING_PASTDUE
	,A.PLAFOND
	,NULL AS MARGIN_ACCRUED
	,B.LOAN_START_DATE AS LOAN_START_DATE
	,B.LOAN_DUE_DATE AS LOAN_DUE_DATE
	,NULL AS TENOR
	,NULL AS PAYMENT_CODE
	,NULL AS PAYMENT_TERM
	,NULL AS MARGIN_CALCULATION_CODE
	,NULL AS MARGIN_PAYMENT_TERM
	,NULL AS RESTRUCTURE_DATE
	,NULL AS RESTRUCTURE_FLAG
	,A.BI_COLLECTABILITY AS ORIGINAL_COLLECTABILITY
	,A.BI_COLLECTABILITY
	,A.DAY_PAST_DUE
	,NULL AS GROUP_SEGMENT
	,A.SEGMENT
	,NULL AS SUB_SEGMENT
	,NULL AS STAGE
	,A.UNAMOR_TRANS_COST_AMT AS UNAMORT_COST_AMT
	,A.UNAMOR_ORIGINATION_FEE_AMT AS UNAMORT_FEE_AMT
	,SYSDATE AS CREATEDDATE
	,'DUMMY' AS CREATEDBY
	,CASE WHEN NVL(A.STAFF_LOAN_FLAG,'N') = 'N' THEN 0 ELSE 1 END
FROM PSAK_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY A
LEFT JOIN
TABLENYA_ADAM B
ON
A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = 
TO_DATE
(
	TO_CHAR
	(
         TO_TIMESTAMP(B.DOWNLOAD_DATE, 'YYYY-MM-DD HH24:MI:SS.FF'),'YYYY-MM-DD'
    ), 'YYYY-MM-DD'
)
AND
A.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID = B.MASTER_ACCOUNT_ID
WHERE 
A.DOWNLOAD_DATE = V_CURRDATE;



END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413.X_SP_IFRS_PATCH_SEGMENT
AS
	dtcurr DATE;
	dtprev DATE;
BEGIN

	 dtcurr := '31-DEC-2025';
	 
	WHILE  dtcurr >= '31-JAN-2020' -- '31-DEC-2025'
	LOOP 
		dtprev := ADD_MONTHS(dtcurr, -1);

				--KORPORASI--
				UPDATE VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
				SET 
					SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'KORPORASI_PIUTANG'
								WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'KORPORASI_PIUTANG'	
								WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_PIUTANG'
							END, 
					
					SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'KORPORASI_MURABAHAH'
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'KORPORASI_QARDH'	
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_RAHN'
								END,
								
					GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'KORPORASI'
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'KORPORASI'	
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS'
								END
				WHERE 
					PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'KORPORASI'
				AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr;
				
				--COMMERCIAL--
				UPDATE VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
				SET 
					SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'KOMERSIAL_PIUTANG'
								WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'KOMERSIAL_PIUTANG'	
								WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_PIUTANG'
							END, 
					
					SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'KOMERSIAL_MURABAHAH'
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'KOMERSIAL_QARDH'	
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_RAHN'
								END,
								
					GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'KOMERSIAL'
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'KOMERSIAL'	
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS'
								END
				WHERE 
					PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'COMMERCIAL'
				AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr;
				
				--BISNIS BANKING/SMALL--
				UPDATE VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
				SET 
					SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'SME_PIUTANG'
								WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'SME_PIUTANG'	
								WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_PIUTANG'
							END, 
					
					SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'SME_MURABAHAH'
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'SME_QARDH'	
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_RAHN'
								END,
								
					GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'SME'
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'SME'	
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS'
								END
				WHERE 
					PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'BISNIS BANKING/SMALL'
				AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr;
				
				--PENSIUN & PRA PENSIUN--
				UPDATE VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
				SET 
					SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_PIUTANG'
								WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_PIUTANG'	
								WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_PIUTANG'
								WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHS0001') THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_PIUTANG'
							END, 
					
					SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_PIUTANG_MURABAHAH'
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_PIUTANG_QARDH'	
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_RAHN'
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHS0001') THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_RAHN'
								END,
								
					GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'PENSIUN & PRA PENSIUN'
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'PENSIUN & PRA PENSIUN'	
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS'
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHS0001')	THEN 'PENSIUN & PRA PENSIUN'
								END
				WHERE 
					PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'PENSIUN & PRA PENSIUN'
				AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr;
				
				--BACK TO BACK & MURABAHAH EMAS--
				UPDATE VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
				SET 
					SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS_PIUTANG'
								WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS_PIUTANG'	
								WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' 			THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_PIUTANG'
							END, 
					
					SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 	THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS_MURABAHAH'
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   	THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS_QARDH'	
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' 		THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_RAHN'
								END,
								
					GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS'
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS'	
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' 			THEN 'GADAI_EMAS'
								END
				WHERE 
					PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'BACK TO BACK & MURABAHAH EMAS'
				AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr;
				
				--KUR--
				UPDATE VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
				SET 
					SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'KUR_PIUTANG' END, 
					SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 	THEN 'KUR_MURABAHAH' END,
					GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' THEN 'KUR' END
				WHERE 
					PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'KUR'
				AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr;
				
				--NON KUR--
				UPDATE VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
				SET 
					SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'NON_KUR_PIUTANG' END, 
					SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 	THEN 'NON_KUR_MURABAHAH' END,
					GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' THEN 'NON_KUR' END
				WHERE 
					PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'NON KUR'
				AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr;
				
				--IMPLAN--
				UPDATE VW_IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY
				SET 
					SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'MULTIGUNA_PIUTANG' END, 
					SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 	THEN 'MULTIGUNA_MURABAHAH' END,
					GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' THEN 'MULTIGUNA' END
				WHERE 
					PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'IMPLAN'
				AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr;
				
				dbms_output.put_line(dtcurr||'|'||dtprev);
				dtcurr := last_day(TO_DATE(dtcurr)-1-TO_NUMBER(TO_CHAR(TO_DATE(dtcurr),'DD')));

			COMMIT;
			
	END LOOP;

END;

									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_PIUTANG_QARDH'	
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_RAHN'
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHS0001') THEN 'PENSIUN&PRAPENSIUN_RAHN'
								END,
								
					GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'PENSIUN & PRA PENSIUN'
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'PENSIUN & PRA PENSIUN'	
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHN0001','RHN0002','RHN0004','RHN0005','RHN0007','RHN0008')	THEN 'GADAI_EMAS'
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' AND PRODUCT_CODE IN ('RHS0001')	THEN 'PENSIUN & PRA PENSIUN'
								END
				WHERE 
					PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'PENSIUN & PRA PENSIUN'
				AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr;
				
				--BACK TO BACK & MURABAHAH EMAS--
				UPDATE IFRS_IMAM_ADAM_TEST
				SET 
					SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS_PIUTANG'
								WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS_PIUTANG'	
								WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' 			THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_PIUTANG'
							END, 
					
					SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 	THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS_MURABAHAH'
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   	THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS_QARDH'	
									WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' 		THEN 'GADAI_EMAS_RAHN'
								END,
								
					GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS'
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'QARDH'	   		THEN 'BTB_MRB_EMAS'	
										WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'RAHN' 			THEN 'GADAI_EMAS'
								END
				WHERE 
					PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'BACK TO BACK & MURABAHAH EMAS'
				AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr;
				
				--KUR--
				UPDATE IFRS_IMAM_ADAM_TEST
				SET 
					SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'KUR_PIUTANG' END, 
					SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 	THEN 'KUR_MURABAHAH' END,
					GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' THEN 'KUR' END
				WHERE 
					PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'KUR'
				AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr;
				
				--NON KUR--
				UPDATE IFRS_IMAM_ADAM_TEST
				SET 
					SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'NON_KUR_PIUTANG' END, 
					SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 	THEN 'NON_KUR_MURABAHAH' END,
					GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' THEN 'NON_KUR' END
				WHERE 
					PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'NON KUR'
				AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr;
				
				--IMPLAN--
				UPDATE IFRS_IMAM_ADAM_TEST
				SET 
					SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 		THEN 'MULTIGUNA_PIUTANG' END, 
					SUB_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' 	THEN 'MULTIGUNA_MURABAHAH' END,
					GROUP_SEGMENT = CASE WHEN PRODUCT_TYPE = 'MURABAHAH' THEN 'MULTIGUNA' END
				WHERE 
					PSAK55_SEGMENT = 'IMPLAN'
				AND DOWNLOAD_DATE = dtcurr;
				
				dbms_output.put_line(dtcurr||'|'||dtprev);
				dtcurr := last_day(TO_DATE(dtcurr)-1-TO_NUMBER(TO_CHAR(TO_DATE(dtcurr),'DD')));

			COMMIT;
			
	END LOOP;

END;

CREATE OR REPLACE PROCEDURE PSAK413."xSP_Patch_segment2" 
AS 
 
    
BEGIN
    
DECLARE
  v_start_date DATE := DATE '2020-01-31';  
  v_end_date   DATE := DATE '2025-12-31';  
 
BEGIN 

  WHILE v_start_date <= v_end_date LOOP
	  
	
UPDATE IFRS_MASTER_ACCOUNT_MONTHLY  a
SET (a.sub_segment, a.segment, a.group_segment) =
    (SELECT x.sub_segment, x.segment, x.group_segment
     FROM TMP_IMA_SEGMENT x
     WHERE a.masterid = x.masterid)
WHERE a.download_date = v_start_date
AND A.PRODUCT_TYPE  IN ('QARDH','RAHN','MURABAHAH')
AND A.ACCOUNT_STATUS  = 'A'
AND EXISTS (
SELECT 1 
FROM TMP_IMA_SEGMENT Y 
WHERE A.MASTERID  = Y.MASTERID
AND Y.SUB_SEGMENT IS NOT NULL 
AND (A.GROUP_SEGMENT <> Y.GROUP_SEGMENT OR A.SEGMENT <> Y.SEGMENT OR A.SUB_SEGMENT <> Y.SUB_SEGMENT)
);

COMMIT ; 
    -- tambah 1 bulan
DBMS_OUTPUT.PUT_LINE('Tanggal: ' || TO_CHAR(v_start_date, 'YYYY-MM-DD'));
    v_start_date := LAST_DAY(ADD_MONTHS(v_start_date, 1));
  END LOOP;
     
END;
